雅思词汇:1频词汇检测

hbaolong@vip.qq.com

1频词汇检测

abate [ə’beɪt]

释义 • v. (of wind, noise, pain, etc.) to make or become less 缓解，减弱，减轻

词根 • 已知 aloud中的 a-是对 loud的强调 ，因而 a-具有加强的意思 。a (加强 ) +bate(走 ，打 )→走下去 →减轻

例句 • The noise will have abated to a fairly large extent. (IELTS3,T4,L4)噪音将会在很大程度上减弱 。

abide [ə’baɪd]

释义 • v. to remain; to continue; to stay (古意)在某地停留

搭配 • abide by 遵守 ，信守

例句 • When children have had a major role in determining procedures, they are more likely to abide by and enforce them. (IELTS4,T3,R1)当孩子们在制定程序中发挥重要作用时 ，他们更有可能遵守并执行程序 。

abject [ˈæbdʒekt]

释义 • adj . (of something bad) experienced or present to the maximum degree卑鄙的，下贱的；（指境况）凄惨的；轻蔑的，被鄙视的；厚颜无耻的

词根 • ab-（away）+ject（投，掷）→被丢弃的→凄惨的

同义 • wretched, miserable, hopeless, pathetic, pitiful, lamentable, appalling

例句 • Rather than a case of abject failure, Rapu Nui is an unlikely story of success, they claim. (IELTS11, T2, R2) 他们说，复活节岛并不是一个可耻的失败案例，而是一个令人难以置信的成功故事。

abnormal [æb’nɔːməl]

释义 • adj. different, esp. in an undesirable way, from what is normal, ordinary or expected 反常的，异常的

词根 • ab(=away, off)+normal(正常 )→反常的 ，异常的

派生 • abnormally adv. 反常地

abnormality n. 异常

例句 • These regions are fragile (i.e. highly vulnerable to abnormal pressures). (IELTS5,T4,R1)这些地区很脆弱 （例如 ：经受不起反常的压力 ）。

abolish [əˈbɒlɪʃ]

释义 • v. to do away with; put an end to; annul; make void 消灭；撤销；废除，废止；取消，革除

词根 • ab(去掉 )+ol（成长 ）+-ish（使 ）→使停止生长 →废止

派生 • abolishment n. 废除 ，废止 ，取消

例句 • In the last 20 years, as internal frontiers have been abolished , the EU has moved from a ‘ stock’ economy to a ‘ flow’ economy. (IELTS10,T1,R2)过去二十年 ，随着内部边界被废除 ，欧盟从 “股份经济”转向 “流动经济”。

absolute [’æbsəluːt]

释义 • adj. total and complete绝对的，完全的

派生 • absolutely9 adv. 绝对地

联想 • relative/relatively相对 ；absolute/absolutely 绝对

例句 • It only lasted 11 minutes but was an absolute sensation, and there were cases of people watching. (IELTS6,T2,L4)它仅仅持续了 11分钟 ，但极其轰动 ，有许多人在观看 。

absurdity [əb’sɜ:dətɪ]

释义 • n . the quality or state of being ridiculous or wildly unreasonable荒谬；谬论；极端无理性；荒谬的行为

派生 • absurd adj . 不合理的，荒唐的 absurdly adv . 荒谬地

例句 • This use of dialogue underscores not only the dizzy quality of the character played by Katherine Hepburn, but also the absurdity of the film itself and thus its humor. (IELTS11,T4, R2) 这种对白的运用不仅突出了凯瑟琳·赫本扮演的角色的愚蠢，而且还突出了电影本身的怪诞与幽默。

accentuate [ək’sentʃʊeɪt]

释义 • v. to emphasize sth. or make it more noticeable 使突出；强调

词根 • ac(to)+cent(说 ，唱 )+uate→不断说 →强调

同义 • emphasize, stress

派生 • accentuation n. 重读 ；强调

例句 • However, their effects are probably accentuated by climatic factors, such as drought and hard winters, or soil imbalances such as soil acidification, which damages the roots. (IELTS7,T3,R3)但是 ，它们的影响很可能因气候因素而加重 ，如干旱 、严寒 、土壤不平衡 (例如土壤酸化 )，这些因素都会对根产生危害 。

acclaim [ə’kleɪm]

释义 • v. to welcome (sb./sth.) with shouts of approval; to applaud loudly 称赞，为……喝彩

词根 • ac-含有 at, to之意 ，claim陈述 ，当面对人的陈述一般是好的 。

例句 • There’ s lots to see and do including the new and the internationally-acclaimed climbing wall. (IELTS6,T2, L2)这有好多可以看 、可以玩的 ，包括这面新的蜚声国际的攀岩墙 。

acclimatise [ə’klaɪmətaɪz]

释义 • v. to get (oneself, animals, plants, etc.) used to a new climate or a new environment, new conditions, etc; to become or make accustomed (to sth.) 适应气候

词根 • ac(to)+climate(气候 )+ise(……化 )→适应气候

派生 • acclimatisation n. 适应气候

例句 • After a couple of days to acclimatise yourself, you’ ll start the trek on Day Three walking through the enormous Katiba Forest which will take the whole of the day. (IELTS7,T3,L2)在经过了数天的适应气候之后 ，你会在第三天开始长途跋涉 ，花一整天的时间穿越广阔的 Katiba森林 。

accrue [ə’kruː]

释义 • v. to come as a natural increase or advantage, esp. financial; accumulate 积累，增加

派生 • accrual1 n. 自然增长 ，自然积累 ，自然增长额

例句 • But some Arctic communities are now operating tour businesses themselves, thereby ensuring that the benefits accrue locally. (IELTS5,T4,R1)但是一些北极社区现在自己开发旅游 ，从而保证当地的财富积累 。

accuse [ə’kjuːz]

释义 • v. to say that sb. has done wrong, is guilty (of sth.) or has broken the law 指控，控告，指责

词根 • 已知 cause表示原因 ，可以推出词根 -cuse表示原因 ，则 ac-(to)+cuse表示找原因 、找茬 ，进而推出控告 。

搭配 • accuse sb. of (doing) sth. 控告某人某事

派生 • accusation n. 指控 ，控告 ，指责

accusatory adj. 指责的

例句 • This climatic phenomenon was accused of wrecking tourism. (IELTS5,T1,R1)人们指责这种气候现象影响了旅游业 。

achievable [ə’tʃiːvəbl]

释义 • adj. that can be achieved 可实现的，可获得成功的

词根 • achiev(e)(成功 )+able(能 ……的 )→可实现的 ，可获得成功的

派生 • achieve49 v. 成功

achiever8 n. 成功者

achievement29 n. 成功

例句 • Regardless of whether goals are achievable or well within management’ s perceptions of the employee’ s ability, if employees see them as unachievable they will reduce their effort. (IELTS6,T3,R2)不管目标是否可以实现 ，或者是否在管理者所预期的员工能力范围内 ，如果员工认为这些目标不能实现 ，他们将减少对此的努力 。

acrobatic [ˌækrə’bætɪk]

释义 • adj. of or like an acrobat 杂技的，杂技表演的

词根 • acro(高 )+bat(走 )+ic(adj .)→在高空走的 →杂技的

派生 • acrobatics n. 杂技

acrobat1 n. 杂技演员

例句 • There are no animals—just very talented clowning and acrobatic routines. (IELTS4,T3,R2)没有动物 ——只有极具天赋的小丑表演和常规的杂技表演 。

adept [əˈdept]

释义 • adj. very skilled or proficient at something精于……的

搭配 • be adept at 擅长于

例句 • Yet others go into mathematical procedures, but assume that the reader is adept in using algebra. (IELTS11,T3, R3) 还有一些人则应用了数学的推理过程，并假定读者对代数非常在行。

adjoin [əˈdʒɔɪn]

释义 • v. be next to and joined with (a building, room, or piece of land) 邻近，毗连；接，贴连；附加，使结合

同义 • be adjacent to, border on, verge on, connect with

例句 • Instead, the company has bought some adjoining land, and this will be used to increase the number of parking spaces. (IELTS11,T3, L2) 相反，公司购买了毗邻的一些地，用于扩充停车空间。

adolescence [ˌædə’lesəns]

释义 • n. the time in a person’ s life between childhood and mature adulthood 青春期

联想 • adol(看做是 adult) + escence(看做 essence精髓 )。成年人的精髓来自青春期的积累 。-escent为一后缀 ，意为逐渐成为某一状态 。

派生 • adolescent adj. 青春期的 n .青少年

例句 • It has been calculated that 17 percent of cases of lung cancer can be attributed to high levels of exposure to second-hand tobacco smoke during childhood and adolescence . (IELTS3,T1,R2)据统计 ，17%的肺癌病例可归因于患者在儿童时期或青春期吸入过多的二手烟 。

adornment [ə’dɔːnmənt]

释义 • n. a thing that adorns; an ornament 装饰品，装饰物

词根 • ad(to)+orn(装饰 )+ment (n .)→装饰用的东西

例句 • A series of acquisitions might represent a decade’ s fieldwork documenting social experience as expressed in the developing preferences in personal adornment and dress. (IELTS3,T3,R1)一系列成就可以代表他 10年的实地工作所积累的社会阅历 ，这从他对个人装饰和衣服的喜好中表现出来 。

aeration [eə’reɪʃən]

释义 • n. the circulation of air for purification 通气

词根 • aer(o) (=air,空气 )+ate(v .使通气 )→aeration n. 通气

派生 • aerate v. 使通气

例句 • The tunnels abandoned by the beetles provide excellent aeration and water channels for root systems. (IELTS3,T2，R1) 被甲虫遗弃的地下通道为植物的根系提供了绝佳的通风和汲水管道 。

aero- 空气:

aeroplane n. 飞机

aeronautics n. 航空学

aerospace n. 航空与航天空间

aerobics n. 有氧健身法

aerodynamic adj. 空气动力

学的，流线型的

aerobics [eə’rəʊbɪks]

释义 • n. energetic physical exercises done in order to increase the amount of oxygen taken into the body 有氧运动，健美操

词根 • aero(空气 )+b+ics(……活动 )→有氧运动 →健美操

例句 • This room is used for badminton and aerobics . (IELTS3,T3, L2)这间屋子用于打羽毛球和跳健身操 。

aeronautical [ˌeərə’nɔːtɪkl]

释义 • adj. aeronautical engineering, skills 航天学的

派生 • aeronautics1 n. 航空学

词根 • aero(空气 )+naut(航行 )+ical(ics学 →adj .)→航天学的

例句 • “Unlike smaller pterosaurs, it could use natural currents—its wings continuously,” said Paul MacCready, an aeronautical engineer. (IELTS6,TB, R3) 航天工程师 Paul MacCready 说过 ：“与小的翼龙不同 ，它可以不断利用自然的气流 ——它的双翼 。”

affiliation [əˌfɪlɪ’eɪʃən]

释义 • n. a link or connection made by affiliating 从属关系，联系

派生 • affiliate v. 隶属于 n. 附属机构 ，分会 ，分公司

例句 • A candidate who has a high need for power and a low need for affiliation should be selected. (IELTS6,T3, R2)须选择一位极度需要权利和不需要联营的候选人 。

afflict [ə’flɪkt]

释义 • v. to cause trouble, pain or distress to sb./sth. (疾病或严重问题)折磨，使苦恼

词根 • af(表加强 )+flict(打击 )→一再打击 →使苦恼 ，折磨

派生 • affliction n. 疾病 ；折磨 ；苦恼 ，苦事

例句 • The results of a 14-year study to be announced later this month reveal that the diseases associated with old age are afflicting fewer and fewer people and when they do strike, it is much later in life. (IELTS6,T2,R2)一项历经 14年的研究表明得老年病的人越来越少 ，即便得病 ，发病年龄也推迟了很多 ，这个研究结果将在本月晚些时候宣布 。

affluent [’æfluənt]

释义 • adj . having an abundance of wealth, property, or other material goods; prosperous; rich富有的，富足的

词根 • af-（to）+flu（flow流动 ）+ent（形容词后缀 ）→（财源 ）滚滚来 →富裕的 ，富足的

派生 • affluence n . 富足

例句 • For industry to take off, there needs to be the technology and power to drive factories, large urban populations to provide cheap labour, easy transport to move goods around, an affluent middle-class willing to buy mass-produced objects. (IELTS10,T2,R1)为了产业的发展 ，我们需要技术和能源以推动工厂的建立 ，需要大量城镇人口以提供廉价的劳动力 ，需要便捷的交通以运输货物 ，需要富足的中产阶级愿意购买大批量生产的物品 。

afield [ə’fiːld]

释义 • adv. away, esp. from home; to or at a distance 在远处

词根 • a(at)+field(田野 )→在田野 →远处

搭配 • far afield 在远处

further/farther afield 更远地

例句 • Further afield the mountains of the central North Island, 3 hours’ drive away, provide superb ski facilities in winter, and hiking country in summer. (IELTS3, TA,R2)离新西兰北岛中央高山稍远的地方 ，距此有三小时车程 ，那里冬天有极好的滑雪设施 ，夏天则可以远足 。

aggravate [’æɡrəveɪt]

释义 • v. to make (a disease, a situation, an offence, etc.) worse or more serious 加重，(局势或病情等)恶化，加剧

词根 • 已知 grave表示严重的 ，ag(表强调 )+grav(重的 )+ate(v .)→加重 ，加剧

派生 • aggravation1 n. 恶化 ，加剧

aggravating adj. 恼人的

例句 • In poor countries, governments aggravate other sorts of damage. (IELTS3,T2,R2) 在贫穷国家 ，政府加剧了其他种类的破坏 。

agreeable [ə’ɡriːəbəl]

释义 • adj. pleasing; giving pleasure 令人愉快的，惬意的 ；ready to agree 乐意的

同义 • attractive, enjoyable, pleasing

反义 • disagreeable, offensive

例句 • Such associations can be powerful enough so that odours that we would generally label unpleasant become agreeable . (IELTS8,T2, R3) 这种联想的力量非常强大 ，那些我们一般认为难闻的气味也因此变得惬意了 。

airy [’eərɪ]

释义 • adj. having plenty of fresh air moving about; well-ventilated 通风的

词根 • air+y(adj. 有 ……的 )→有风的 →通风的

例句 • The small dark dressing rooms we used to have, have been converted into two large airy rooms. (IELTS6,T1,L2)我们过去拥有的又小又黑的换衣间已经被换成两间宽敞又通风的房间了 。

-y: 有…的

hairy adj. 多毛的

cloudy adj. 多云的

smoky adj. 烟雾弥漫的

icy adj. 冰冷的

wordy adj. 冗长的

align [ə’laɪn]

释义 • v. to give your support publicly to a group, political party, or country公开支持 ；to join sb. as an ally; come into agreement with sb.结盟 ；to adjust (parts of a mechanism, for example) to produce a proper relationship or orientation 校准，调整，调节

联想 • lign可以想象成 line，a+lign→排成直线 →结盟 ；调整 ，校准

派生 • alignment1 n. 校准 ；调整 ；结盟

例句 • By the late 1980s, the term artificial intelligence was being avoided by many researchers, who opted instead to align themselves with specific sub-disciplines such as neural networks, agent technology, case-based reasoning, and so on. (IELTS5,T3,R3) 到 20世纪 80 年代晚期 ， 许多研究者就避免使用人工智能这个词 ， 他们选择把自己的研究方向归为具体的分支学科 ， 如神经网络 、 代理技术 、 基于案例的推理等等 。

alleged [ə’ledʒd]

释义 • adj . said, without proof, to have taken place or to have a specified illegal or undesirable quality 声称的，所谓的；被断言的

派生 • allege v . 声称，断言

例句 • The alleged gap can be narrowed or completely overcome by anyone, in part because each of us is far from using the full capacity of either side of the brain. (IELTS11,T3, R3) 任何人都可以缩小或者彻底跨越这个鸿沟，部分原因是所有人都远没有彻底开发我们任一边大脑的潜能。

allowance [ə’laʊəns]

释义 • n. the amount of sth., esp. money, allowed or given regularly 津贴 ；deserving to be treated differently from others for some reason 体谅 ；to consider sth. when making a decision, etc. 考虑

联想 • allow(允许 )+ance(n .)→允许 ，容忍 →体谅 ；考虑

搭配 • make allowance/allowances for 考虑到 ，顾及 ，为 ……留有余地 ；体谅 ，原谅

例句 • The lecturers will make little or no allowance for the presence of non-native speakers in the audience. (IELTS5,T3,L2) 演讲人极少或者不会考虑听众中的非母语人士 。

alphabetical [ˌælfə’betɪkəl]

释义 • adj. in the order of the alphabet 按照字母顺序的

联想 • 中学我们学过 α(alpha)和 β(beta)这两个希腊字母 ，它们是希腊的第一 、二个字母 ，正如英文字母中的 AB，因此可以引申出 “按照字母顺序的”意思 。

派生 • alphabet1 n. 字母表

alphabetically1 adv. 按字母顺序地

alphabetize v. 按字母顺序排列

例句 • It is also a good idea to log these alphabetically so that you can find them easily rather like keeping telephone numbers. (IELTS6,TB,R2)一个很好的办法是 ，你可以将这些东西按照字母顺序记录 ，这样很容易就能找到它们 ，就像存电话号码一样 。

alpine [’ælpaɪn]

释义 • adj. of or found in high mountains, esp. the Alps 高山的，阿尔卑斯山的

联想 • 你喜欢阿尔卑斯糖吗 ？吃个糖鼓励一下自己吧 ，顺便把这个单词记住 。

派生 • the Alps2 阿尔卑斯山脉

例句 • Indeed, in some alpine villages, it can be a vehicle for reinvigorating local cultures. (IELTS5,T4,R1) 实际上 ，阿尔卑斯地区的一些山庄可作为复兴当地文化很好的媒介 。

altruistic [ˌæltrʊ’ɪstɪk]

释义 • adj. principle of considering the welfare and happiness of others before one’ s own; unselfishness 利他的，利他主义的

派生 • altruism n. 利他主义

例句 • Yet a green organization opposing such a weakening is seen as altruistic , even if an impartial view might suggest they are doing more harm than good. (IELTS5,T1,R3) 然而一个反对这种弱化的绿色组织被看做是无私的 ，即便公正的观点认为他们的行为是弊大于利的 。

ambassador [æm’bæsədə]

释义 • n. a diplomat sent from one country to another either as a permanent representative or on a special mission 大使

词根 • amb-两边的 ，as-sa联想为去了又回来 ，两边走动 ，即为大使

派生 • embassy n. 使馆

ambassadorial adj. 大使的

搭配 • ambassador to … 驻 ……的大使

例句 • The people you employ are your ambassadors , says Peter Griffin, managing director of a major retailer in the UK. (IELTS3,TB,R3) 英国一家大型零售商的总经理彼得说 ，你雇佣的员工是你公司的形象大使 。

amidst [ə’mɪdst]

释义 • prep . in the middle of (sth.); among 在……之中

联想 • 该词来自现代英语中的 amid, a(in,at)+mid (middle)

例句 • Johnson had worked for nine years, with little assistance of the learned, and without any patronage of the great; not in the soft obscurities of retirement, or under the shelter of academic bowers, but amidst inconvenience and distraction, in sickness and in sorrow. (IELTS5,T1,R1)约翰逊工作了九年 ，在此期间 ，他没有学者的协助 ，没有伟人的关照 ，没有退休后的闲适 ，没有学术界的庇护 ，伴随他的只有不便与干扰 ，疾病与悲伤 。

-st:

通常把一些词变为更文学性的词，如while-whilst, among-

amongst

amphibious [æm’fɪbiəs]

释义 • adj . relating to, living in, or suited for both land and water 水陆两用的；水陆两栖的

词根 • amphi(两边 )+bious(生命的 ) →两地都能生存的

派生 • amphibian2 n . 水陆两栖动物

例句 • Sure enough, these amphibious species show up on the triangular graph approximately half way between the “wet cluster” of sea turtles and the “dry cluster” of land tortoises. (IELTS9,T1,R3) 毫无疑问 ，三角形图表上显示的这些两栖类物种大约介于水生龟和陆生龟之间 。

amplifier [’æmpləˌfaɪə]

释义 • n. a device for amplifying (esp. sounds or radio signals) 扩音器，扬声器

派生 • amplify1 v. 扩大 ，放大 ；进一步阐明

ample2 adj. 足够的 ，充裕的 ，丰富的

联想 • 已知 sample为样本 ，我们在研究时需要 ample sample (充足的样本 )才能把实验做好 。

例句 • They’ d also see that you need motion and an amplifier to make the sound heard. (IELTS4,T4,L3)他们也看到 ，你需要不断走动 ，使用扩音器 ，这样 ，声音才能被听到 。

amplify [ˈæmplɪfaɪ]

释义 • v . increase the volume of (sound), especially using an amplifier增强；详述；放大，扩大

派生 • amplification n .扩大，增强

amplifier n . 扩音器

例句 • In order to improve the acoustic properties of the auditorium and to amplify the sound, they are not straight, they are curved. (IELTS11,T2, L4) 为了改善讲堂的音效，扩大音量，它们被弄成弯曲的，而不是直的。

anatomist [ə’nætəmɪst]

释义 • n. a person who studies anatomy 解剖学家

词根 • ana(分开 )+tom+ist(n .……家 )→解剖学家

派生 • anatomy n. 解剖学

anatomical adj. 解剖的 ，结构上的

anatomize v. 解剖

例句 • It was not until 1791 that the great French anatomist Georges Cuvier deduced that the animal was in fact a flying reptile. (IELTS6,TB,R3) 直到 1791年伟大的法国解剖学家乔治才推断出那种动物实际上是一种会飞的爬行动物 。

animate [’ænəmeɪt]

释义 • v. to give life to (sth/sb); to make lively 使活跃，使生机勃勃，激励 adj. living; having life 活的

词根 • anim(animal)+ate (v .使 ……； adj. 具有 ……性质 )→使活跃 ；活的

派生 • animation1 n. 动画片 ，动画片制作

animated adj. 活跃的

例句 • Early cinema programmes were a mixture of items, combining comic sketches, free-standing narratives, serial episodes and the occasional trick or animated film. (IELTS4,TA,R3) 早期的影院节目是个混合体 ，融合了漫画 、独立的故事片 、连续剧和偶尔出现的搞笑剧或动画片等艺术形式 。

anniversary [ˌænɪ’vɜːsərɪ]

释义 • n. yearly return of the date of an event; celebration of this 周年纪念，纪念日

词根 • 已知 annual每年的 →ann-年 ；universe宇宙 →vers=turn旋转 ；那么 anniversary = ann(i)(一年 )+vers(turn)+-ary→时间整整又转了一年 →周年纪念

例句 • business lunches, anniversaries and weddings, all special occasions (IELTS4,TA,R1) 商务午餐 、周年纪念与婚礼 、所有特殊场合

annoying [ə’nɒɪɪŋ]

释义 • adj. causing vexation or irritation; troublesome: 使人烦恼的，恼人的，讨厌的

词根 • an(in)+noy(恨 )+ing(adj .)→恼人的

派生 • annoy v. 使恼怒 ，使生气 ；打搅

annoyance n. 烦恼 ，烦恼事

annoyed adj. 恼火的

例句 • Subjects reported finding the predictable and unpredictable noise equally annoying , and all subjects performed at about the same level during the noise portion of the experiment. (IELTS7,T4,R3) 实验对象说可预见的噪音和不可预见的噪音同样令人恼火 ，所有的研究对象在试验中对噪音的反应程度都一样 。

antenna [æn’tenə]

释义 • n . one of two long thin parts on an insect’ s head, that it uses to feel things触角，触须 ；a wire rod etc. used for receiving radio and television signals天线

联想 • ant蚂蚁熟悉吧 ？蚂蚁是不是有触角 ？

例句 • The other part of the project is an undirected search which is monitoring all of space with a lower sensitivity, using the smaller antennas of NASA’ s Deep Space Network. (IELTS9,T1,R2) 项目的另一部分没有什么针对性 ，只是利用美国国家航空航天局深空网较小的天线对整个宇宙空间进行低敏度的监测 。

antique [æn’tiːk]

释义 • n. an object having special value because of its age, especially a domestic item or piece of furniture or handicraft esteemed for its artistry, beauty, or period of origin 古物，古玩，古董 adj. of or dealing in antiques 古董的

派生 • antiquity1 n. 古物 ，古建筑物

antiquated1 adj. 陈旧的 ，老式的

例句 • On one side of that you can see the Engine Room and on the other is the Café, which isn’ t an antique . (IELTS4,T1,L2) 在它的一边 ，可看到机房 ，在另外一边是咖啡厅 ，咖啡厅并不是古老建筑 。

apace [ə’peɪs]

释义 • adv. at a rapid pace; swiftly 飞快地

词根 • a(表加强 )+pace(步伐 )→加快步伐 →飞快地

例句 • While policy makers struggle to define and implement appropriate legislation, development of the most destructive kind has continued apace over vast areas. (IELTS3,T3,R2)虽然政策制定者们努力制定和实施合适的法律 ，但是在很多领域最具摧毁力的法律仍然快速发展 。

appalling [ə’pɔːlɪŋ]

释义 • adj. causing consternation or dismay; frightful 令人震惊的，骇人的；非常低劣的

派生 • appall v. 使震惊

appalled adj. 极度惊恐的

例句 • The vast majority of people lived in extreme poverty, and suffered from appalling sanitary conditions. (IELTS6,T1,L4) 很多人极端贫困 ，忍受着极其恶劣的卫生条件 。

apparatus [ˌæpə’reɪtəs]

释义 • n. a set of instruments, etc. used esp. in scientific experiments 器械，设备，装置

词根 • ap(加强 )+para(辅助 )+tus→起辅助作用的东西 →器械

例句 • The orbital cortex seems the best candidate for the site that feeds such feelings into higher-level thought processes, with its close connections to the brain’ s sub-cortical arousal apparatus and centers of metabolic control. (IELTS5,T2,R2) 额眶部皮质是将这些感情植入更高层次思维过程的最佳场所 ，因为它与大脑的次皮层觉醒系统和控制新陈代谢的中心区域有密切联系 。

apportion [ə’pɔːʃən]

释义 • v. to give sth. as a share; to allot sth. 分摊，分配，明确责任人

词根 • ap(加强 )+portion(v .分配 )→分配

派生 • apportionment n. 分摊

搭配 • apportion sth. among/between 在 ……之间分摊

例句 • The problem of how health-care resources should be allocated or apportioned , so that they are distributed in both the most just and most efficient way, is not a new one. (IELTS4,T4,R3)医疗资源该怎么分配才能做到最公正和最有效 ，这个问题存在已久 。

apprehensive [ˌæprɪ’hensɪv]

释义 • adj. feeling anxiety; fearful; uneasy 忧虑的，担心的

联想 • 大家对 comprehension/comprehend肯定熟悉 ，意为理解 ，理解了就抓住了大意 ，那么其词根 prehend则意为抓住 。

词根 • apprehensive来自 apprehend：ap(加强 )+prehend(抓住 )，如果你对一件事情抓得过紧 ，你可能就忧虑了 。

派生 • apprehend v. 逮捕 ，领会

apprehension n. 忧虑 ，恐惧

apprehensively adv. 忧虑地

例句 • The atmosphere is relaxed and unthreatening and great emphasis is placed on developing the confidence and abilities of people who may initially be a little apprehensive . (IELTS4,TA,R1)气氛很轻松 ，没有胁迫感 ，重点是培养起初还有些忧虑的人们的信心和能力 。

apprenticeship [ə’prentɪsʃɪp]

释义 • n. being an apprentice 学徒身份，徒弟

词根 • apprentice (徒弟 ，学徒 )+ship(身份 )

派生 • apprentice1 n . 徒弟 ，学徒

例句 • After serving an apprenticeship in Birmingham, Darby had started a business in Bristol, but he moved to Coalbrookdale in 1710 with an idea that coke derived from coal could provide a more economical alternative to charcoal as a fuel for ironmaking. (IELTS7,TB,R3)在伯明翰学完徒之后 ，Darby来到布里斯托尔创业 ，但在 1710年他又来到 Coalbrookdale，因为他认为用煤炭提取焦炭可以为冶金业提供一种比木炭更为经济的燃料 。

-ship 身份，职位，资格：

doctorship n. 博士学位

citizenship n. 公民权或身份

kingship n. 王位

professorship n. 教授职位

heirship n. 继承权

lordship n. 贵族身份

rulership n. 统治权

studentship n. 学生身份

aptitude [’æptɪtjuːd]

释义 • n. natural ability or skill 才能，天资，悟性

联想 • attitude(态度 )是一种状态 ，故 -itude表示性质 、状态

词根 • apt(能力 )+itude(状态 )→才能 ，天资

例句 • Each division was organized in exactly the same way, used the same technology, did exactly the same kind of work, and had employees of comparable aptitudes . (IELTS3,T4,R3)每个部门都以相同的方式组织 ，使用同样的技术 ，做同样的活 ，雇佣能力基本上相同的员工 。

aquarium [ə’kweərɪəm]

释义 • n. (building containing an) artificial pond or glass tank where live fish and other water creatures and plants are kept 养鱼池，玻璃缸；水族馆

词根 • aqua(水 )+r+ium(表场所 )→水族馆

派生 • aquatic adj. 水生的 ，水栖的

例句 • The internationally acclaimed climbing wall was built on the site of the old aquarium. (IELTS6,T2,L2)世界闻名的攀墙就建立在旧水族馆中 。

arable [’ærəbəl]

释义 • adj. (land that is) suitable for ploughing and for growing crops 适于耕种的

例句 • This is equivalent to 8 dollars for every hectare of arable land and permanent pasture, almost as much again as the local government and EU spend on British farming in that year. (IELTS7,T2,R2) 这相当于可耕地和永久牧场每公顷 8美元 ，等于政府和欧盟在英国农业上当年投入的总和 。

archive [’ɑːkaɪv]

释义 • n. a collection historical documents or records of a government, town, etc. 档案 v. to put or store a document or other material in an archive 把……存入档案

例句 • The Museum of London has drawn on its archive collection to convey a fresh picture with its exhibition. (IELTS3,T4,R2)伦敦博物馆用它的展品来传达新鲜的画面 。

arduous [’ɑːdjʊəs]

释义 • adj. needing much effort or energy; laborious 困难的，艰巨的

同义 • difficult, hard

派生 • arduousness n. 艰巨性

arduously adv. 艰巨地

例句 • Most goods were transported along the paths that provide short-cuts up and down the hillsides, but the paths were a real safety risk and made the journey on foot even more arduous . (IELTS7,T2,R3) 大多数货物都是沿着这些道路运输的 ，这些道路提供上下山的捷径 ，但是却存在极大的安全隐患 ，使步行更加艰难 。

arena [ə’riːnə]

释义 • n. a level area in the centre of an amphitheatre or a sports stadium 竞技场；领域 ；a place or scene of activity or conflict 表演场地，活动舞台

例句 • Environmental education offers an arena in which these skills can be developed, which is essential for these children as future decision-makers. (IELTS4,T1,R2)环境教育为这些技能的培养提供了舞台 ，这对于将来要成为决策者的孩子们是非常重要的 。

ascent [əˈsent]

释义 • n . a climb or walk to the summit of a mountain or hill上升；上坡

词根 • a-(向上)+scent（爬）→向上爬

派生 • ascend v. 上升，攀爬

例句 • Without language, we could never have embarked on our ascent to unparalleled power over all other animals, and even over nature itself. (IELTS11,T4,R3) 没有了语言，我们人类就绝不可能登上傲视其他动物的权力之巅，甚至是征服大自然本身。

ascribe [ə’skraɪb]

释义 • v. to consider sth. to be caused by, written by or belonging to sb./sth. 归因于

联想 • 已知 describe表示描绘 ，推出 scribe意为 “书写”。a(表强调 )+scribe，要追溯原因重点在于有书面证据 ，故而写下来是最好的 。

搭配 • ascribe sth. to sth. 把 ……归因于 ，认定 ……是某物的特点

例句 • A full 94% ascribed happy to the circle, instead of sad. (IELTS4,T1,R3)足足有 94%的人认为圆圈象征着快乐 ，而不是悲伤 。

ash [æʃ]

释义 • n. the powder that remains after sth. has been destroyed by burning 灰，灰烬 ；powder that remains when a dead person’ s body is burned 骨灰，遗骸

例句 • A violent eruption can blow the top few kilometers off a mountain, scatter fine ash practically all over the globe. (IELTS4,T3,R2)强烈的火山爆发可能把山顶喷出几千米远 ，并把细小的灰烬洒落全球 。

ashamed [ə’ʃeɪmd]

释义 • adj. feeling shame, embarrassment, etc. about sth/sb or because of one’ s own actions 羞愧的，惭愧的，负疚的，害臊的

词根 • a (表加强 )+shamed(羞愧 )→羞愧的

例句 • I’ m ashamed to say that the significance of this didn’ t strike me until after I had read 50 or 60 studies. (IELTS5,T3,R2)很惭愧 ，我读了五六十篇相关研究文章以后才认识到它的重要性 。

assimilation [əˌsɪmə’leɪʃən]

释义 • n. the process of assimilating or being assimilated 吸收，吸取 ；a change in a speech sound when it becomes similar to another speech sound next to it 同化

联想 • 已知 similar意为相同 ，as-意为加强 ，-ation为名词后缀 。为了使你的特点与其他东西取得一致 ，你需要吸收一些东西 。

派生 • assimilate v. 吸收 ；同化 ，使融入

例句 • With the independence of much of Asia and Africa after 1945, it was assumed that economic progress would rapidly lead to the disappearance or assimilation of many small-scale societies. (IELTS3,T3,R1) 人们认为 ，随着 1945年后亚洲和非洲很多国家独立 ，经济进步会很快导致很多小型社会消亡或同化 。

assortment [ə’sɔːtmənt]

释义 • n. a collection of different things or of different types of the same thing; mixture 混杂物，各类东西的混合

词根 • as+sort(种类 )+ment(n .) →很多种类放在一起 →混杂物

派生 • assort v. 把 ……归类

assorted adj. 各种各样的 ，五花八门的

例句 • The supposed pupil was in reality an actor hired by Milgram to simulate receiving the shocks by emitting a spectrum of groans, screams and writhings together with an assortment of statements and expletives denouncing both the experiment and the experimenter. (IELTS5,T1,R2) 所谓的学生实际上是由 Milgram 雇来的 。 他们通过发出一系列呻吟和尖叫声来模仿受到电击后的反应 ， 嘴上骂骂咧咧 ， 谴责试验与试验者 ， 同时身体翻滚 。

astound [ə’staʊnd]

释义 • v. to overcome (sb.) with surprise or shock; amaze 使震惊

联想 • as+tound(看作 sound)→像被大声所吓倒 →震惊

派生 • astounded adj. 惊呆的 ，惊愕的

astounding adj. 令人震惊的 ，使人惊愕的

例句 • The fertile land of the Nile delta is being eroded along Egypt’ s Mediterranean coast at an astounding rate, in some parts estimated at 100 meters per year. (IELTS5,T3,R2) 尼罗河三角洲埃及地中海海岸一带肥沃的土地正在以惊人的速度被侵蚀 ，有些地方预计达到每年 100米 。

astray [ə’streɪ]

释义 • adv. away from the right path or direction 迷路地，误入歧途地；搞错地

联想 • as(像 )+tray(盘子 )→像在盘子里转圈圈 →迷路地

搭配 • go astray 迷路 ，走失

lead sb. astray 将 (某人 )引入歧途

例句 • A bit of background would not go astray . (IELTS3,T4, L4) 掌握一点背景知识就不会搞错 。

atom [’ætəm]

释义 • n. the smallest part of an element that can exist chemically 原子

派生 • atomic adj. 原子的 ，原子能的

atomize v. 使粉碎 ，使成小块

例句 • As the glass is heated, these atoms react to form tiny crystals of nickel sulphide. (IELTS5,T4,R2) 随着玻璃受热 ，这些原子发生反应并形成微小的镍硫化物晶体 。

attachment [ə’tætʃmənt]

释义 • n. a thing that is or can be attached 附件，附加装置 ；affection; devotion 爱慕，喜爱

词根 • at( 加强 ) +tach( 接触 )+ment( n .) → 接触上的东西 → 附件 ； 如果是感情方面的接触 ， 那就是爱慕

派生 • attach6 v. 缚 ，系 ；附上

attached7 adj. 连接的 ，附加的 ；非常喜爱的

例句 • Perhaps the most fundamental step in developing a sense of number is not the ability to count, but rather to see that a number is really an abstract idea instead of a simple attachment to a group of particular objects. (IELTS6,T2,R3)培养数字敏感性最重要的步骤并不是计算的能力 ，也不是仅仅把其看作是一组特定物体附属物的能力 ，而是将数字看作一个抽象的概念的能力 。

attendance [ə’tendəns]

释义 • n. the action or time of being present 出席 ；the number of people present 出席人数

词根 • at+tend (伸展 )+ance(n .)→大家都伸展脖子看的状态 →出席

派生 • attend21 v. 出席 ；照料 ；专心于 ，致力于

attention20 n. 注意

attendant2 n. 服务员 ，侍者 adj. 伴随的 ，随之产生的 ；照料的

例句 • She also has a few ,000 honoraria to offer in exchange for doctors’ attendance at her company’ s next educational lecture. (IELTS6,T4,R1) 为了让医生们来参加她公司的下期教育报告 ，她还准备了几份价值 1000美元的谢礼 。

audio-visual [ˌɔːdɪəʊ’vɪʒʊəl]

释义 • adj. using both sight and sound 音像的，视听的

词根 • 已知 audience推出 audi-表示听 ，已知 visible推出 vis-表示看

派生 • audio2 adj. 听觉的 ；声音的

auditory1 adj. 听觉的 ，听力的

visual1 adj. 视觉的

例句 • The Carey Learning Resources Centre provides easy access to a wide range of printed and audiovisual learning materials which can help students with coursework. (IELTS4,TA,R2) 凯里学习资源中心提供大量的书面材料和视听材料 ， 可以帮助学生学习课 程 。

autocratic [ˌɔːtə’krætɪk]

释义 • adj. ruling with complete power 独裁的，专制的

词根 • auto(自己的 )+crat(统治者 )+ic→自己统治的 →专制的

派生 • autocrat n. 独裁者 ，专制者

autocracy n. 独裁政治 ，独裁权

例句 • Just as a doctor calls on the full power of autocratic suggestion by insisting that the patient take precisely this white capsule precisely three times a day before meals, Lozanov is categoric in insisting that the suggestopedic session be conducted exactly in the manner designated, by trained and accredited suggestopedic teachers. (IELTS7,T1,R3) 就像医生坚持让病人必须每天三次在饭前服用这种白色胶囊一样 ，Lozanov 坚持认为暗示法教学会议必须由受过良好培训 、经过认证的暗示法教学老师主持 ，这一点没有任何回旋的余地 。

automobile [’ɔːtəməbiːl]

释义 • n. a car 汽车

词根 • auto(自己 )+mobile(移动的 )→自己能够移动的 →汽车

例句 • When Britain’ s Royal Automobile Club monitored the exhausts of 60,000 vehicles, it found that 12 percent of them produced more than half the total pollution. (IELTS3,T4,R1)英国皇家汽车俱乐部监测了 60,000辆汽车的尾气 ，发现其中 12%的车辆造成的污染占所有污染的一半还多 。

avid [’ævɪd]

释义 • adj. eager; greedy热衷的，渴望的

派生 • avidity n. 热衷 ，渴望

avidly1 adv. 渴望地

例句 • Packed full of information for the avid hiker, this book is a must. (IELTS5,TA,R1)这本书包含了热衷于徒步旅行的人应该了解的所有信息 ，因此对他们来说是必备品 。

await [ə’weɪt]

释义 • v. to wait for (sb./sth.)等待，期待

词根 • a(加强 )+wait(等待 )→等待 ，期待

例句 • A friendly greeting awaits new members. (IELTS4,TA,R1) 友好地期待新成员 。

awayday [ə’weɪdeɪ]

释义 • n. a trip taken for pleasure, relaxation, etc.; day excursion消遣，放松的旅行

例句 • Special family awayday fares are available for this service now during the school holidays. (IELTS6,T2,L2) 学校放假期间 ，这项服务提供家庭欢乐游特价票 。

awful [’ɔːfəl]

释义 • adj. very bad; dreadful 糟糕的

例句 • Everybody says that the food is awful . (IELTS5,T3,L2) 大家都说食物很糟糕 。

awkward [’ɔːkwəd]

释义 • adj. causing difficulty, embarrassment or inconvenience 难处理的，棘手的，令人尴尬的

例句 • This would have made flying awkward , as they would have lacked the endurance to power their muscles for long periods of time. (IELTS6,TB,R3)这可能使飞行很艰难 ，因为他们没有足够的耐力长时间为肌肉提供动力 。

babyish [’beɪbɪɪʃ]

释义 • adj. of, like or suitable for a baby 适合婴儿的，适合幼儿的；婴儿般的，幼稚的

词根 • baby(婴儿 )+ish(如 ……的 ，有 ……性质的 )→婴儿般的

例句 • Don’ t you think the activity itself is a bit babyish ? (IELTS4,T4, L3) 你不觉得活动本身有点幼稚吗 ？

bachelor [’bætʃələ]

释义 • n. an unmarried man未婚男子，单身汉 ；a person who holds a first university degree 学士

例句 • From a soldier in the ranks to officer, from bachelor to married man, the change of role has to have a very obvious sign. (IELTS3,T2,R3)从士兵到军官 ，从单身汉到已婚男人 ，角色转换必须有很明显的迹象 。

backdrop [’bækdrɒp]

释义 • n. the conditions or situation in which something happens 背景

例句 • It was against this backdrop that Perkin’ s discovery was made. (IELTS9,T1,R1)正是在这种背景下 ，珀金做出了他的发现 。

backlash [’bæklæʃ]

释义 • n. a strong, negative, and often angry reaction to something that has happened, especially a political or social change (尤指对政治或社会变化的)强烈反应

联想 • lash意为鞭子 ，可以想象一条长鞭 (lash)把人打成灰烬 。back+lash表示反击 →反应

例句 • Thinking computers and household robots failed to materialize, and a backlash ensued. (IELTS5,T3,R3)有思维的电脑以及家用的机器人都不能成为现实 ，随之产生了强烈反应 。

backup [’bækʌp]

释义 • n. a person or thing that supports or reinforces another 支持，后援

例句 • The higher the children’ s IQ scores, the better the quality of their educational backup , measured in terms of reported verbal interactions with parents, number of books and activities in their home etc. (IELTS10,T2,R2)儿童的智商越高 ，他们受到额外教育的质量就会更高 。这体现在与父母的言语交流 、家中书本的数量和活动等 。

baggage [’bægɪdʒ]

释义 • n. trunks, suitcases, etc., used in traveling; luggage 行李

例句 • Baggage services (IELTS10,TB,R1)行李服务

bale [beɪl]

释义 • n. a large bundle of paper, straw, goods, etc. pressed together and tied with rope or wire ready to be moved, sold, etc. 大包，大捆 v. to make sth. into or pack sth. in bales 把……打包

例句 • We also discovered that waste that’ s collected from householders is taken to places called “bring banks”, for sorting and baling into loads. (IELTS5,T3,L4) 我们还发现 ，从住户处收集的垃圾都被运往了一个叫 “bring banks”的地方进行分类打包装载 。

bathing [’beɪðɪŋ]

释义 • n. a washing or immersion of something, especially the body, in water, steam, etc., as for cleansing or medical treatment 沐浴

例句 • During the sixth and seventh centuries, the inhabitants of the modern-day states of Gujarat and Rajasthan in north-western India developed a method of gaining access to clean, fresh groundwater during the dry season for drinking, bathing , watering animals and irrigation. (IELTS10,T1,R1)在公元6世纪和7世纪时期 ，印度西北部即现代古吉拉特和拉贾斯坦邦的居民发明了一种办法 ，能够在干旱季节获取干净 、新鲜的地下水 ，用来饮用 、沐浴 、畜牧和灌溉 。

baulk [bɔːk]

释义 • v. to deliberately obstruct or prevent (sth.) 阻碍，妨碍(目的、计划等) ；to be reluctant to tackle sth. because it is difficult, dangerous, unpleasant, etc. 犹豫不决，举棋不定

同义 • hesitate

例句 • Many of the teacher-subjects baulked at administering the higher levels of punishment, and turned to Milgram with questioning looks and/or complaints about continuing the experiment. (IELTS5,T1,R2) 许多参加实验的教师都对施加更高级的惩罚感到犹豫 ，他们向 Milgram投以质问的目光 ，抱怨继续进行实验 。

ballet [’bæleɪ]

释义 • n. a style of dancing used to tell a story in a dramatic performance with music but without speech or singing 芭蕾舞

例句 • The dance studio provides a smaller, more intimate space, which we use for ballet , modern dance and martial arts. (IELTS3,T3,L2) 舞蹈演播室提供了更小的 、更私密的空间 ，我们用它来练习芭蕾 、现代舞和武术 。

banal [bəˈnɑ:l]

释义 • adj. so lacking in originality as to be obvious and boring 平庸的；陈腐的

同义 • vapid, conventional, stereotyped, stale, commonplace

例句 • For example, in the highly successful science-fiction film 2001 , little dialogue was evident, and most of it was banal and of little intrinsic interest. (IELTS11,T4, R2) 比如，在这部成功的科幻电影《2001》中，明显的对白很少，多数对白都很陈腐，没什么意思。

bargain [’bɑːɡɪn]

释义 • n. an agreement in which both or all sides promise to do sth. for each other 交易，契约，合同 ；a thing bought or sold for less than its usual price 特价商品，便宜货 v. to discuss (with sb.) prices, terms of trade, etc. with the aim of buying or selling goods, or changing conditions, on terms that are favourable to oneself 讨价还价

同义 • trade, business, transaction, contract, deal

搭配 • into the bargain 另外 ，加之

drive a bargain 讨价还价

make a bargain with 与 ……签订合同

bargain for/on 企图廉价获取

例句 • It sounds like a bargain to me. (IELTS8,T1,L1) 听起来对我来说很划算 。

barge [bɑːdʒ]

释义 • n. a large flat-bottomed boat for carrying goods and people on rivers, canals, etc. 平底载货船，驳船 v. to rush or bump heavily and clumsily 碰撞

例句 • But the picture clearly shows sections of the bridge being raised from a barge in the river. (IELTS7,TB,R3) 但那张图片清楚地显示桥的几个部分正从河中驳船的位置开始上升 。

basement [’beɪsmənt]

释义 • n. a lowest room or rooms in a building, partly or wholly below ground level 地下室；地下层

词根 • base(基础 )+ment(n .)→地下层 ；地下室

例句 • The entire ocean floor has a basement of volcanic basalt. (IELTS4,T3,R2)整个海底都有火山玄武岩层 。

batter [’bætə]

释义 • v. to hit (sb./sth.) hard and often 连击，打碎；连续猛打

例句 • Because of the typhoons that batter Japan in the summer, Japanese builders learned to extend the eaves of buildings further beyond the walls. (IELTS7,T2, R1) 由于夏季台风猛袭日本 ，日本的建筑师们学会了将建筑物的屋檐延长 ，直至 超过墙壁 。

bead [bi:d]

释义 • n. a small, usually round object of glass, wood, stone, or the like with a hole through it, often strung with others of its kind in necklaces, rosaries, etc. 有孔小珠

例句 • In the time of Queen Victoria of England (1837-1901), some pieces were made into fashionable amber beads that women wore around their necks. (IELTS10,TA,R3) 在英国维多利亚女王时代 (1837-1901)， 一些东西被做成时尚的琥珀珠子 ， 女人们把它们戴在脖子上 。

beneficiary [ˌbenə’fɪʃərɪ]

释义 • n. a person who receives sth., esp. one who receives money, property, etc. when sb. dies 受益人，受惠者

词根 • bene(善 ，好 )+fici(做 )+ary(表示人 )→从善行中行到好处的人 →受益人 ，受惠者

派生 • benefit62 n. 益处 ，好处 v. 受益 ，得到好处

beneficial7 adj. 有益的 ，有利的

例句 • We appreciate that some of our ideas may not be feasible in the circumstances, but we do feel that it is important that the ultimate beneficiaries of the facilities should have some say in its design. (IELTS4,T3,L4) 我们知道我们的一些想法可能在某些情况下不可行 ， 但是我们觉得作为这些设备的最终受益者 ， 我们对它的设计应该有一定的发言权 。

besiege [bɪ’siːdʒ]

释义 • v. to surround a place, especially with an army, to prevent people or supplies getting in or out围攻，包围

例句 • He was thwarted by the fact that the British were besieging his observation site at Pondicherry in India. (IELTS9,T2,R2) 由于英国人包围了他在印度本地治里的观察台 ，他不得不中止观察 。

bestow [bɪ’stəʊ]

释义 • v. to present as a gift; give; confer (usually followed by on or upon) 赠给，授予

同义 • confer, donate, grant, award, present, offer

例句 • In setting up the Nobel Foundation and the Nobel Peace Prizes, he hoped to accomplish what he had not been able to do during his lifetime: to encourage research and activities that would bestow the ‘ greatest benefit to mankind’ , especially peace and fraternity between nations. (IELTS10,TB,R3)他设立诺贝尔基金和诺贝尔奖 ，是希望能够完成在他有生之年不能实现的事情 ：鼓励那些能够赐予 “人类最大福祉”的研究和活动 ，特别是各国之间和平 、友爱的研究和活动 。

betray [bɪ’treɪ]

释义 • v. to hand over or show sb./sth. disloyally (to an enemy) 背叛，出卖 ；to show what or who one really is 暴露；辜负

联想 • 本词发音类似 “被踹”→被人暗地里踹了一脚 →出卖

派生 • betrayal n. 背叛

例句 • But the human history of Amazonia in the past 11,000 years betrays that view as myth. (IELTS3,T3,R2) 但是亚马逊流域过去 11,000年的人类历史显示那种观念只是神话 。

bewildering [bɪ’wɪldərɪŋ]

释义 • adj. extremely confusing 让人困惑的

同义 • baffling, confounding, puzzling, perplexing

例句 • This gum came in a bewildering variety of colours, degree of transparency and hardness, depending on the length and location of burial, as well as the health of the original tree and the area of the bleeding. (IELTS10, TA, R3)这种树胶有各种令人眼花缭乱的颜色 ，透明度和硬度也各不相同 ，这取决于被埋藏的时长和埋藏地点 ，以及原来树木的健康状况和裂口的位置 。

bias [’baɪəs]

释义 • n. an opinion or feeling that strongly favours one side in an argument or one item in a group or series; predisposition; prejudice 偏见，偏心，偏袒 v. to give a bias to sb.; to prejudice sb.; to influence sb., esp. unfairly 使有偏见

派生 • biased1 adj. 有偏见的 ，偏袒一方的

例句 • Cinema presents a biased view of other countries. (IELTS6,T3, R1)电影对其他国家的描述是有偏见的 。

bizarre [bɪ’zɑː]

释义 • adj. strange in appearance or effect; grotesque; eccentric 古怪的，奇怪的

同义 • strange, odd, eccentric, grotesque

例句 • The most bizarre case was a telephone interview I did with a teacher at a university in France. (IELTS8, T2, L4) 最奇怪的例子是我跟一位法国大学的老师做的电话采访 。

blade [bleɪd]

释义 • n. a flat narrow leaf of certain plants, esp. grasses and cereals 刀片，叶片，浆叶

联想 • 还记得电影 《刀锋战士 》吗 ？英文名为 Blade 。

例句 • The stone blade of a plough has been discovered during excavation in County Mayo in western Ireland. (IELTS6,T3, L4) 人们在西爱尔兰的梅奥郡挖掘时发现了装有石头犁片的犁 。

bleeper [’bliːpə]

释义 • n. a device that emits bleeps 传呼机，能够发出短促声音的电子装置

联想 • 本词与 beeper意思相同

派生 • bleep n. (电子装置发出的 )短促高音 v. 发出短促高音 ，发出嘟嘟声

例句 • You’ ve made the jigsaw for blind children, with the bleeper . (IELTS3,T3,L3)你用能够发出短促声音的电子装置为盲人儿童制作了拼图游戏 。

blink [blɪŋk]

释义 • v. to shut and open the eyes quickly 眨眼，闪烁 n. the act of blinking 眨眼睛

搭配 • in the blink of an eye 一眨眼功夫

例句 • Energy and arousal levels may need to be retuned in the blink of an eye. (IELTS5,T2,R2)能量和清醒水平需在极快的时间内恢复 。

blonde [blɒnd]

释义 • adj. (of hair) pale gold in colour(头发)浅黄色的，金黄色的 n. a woman having golden or pale-coloured hair 金发女郎

例句 • Hence, there is some likelihood that all accountants will be alike or that all blondes are similar—they are forced that way by the expectations of their role. (IELTS3,T2, R3)因此 ，很可能所有的会计都很相似 ，就像所有的金发女郎都相似一样 ——她们的角色期望值迫使她们必须这样 。

bloom [bluːm]

释义 • n. a flower, esp. of plants admired chiefly for their flowers (e.g. roses, tulips, chrysanthemums) 花 v. to produce flowers; to flower; to blossom 开花 ；to be in a healthy or flourishing condition 繁盛，兴旺

搭配 • in full bloom 盛开着花

例句 • If it were not for the dung beetle, chemical fertilizer and dung would be washed by rain into streams and rivers before it could be absorbed into the hard earth, polluting water courses and causing blooms of blue-green algae. (IELTS3,T2,R1)如果没有屎壳郎 ，化学肥料和牛粪就会被雨水冲进小溪和江河 ，而不会被硬地所吸收 ，这样就会污染水道 ，并使水藻迅速繁衍 ，生长 。

bold [bəʊld]

释义 • adj. confident and brave; daring; enterprising 勇敢的，大胆的 ；clearly visible; distinct; striking; vivid 鲜明的，醒目的 ；printed in thick type 粗的，黑体的 ；dare (to do sth); presume or venture 冒失的

同义 • fearless, dauntless, gallant, audacious; striking, conspicuous, evident; rash, abrupt

派生 • boldness n. 大胆 ，勇敢

boldly adv. 大胆地

例句 • They could decide on a bolder move and offer some new shares if they wanted. (IELTS5,T4,L3) 如果他们想这么做的话 ，他们可以决定采取更为大胆的行动并提供一些新的份额 。

bombard [bɔm’bɑ:d]

释义 • v. to attack (a place or person) continuously with bombs, shells, or other missiles (用炸弹、炮弹、导弹等)连续轰炸，连续攻击

词根 • bomb(轰击 )+ard→轰炸

例句 • The best way to see things differently to other people is to bombard the brain with things it has never encountered before. (IELTS9,T2,R3) 要想形成与众不同的看法 ，最好的方法就是给大脑灌输新鲜事物 。

booth [buːð]

释义 • n. a small enclosure or compartment for a specific purpose (隔开的)小房间；公用电话亭 ；a small, usu. temporary, stall where goods are sold or displayed at a market, a fair or an exhibition 售货棚

例句 • We’ ve also put those of you who’ ll be staffing the information booths around the conference centre on the yellow team. (IELTS6,T4,L2)我们把在会议中心四周的问讯亭服务志愿者分在黄队 。

botanist [’bɒtənɪst]

释义 • n. an expert in botany 植物学家

派生 • botany n. 植物学

botanical3 adj. 植物学的

例句 • The grain itself was destroyed by the firing, but it left an impression on the pot which could be studied and identified by botanists . (IELTS6,T3,L4) 谷粒是被火烧掉了 ，但它在容器上留下了痕迹 ，植物学家可以对这些痕迹进行研究和辨认 。

bounty [’baʊntɪ]

释义 • n. a generous gift慷慨的赠予物 ；a reward or payment offered (usu. by a government) to encourage sb. to do sth. (e.g. to increase production of goods) 奖金，赏金

派生 • bountiful adj. 慷慨的 ，大方的

例句 • Taking advantage of this rich bounty , Alaskas commercial fisheries have developed into some of the largest in the world. (IELTS7,T4,R2)阿拉斯加的商业型渔业充分利用这个得天独厚的优势 ，已经发展成为世界上最大规模的渔业产业之一 。

bout [baʊt]

释义 • n. a short period of a specified activity (生病或感到不愉快的)一段，一阵，一场

例句 • Siviy studied how bouts of play affected the brain’ s levels of a particular chemical associated with the stimulation and growth of nerve cells. (IELTS4,T2, R3) Siviy研究一阵阵玩耍是怎样影响大脑中某个特定化学物质的水平的 ，这些化学物质刺激并促进神经细胞的生长 。

bow [bəʊ]

释义 • v. to bend the head or body as a sign of respect or as a greeting 鞠躬，弯腰 n. bending of the head or body (as a greeting, etc.) 鞠躬 ；a piece of wood bent into a curve by a tight string joining its ends, used as a weapon for shooting arrows 弓 ；a knot made with loops; ribbon tied in this way 蝴蝶结

联想 • rainbow彩虹就是天上色彩多样的 “弓形物”(bow)

例句 • Other than bows , arrows and crude digging sticks, the only tools the Siriono seemed to possess were two machetes worn to the size of pocket-knives. (IELTS3,T3,R2)除了弓 、箭和原始的挖掘棍 ，Siriono拥有的唯一工具是两个砍刀 ，它们被磨成口袋刀那样的尺寸 。

bracelet [’breɪslət]

释义 • n. an ornamental band or circlet for the wrist or arm or, sometimes, for the ankle 手镯

例句 • The occasional lump that contained preserved insects was prized for use in necklaces and bracelets . (IELTS10,TA,R3)偶尔出现的含有昆虫尸体的大块琥珀是制作项链和手镯的最佳原料 。

brand [brænd]

释义 • n. particular make of goods or their trade mark 商标，品牌 v. to mark sth. with or as if with a brand 铭刻，打烙印于

派生 • branded adj. 名牌的

branding1 n. 品牌创建

例句 • But translating corporate philosophies into the right mix of colour, style, degree of branding and uniformity can be a fraught process. (IELTS3,TB,R3) 但是将企业理念变成颜色 、风格 、品牌特色和一致性的有机融合是极有难度的过程 。

breast [brest]

释义 • n. (in bipeds) the outer, front part of the thorax, or the front part of the body from the neck to the abdomen; chest 乳房，乳腺；胸脯，胸部

例句 • Macfarlane guessed that the fact that water had to be boiled, together with the stomach-purifying properties of tea meant that the breast milk provided by mothers was healthier than it had ever been. (IELTS10,T2,R1) Macfarlane猜想 ，茶水必须要煮沸 ，而且茶叶具有清洁肠胃的特征 ，这使得母乳比之前更加健康 。

bribe [’braɪb]

释义 • v. to give a bribe (of sth.) to sb.; try to persuade sb. to do sth. with a bribe 向……行贿，收买，贿赂 n. a thing given, offered or promised to sb. to influence or persuade him to do sth. (often dishonest) for the giver 贿赂，贿赂物

搭配 • bribe sb. to do sth. 贿赂某人去做某事

派生 • bribery n. 行贿

例句 • Salespeople are bribing the doctors to prescribe their drugs. (IELTS6,T4,R1)推销员贿赂医生 ，目的是想让医生开他们销售的药品 。

brittle [’brɪtl]

释义 • adj. hard but easily broken; fragile 脆的，易碎的 ；easily damaged; insecure (关系)不牢固的，靠不住的

联想 • break sth. down to little pieces 把某物弄成一小片一小片的 →易碎的

例句 • Geologists consider the Earth as having a molten core, surrounded by a semi-molten mantle and a brittle, outer skin. (IELTS4,T3,R2)地质学家认为地球有熔化的地心 ，外面包着半熔化的地幔 ，最外面的是不牢固的地表 。

broker [’brəʊkə(r)]

释义 • n. an agent who buys or sells for a principal on a commission basis without having title to the property（股票、外币等）经纪人

例句 • You can build this up from your own market research, existing clients and advertising responses, or you can contact list brokers and rent or buy a compiled list. (IELTS10,TA,R2)你可以从市场调研 、已有客户和广告活动反馈中积累联系人 ，也可以联系名单经纪人 ，租赁或购买一份汇总的名单 。

bronze [brɒnz]

释义 • n. an alloy of copper and tin 青铜 adj. made of or having the colour of bronze 青铜的

联想 • bronze medal铜牌

silver medal银牌

gold medal金牌

例句 • The Bronze scheme would probably suit you best. (IELTS6,T1,L1)青铜计划可能最适合你了 。

brood [bruːd]

释义 • v. to think (about sth.) for a long time in a troubled or resentful way 沉思 ；to sit on eggs to hatch them 孵蛋 n. all the young birds or other animals produced at one hatching or birth (小鸡等)一窝

联想 • 一家的孩子 (brood)肯定都留着同样的血 (blood)

例句 • These beetles make sausage-shaped brood chambers along the tunnels. (IELTS3, T2,R1)这些甲虫沿着洞穴建立香肠形状的卵室 。

browse [braʊz]

释义 • v . to examine books in a casual, leisurely way 浏览，翻阅，漫不经心地看 ；(of cows, goats, etc.) to eat leaves, etc. that are growing high up牲畜吃草

搭配 • browse through 浏览

例句 • Do take time to browse round our shop. (IELTS8,T2,L2) 一定要花时间浏览一下我们的商店 。

brute [bruːt]

释义 • n. an animal, esp. a large or fierce one 野兽，畜生 ；a brutal and insensitive person 愚蠢、残忍而粗野的人 adj. of or like a brute 畜生(一般)的，残忍的

派生 • brutal adj. 野兽般的 ，残忍的 ；无情的 ，冷酷的

例句 • The evidence for using kites to move large stones is no better or worse than the evidence for the brute force method, Gharib says. (IELTS7,T4,R1) 用风筝运巨石的证据与用蛮力的方式相差无几 ，Gharib如是说 。

bulge [bʌldʒ]

释义 • n. a rounded swelling; an outward curve 突出，膨胀 v. to form a bulge; to swell outwards 突出，膨胀

例句 • During a routine mail screen that can take hours, the dogs stay so focused that not even a postcard lined with 0.5 grams of heroin and hidden in a bulging sack of letters escapes detection. (IELTS7,TA,R3) 在一般持续几个小时的常规邮件检查中 ，狗都可以保持很好的注意力 ，即使是隐藏在一满袋信中的含有 0.5克海洛因的明信片也逃不出它们的法眼 。

bulk [bʌlk]

释义 • n. a large amounts 大量，大批

联想 • 公牛 (bull)总是大批 (bulk)地行动

派生 • bulky2 adj. 笨重的 ，庞大的

例句 • Bulk cargo can be safely and efficiently moved over long distances. (IELTS6,T1,R2)大批量货物可以安全高效地长途运输 。

bump [bʌmp]

释义 • v. to knock or strike sth. with a dull-sounding blow; to collide with sth. 撞伤，(使)撞击，猛击

搭配 • bump into 邂逅 ，不期而遇

例句 • The flow, thought to be in the form of convection currents, is powerful enough to fracture the eggshell of the crust into plates, and keep them bumping and grinding against each other, or even overlapping, at the rate of a few centimeters a year. (IELTS4,T3,R2)水的流动虽然是对流的形式 ，但力量也非常大 ，可以将地壳的薄壳磨成片状 ，使它们相互撞击摩擦 ，甚至以每年几厘米的速度叠加在一起 。

bumper [’bʌmpə]

释义 • n. a bar fixed to the front and back of a motor vehicle to lessen the effect of a collision (汽车车身前后的)保险杠

例句 • Pacrite recycles all sorts of things, from bottles to car bumpers , and one of its most successful activities is recycling plastic bottles to make containers which are used all over the country to collect waste. (IELTS5,T3,L4) Pacrite循环利用很多东西 ，包括瓶子和汽车保险杠等 。它最成功的举措是循环利用塑料瓶 ，把塑料瓶制成容器 。全国都在用这种容器装垃圾 。

bureaucratic [ˌbjʊərə’krætɪk]

释义 • adj. involving a lot of complicated official rules and processes 官僚的，官僚主义的；繁琐的

词根 • bureau(政府的部 ，司 ，局 ，处 ，署 )+cratic(adj .统治的 )→官僚主义的

派生 • bureaucracy n. 官僚作风

bureaucrat n. 官僚 ，官僚主义者

例句 • However, if the job to be filled is a managerial pest in a large bureaucratic organization, a candidate who has a high need for power and a low need for affiliation should be selected. (IELTS6,T3,R2) 然而 ，如果空缺的职位是大型官僚组织中的一个管理人员的话 ，那么就应该选择一个有极高的权力欲望和不需要联营的人 。

burglar [’bɜːɡlə]

释义 • n. a person who enters a building illegally, esp. by force, in order to steal 窃贼

联想 • burg(看做 bag)+lar→背着大包入室盗窃 →窃贼

派生 • burglary2 n. 入室盗窃 (罪 )

burgle v. 入室盗窃

例句 • This is a fake video camera which you fix to your wall to scare off burglars . (IELTS3,T4,L2) 这是一个假摄像机 ，你可以把它装在墙上吓跑窃贼 。

bygone [ˈbaɪgɒn]

释义 • adj. past; gone by; earlier; former 过去的

例句 • Richard Cox travelled to north-western India to document these spectacular monuments from a bygone era. (IELTS10,T1,R1) Richard Cox游历至印度西北部 ，如实记录了这些从古代遗留下来的壮观遗迹 。

camouflage [’kæməflɑːʒ]

释义 • n. a way of hiding or disguising soldiers, military equipment, etc, e.g. with paint, netting or leaves, so that they look like part of their surroundings 伪装，掩饰；迷彩服 v. to hide (sb./sth.) by camouflage 把……伪装起来，掩盖

例句 • HNC claim that their system, based on a cluster of 30 processors, could be used to spot camouflaged vehicles on a battlefield or extract a voice signal from a noisy background—tasks humans can do well, but computers cannot. (IELTS5,T3,R3) HNC 宣称 ， 他们的系统建立在 30 个处理器的集合体之上 ， 可以用来识别战场上经过伪装的车辆 ， 或者在喧闹的背景中分离出声音信号 —— 这些事情人类能做好 ， 但是电脑却不能 。

cap [kæp]

释义 • n. a soft head-covering without a brim but often with a peak, worn by men and boys 帽子 v. to put a cap on (sth.); to cover the top or end of 盖在……上面

例句 • During quiet periods, volcanoes cap themselves with their own lava by forming a powerful cone from the molten rocks slopping over the rim of the crater. (IELTS4,T3, R2) 在休眠期 ，溢出火山口边缘的熔岩形成一个强大的锥形 ，火山就是通过这种方式用岩浆把自己盖住的 。

capitalism [’kæpɪtlɪzəm]

释义 • n. economicsystem in which a country’ s trade and industry are controlled by private owners for profit, rather than by the State 资本主义

词根 • capital (资本 )+ism(主义 )→资本主义

派生 • capital9 n. 资本 ；首都 ；大写

capitalist n. 资本家 adj. 资本主义的

例句 • Back in 1928, the British writer George Bernard Shaw wrote in his Intelligent Women ’ s Guide to Socialism and Capitalism that “A man is supposed to understand politics, economics and finance and is therefore unwilling to accept essential instruction.” (IELTS5,T1,L4)早在 1928年 ，英国作家乔治 · 肖伯纳就在他的 《智慧女人的社会主义与资本主义指南 》一书中指出 “男人应该懂得政治 、经济和金融 ，因此他们不愿意接受这方面的基础教育 。”

capriciousness [kə’prɪʃəsnəs]

释义 • n. sudden changes in attitude or behaviour 反复无常性，善变性，任性

词根 • capricious(反复无常的 )+ness(n .)→反复无常 ，善变

派生 • capricious adj. 反复无常的 ， 善变的 ， 任性的

capriciously adv. 善变地

caprice n. (意见或行为 ) 突然变化 ，反复无常 ；怪念

例句 • IQ could help to bridge the gap and resolve the tremendous uncertainty about how much of what we’ re seeing is natural capriciousness and how much is the consequence of human activity. (IELTS6,T1,R3) 智商可以帮助弥补鸿沟和应对巨大的不确定性 。这些不确定性包括我们所见的多少是自然的善变 ，多少是人类活动的结果 。

capsize [kæp’saɪz]

释义 • v. to overturn or be overturned (使)翻船

例句 • The invention of the container crane made it possible to load and unload containers without capsizing the ship and the adoption of standard container sizes allowed almost any box to be transported on any ship. (IELTS6,T1,R2) 集装箱起重机的发明使人们能够装载与卸载集装箱而不至于翻船 。采用标准的集装箱尺寸使其能够在任何船只上装运 。

cerebrospinal [ˌserɪbrəʊ’spaɪnəl]

释义 • adj. pertaining to or affecting the brain and the spinal cord 脑脊髓的

词根 • cerebro（脑的 ）+spine（脊柱 ）+al（形容词 ）→脑脊髓的

例句 • When he got back, he switched labs to study how cerebrospinal fluid nourishes the developing nervous system. (IELTS10,T4,R2)他回来以后 ，转而开始研究脑脊髓液如何滋养正在发育的神经系统 。

carefree [’keəfriː]

释义 • adj. free of worries and responsibilities 无忧无虑的

词根 • care(忧虑 )+free(免除的 )→免除忧虑的 →无忧无虑的

例句 • Play may look like a carefree and exuberant way to pass the time before the hard work of adulthood comes along. (IELTS4,T2,R3) 在成年阶段辛苦劳作来临之前 ，游戏可能看起来像是以无忧无虑 、充满活力的方式去度过时间的 。

carton [’kɑːtn]

释义 • n. any of various containers made from cardboard or coated paper (盛液体的)硬纸盒

例句 • Millions of people may be paying a small amount extra for their carton of orange juice. (IELTS4,T2,L4)数以百万计的人买盒装橙汁时会额外花一点钱 。

cartoon [kɑː’tuːn]

释义 • n. an amusing drawing in a newspaper or magazine, esp. one that comments satirically on current events 漫画 ；a film made by photographing a series of gradually changing drawings, giving an illusion of movement 动画片

联想 • 根据发音推出 “卡通”

派生 • cartoonist1 n. 漫画家

例句 • The making of cartoons became a separate branch of film-making, generally practiced outside the major studios, and the same was true of serials. (IELTS4,TA,R3) 漫画制作成为电影制造业的一个分支 ，一般不在大型演播厅制作 ，连续剧也是一样 。

catastrophic [ˌkætə’strɒfɪk]

词根 • cat(看做 cad落下 )+astro(星星 )+phic→落下的流星常常代表不幸 →悲惨的 ，灾难性的

派生 • catastrophe1 n. 大灾难

例句 • The writer says that global warming will not have a catastrophic impact on our future. (IELTS5,T1,R3)作者说全球变暖对我们未来的影响并不是灾难性的 。

cavern [’kævən]

派生 • cavernous adj. 像大洞穴的 ，大而幽暗的

例句 • This is where they make scenes with fishes, underground caverns and so on. (IELTS6,T2,L1) 这就是他们拍摄鱼和地下大洞穴等场景的地方 。

cavort [kə’vɔːt]

释义 • v. to have lively or boisterous fun; romp 寻欢作乐，纵欲嬉戏

例句 • Playful young animals use around two or three percent of their energy cavorting , and in children that figure can be closer to fifteen percent. (IELTS4,T3,R3) 顽皮的小动物将他们 2%到 3%的精力用于嬉戏 ，而小孩会用大约 15%的精力玩耍 。

cease [siːs]

释义 • v. to come or bring (sth.) to an end; to stop 中断，终止，停止

联想 • c+ease(安逸 ，安心 )→生于忧患 ，死于安乐 →停止 ，终止

派生 • ceaselessly adv. 无休止地

例句 • As mining ceases in one section of the open-cut, the disturbed area is reshaped. (IELTS3,TA,R3) 在一个露天开采的矿山停止开采后 ，被挖掘过的地方将被重新整理 。

cellular [’seljʊlə]

例句 • As researchers on aging noted recently, no treatment on the market today has been proved to slow human aging—the build-up of molecular and cellular damage chat increases vulnerability to infirmity as we grow older. (IELTS6,T3,R3)研究者们在最近关于衰老的研究中发现 ，现在市场上任何治疗方法都不能够减缓衰老 ——随着我们变老 ，分子和细胞的累积损坏使我们更容易虚弱 。

censor [’sensə]

派生 • censorship2 n. (对书 、电影 、信件等的 )审查

censorious adj. 好挑剔的 ，吹毛求疵的

例句 • Should films and television be censored or should we be free to choose what we see? (IELTS3,T2,S3)电影和电视节目需要经过审查还是我们可以随意选择想看的节目 ？

certify [’sɜːtɪfaɪ]

释义 • v. to formally declare (sth.), esp. in writing or on a printed document 证明，证实

词根 • certi(确实 ，确信 )+fy(使 )→证明

同义 • testify, verify

派生 • certificate14 n. 证书

certification7 n. 证明

例句 • The Council, which was founded in 1996, certifies fisheries that meet high environmental standards, enabling them to use a label that recognises their environmental responsibility. (IELTS7,T4,R2) 委员会成立于 1996年 ，它为符合高环境标准的渔业颁发证书 ，使其从业者能够使用这个标签 ，以此证明他们是对环境负责的 。

chant [tʃɑːnt]

释义 • n. words sung or shouted rhythmically and repeatedly 吟唱，有节奏的一再重复的话语 v. to sing or shout (sth.) rhythmically and repeatedly 吟唱，反复说

例句 • Such chemical communication can be compared to the human use of visual and auditory channels (as in religious chants , advertising images and jingles, political slogans and martial music) to arouse and propagate moods and attitudes. (IELTS7,T3,R1)这样的化学交流类似于人类运用视觉与听觉 (如在宗教吟唱 、广告形象和广告词 、政治标语和婚礼音乐中 )来激起情绪 ，表明态度的做法 。

chaplain [’tʃæplɪn]

释义 • n. the carbonaceous material obtained by heating wood or other organic substances in the absence of air木炭

例句 • He then tried to use fibrous material such as sawdust, charcoal or paper to stabilise the explosive, but these combustible materials tended to catch fire when placed near nitroglycerine. (IELTS10,TB,R3)他之后尝试采用纤维物质 （如锯末 、木炭或纸张 ）去稳定炸药 ，但是这些易燃物质一靠近炸药 ，就非常容易燃烧起火 。

cheat [tʃiːt]

chic [tʃiːk]

chop [tʃɒp]

释义 • v. to cut sth. into pieces with an axe, a knife, etc. 切碎(食物) ； to make sth., such as a tree, fall by cutting it at the base with a sharp tool 劈开(木头) n. a thick slice of meat, usu. including a rib 排骨，肋条肉

例句 • The stone axes used to chop down trees to make these dwellings were far superior to any that the Stone Age hunter-gatherers used. (IELTS6,T3, L4) 砍树来建造这些住所的石斧比石器时代追捕猎物的人们使用的工具要高级许多 。

chorus [’kɔːrəs]

派生 • choral1 adj. 合唱的 ，合唱队的

例句 • Notable exceptions are the heady song-like choruses of bowhead whales in summer and the complex, haunting utterances of the humpback whales. (IELTS4,T1,R3)明显的例外是夏天北极露背鲸高亢的吟唱声和驼背鲸复杂的 、萦绕于心的窃窃私语 。

cinematic [ˌsɪnɪ’mætɪk]

cipher / cypher [’saɪfə]

释义 • n. a secret writing in which a set of letters or symbols is used to represent others; code 密码 ；a person or thing of no importance 无足轻重的人

例句 • And in the mid-17th century it was common practice for mathematicians to keep their discoveries and proofs secret, by writing them in cipher , in obscure languages, or in private messages deposited in a sealed box with the Royal Society. (IELTS5,T2,R3) 17世纪中叶 ，数学家通常对他们的发现和证明保密 。他们把这些发现和证明用密码 、模糊语言写出来或者作为秘密信息保存在皇家学会的密封盒子里 。

circuit [’sɜːkɪt]

释义 • n. a regular pattern of visits or the places visited 定期前往的一系列场所 ；a complete path along which an electric current flows 电路 ；a line, route or journey round a place 环形路线

词根 • 已知 circle意为圆 ，推出 circ(圆圈 )，circ+uit→在一个圆圈走动 →环形路线

派生 • circuitous adj. 迂回的 ，绕行的 ，曲折的 ；拐弯抹角的

例句 • Both social and cognitive types of laughter tap into the same expressive machinery in our brains, the emotion and motor circuits that produce smiles and excited vocalizations. (IELTS5,T2,R2) 社会类型和认知类型的笑都刺激我们大脑中相同的表达机制 ——产生笑容和激发言语的情感和动力回路 。

circumscribe [’sɜːkəmskraɪb]

释义 • v. to draw a line round 在周围划线 ；to restrict (sth.) within limits; to confine 限制，约束

词根 • circum(周围 )+scibe(书写 )→在周围划线 →限制 ，约束

派生 • circumscription n. 在周围画的线 ；限制 ，约束

例句 • Beyond the practical need to make order out of chaos, the rise of dictionaries is associated with the rise of the English middle class, who were anxious to define and circumscribe the various worlds to conquer—lexical as well as social and commercial. (IELTS5,T1,R1) 除了使混乱的语言恢复秩序这一需要 ，字典的兴起与英国中层阶级的兴起也是相关的 。这些中层阶级人士急于界定和瓜分要征服的领域 ——不仅在社会上和商业上 ，还包括词汇上 。

civic [’sɪvɪk]

释义 • adj. of a town or city; municipal 城镇的，城市的 ；of citizens or citizenship 公民的，市民的

联想 • 与 civil一起记

例句 • What was necessary in order to fulfill a civic role? (IELTS6,T2,R3)要履行市民责任 ，什么是必须的 ？

clash [klæʃ]

释义 • n. a fight or argument between people 冲突

联想 • 想象事物相撞发出的声音

例句 • In the clash between environmentalists and developers, the Indians, whose presence is in fact crucial to the survival of the forest, have suffered the most. (IELTS3,T3,R2)在环境学家和发展学家的冲突中 ，印第安人受害最深 。而印第安人的存在实际上对森林的留存至关重要 。

cling [klɪŋ]

搭配 • cling to坚持 ，默守 ，忠于 ；粘着 ，紧贴

coachload [’kəʊtʃləʊd]

释义 • n. a group of people travelling in a coach, especially when it is full 长途汽车的全体乘客

词根 • coach(公共汽车 ，客车 )+load(担子 ，载重 )→长途汽车的全体乘客

例句 • We like to keep those tours small and personal so we don’ t take a whole coachload of people. (IELTS5,T1,L1)我们将保持旅游团的小巧规模 ，使其更加人性化 ，所以我们不载满车的人 。

coconut [’kəʊkənʌt]

释义 • n. the large, hard-shelled seed of the coconut palm, lined with a white edible meat, and containing a milky liquid 椰子

例句 • Once out there, skilled seafarers would have detected abundant leads to follow to land: seabirds, coconuts and twigs carried out to sea by the tides. (IELTS10,T3,R3)一旦航行在外 ，娴熟的水手能够发现大量的线索引领自己返回陆地 ：海鸟 、椰子树 ，还有被潮水卷入海中的树枝 。

coffer [’kɒfə]

释义 • n. a store of money; treasury; funds (常用复数)资金 ；a large strong box for holding money or other valuables; a chest 保险箱

联想 • c联想成 capital资金 ，offer指商务中的报价 →资金

例句 • But the paper and merchandising activities alone did not provide sufficient funds for the WSPU to meet organisational costs, so numerous other fundraising activities combined to fill the coffers of the war chest. (IELTS3,T4,R2) 但是仅仅靠报纸业和商业活动不能满足妇女社会政治联盟组织各种活动的开销 。因此 ，也发起许多其他筹集资金活动来填补斗争所需资金 。

词根 • cogni(知道 )+tion→认知

The Australian Institute of Sport(AIS) employs more than 100 sports scientists and doctors, and collaborates with scores of others in universities and research centres. (IELTS6,T1,R1)在学术界 ，科学占首要地位 。澳大利亚体育学院聘请 100多位体育科学家和医生 ，并与许多来自其他大学和研究中心的人员合作 。

(IELTS10,T4,R3) Cesare Lombroso是19世纪的一位意大利医生 ，很大程度上说 ，正是他使这个词染上了负面色彩 。他认为罪犯是天生的 ，而非后天的 ，并且人们可以通过他们身上某些返祖特征来加以辨别 。

释义 • n. contradicting矛盾，不一致

词根 • 已知 dictionary为词典 ，推出 diction为词 ，话语之意 。contra(反对 )+diction(言语 )→反对的话 →矛盾 ，不一致

派生 • contradict86 v. 反驳 ，否认 ；与 ……相矛盾 ，与 ……抵触

例句 • For example, during the 1968 Olympics in Mexico City, a relatively unknown high jumper named Dick Fosbury won the gold by going over the bar backwards, in complete contradiction of all the received high-jumping wisdom, a move instantly dubbed the Fosbury flop. (IELTS4,T4,R1) 例如 ，在墨西哥城举行的 1968年奥林匹克运动会中 ，一位相对不知名的跳高运动员迪克 · 福斯贝里用与传统跳高完全相反的背越式跳法赢得了金牌 。这个动作很快被称作福斯贝里跳 。

converge [kənˈvɜ:dʒ]

converse [kən’vɜːs]

词根 • con(共同 )+vers(转 )+e→别人转 ，你也转 ，但是方向相反 →相反的

例句 • Comparing measurements for fifteen orders of mammal, he and his team found larger brains (for a given body size) are linked to greater playfulness, The converse was also found to be true. (IELTS4,T2,R3) 在比较了 15种哺乳动物的测量结果后 ，他和他的团队发现大脑越大 (根据特定的身体大小 )，其玩耍能力越强 。反之亦然 。
