派生 • grimly adv. 糟糕地 ；严肃地

grimness n. 严肃 ，严厉 ；糟糕

例句 • In broad terms, it is thought that rainfall zones will shift northwards, adding to the water deficit in Africa, the Middle East and the Mediterranean—a grim prospect indeed. (IELTS6,TA,R3) 从广义上讲 ，人们认为雨水圈会向北移动 ，使得非洲 、中东和地中海的水资源更加匮乏 ——前景不容乐观 。

groan [grəʊn]

释义 • v. to make a deep sad sound when in pain, or to express despair, disapproval or distress 呻吟 ；to suffer or be oppressed by sth. 受折磨 n. a deep sound made when in pain, etc. 呻吟

联想 • 与 moan(抱怨 ，呻吟 )同记

例句 • The supposed pupil was in reality an actor hired by Milgram to simulate receiving the shocks by emitting a spectrum of groans , screams and writhings together with an assortment of statements and expletives denouncing both the experiment and the experimenter. (IELTS5,T1,R2) 所谓学生实际上是由 Milgram雇来的演员 ，他们通过发出一系列呻吟 、尖叫来模仿受到电击后的反应 ，还胡乱说话 ，骂骂咧咧 ，谴责实验与实验者 ，同时将身体不断翻滚 。

guilty [’ɡɪltɪ]

释义 • adj . suffering from or prompted by a sense of guilt 内疚的 ；being responsible for or chargeable with a reprehensible act; deserving of blame; being culpable 有罪的

派生 • guilt n. 罪行 ，过失 ；内疚 ，羞愧

例句 • Fancy Foods will pay a reward of 0,000 to 0,000 for information which leads to the conviction of any person found guilty of placing metal pieces in its products. (IELTS3,TB,R1) 如果有谁能提供线索帮助抓获把金属碎片放进他们产品的罪犯 ，Fancy Foods将对其提供 10,000到 50,000万美元的奖励 。

gush [gʌʃ]

释义 • v. to flow or pour out suddenly in great quantities 喷，涌出 ；to talk with excessive enthusiasm 滔滔不绝地讲

例句 • This prevents rainwater gushing down the walls. (IELTS7,T2,R1) 这可以避免雨水从墙壁喷涌而下 。

gust [gʌst]

释义 • n. a sudden violent rush of wind 阵风，强风

例句 • Trees filter the wind and considerably reduce it, preventing those very large strong gusts that you so often find around tall buildings. (IELTS4,T1,L4) 树木可以过滤风 ，并很大程度上降低风速 ，防止你经常在高楼周围遇到的强风的出现 。

habitual [hə’bɪtʃʊəl]

释义 • adj. regular; usual 通常的 ；done constantly or as a habit 习惯的，已养成习惯的

词根 • habit(习惯 )+ual(adj .)→习惯的

派生 • habit4 n. 习惯

例句 • No attempt was made to place a division in the programme that would best fit its habitual methods of supervision used by the manager, assistant managers, supervisors and assistant supervisors. (IELTS3,T4,R3) 公司并没有刻意去把某个部门放在整体项目中 ，这种做法让这个部门最符合经理 、经理助理 、主管和助理主管通常的管理方法 。

halve [hɑːv]

释义 • v. to divide (sth.) into two equal parts 二等分 ；to reduce (sth.) by a half 减半

派生 • half n. 一半

例句 • In Norway, after an intervention campaign was introduced nationally, an evaluation of forty-two schools suggested that, over a two-year period, bullying was halved . (IELTS6,T4,R3) 在挪威 ，干预运动投放于全国后 ，一项对 42所学校的评估表明通过 2年的时间欺凌现象减半了 。

handy [’hændɪ]

释义 • adj. convenient to handle or use; useful 方便的，手边的 ；clever with one’ s hands 手巧的

同义 • at hand, available, accessible

搭配 • come in handy 有用 ，派上用场

例句 • Coffee break’ s always the best time, cos people have got their money handy. (IELTS4,T4,L1) 喝咖啡的时间是最好的时间 ，因为人们可以把自己的钱派上用场 。

hardwired [’ha:dwaɪəd]

释义 • adj . involving or achieved by permanently connected circuits rather than software硬连线的；不可改变的

例句 • ‘It’ s very clear when you look at twins that much of what they share is hardwired ,’ she says. (IELTS11,T4, R1) 她说：“很显然，当你观察双胞胎时，就会发现他们身上有很多共有的东西是无法改变的。”

hardy [’hɑːdɪ]

释义 • adj. able to endure cold or difficult conditions; tough, robust 能吃苦耐劳的，强壮的

词根 • hard(坚韧的 )+y→能吃苦耐劳的

派生 • hardihood n. 大胆 ；刚毅 ；健壮

hardily adv. 大胆地 ，狂妄自大地

hardiness n. 强壮 ，结实 ；耐性 ；大胆

例句 • This popular half-hour science magazine continues into its twenty-ninth year, proving itself to be a hardy survivor in the television world. (IELTS5,TB,R1) 这种流行的半小时科学杂志进入其第 29个发展年头 ，证明了它在电视的重围中坚强地生存了下来 。

harmonise [’hɑːmənaɪz]

释义 • v. to be or make (sth.) harmonious (使)协调，使一致，融洽

词根 • harmo(结合 )+nise(动词 )→结合在一起 →使一致

派生 • harmony1 n. 和谐 ，协调

harmonious adj. 和谐的 ，协调的

disharmony n. 不和谐

例句 • This would also involve harmonising activities in individual countries as well as identifying a number of priority research topics relating to the protection of forests. (IELTS7,T3,R3) 这包括协调各个国家的活动 ，同时确定一些与保护森林有关的最重要的研究话题 。

harridan [’hærɪdən]

释义 • n. a bad-tempered old woman 衰老而脾气坏的女人，恶妇，丑婆

例句 • The programme begins with a short film devised by the antis—those opposed to women having the vote—depicting a suffragette as a fierce harridan bullying her poor, abused husband. (IELTS3,T4,R2) 这个节目以反对党 —— 也就是那些反对妇女拥有选举权的人们 —— 设计的一个短片为开端 ， 短片中参政妇女被描绘成虐待自己可怜的丈夫的恶妇 。

hasten [’heɪsən]

释义 • v. to cause (sth.) to be done or to happen earlier 催促，加快

词根 • haste(快 ，匆忙 )+en(使 ……)→使加快

派生 • hasty adj. 匆忙的

例句 • It can actually hasten death, as it did in December 1991 when a cloud of exhaust fumes lingered over the city of London for over a week. (IELTS3,T4,R1) 实际上它会加速死亡 。1991年 12月 ，在伦敦上空停留了一周的一团废气验证了这点 。

haunting [’hɔːntɪŋ]

释义 • adj. continually recurring to the mind; unforgettable 难以忘怀的，萦绕的

派生 • haunt n. 常去的地方 v. (鬼魂等 )常出没于 ……；(思想 、回忆等 )萦绕在心头 ，缠绕

例句 • Notable exceptions are the heady song-like choruses of bowhead whales in summer and the complex, haunting utterances of the humpback whales. (IELTS4,T1,R3) 明显的例外是北极露背鲸在夏天高亢的吟唱和驼背鲸复杂的 、萦绕于心的窃窃私语 。

havoc [’hævək]

释义 • n. widespread destruction; devastation 大破坏，大毁坏

搭配 • play havoc with/ wreak havoc with 造成洗劫 /大破坏

例句 • The havoc that the ‘ treadmill syndrome’ can bring about is well illustrated by what happened to cotton farmers in Central America. (IELTS8,T4,R2) “枯燥工作综合征”能够带来危害 ，中美洲的棉农就是最好的例子 。

headline [’hedlaɪn]

释义 • n. the title or caption of a newspaper article, usually set in large type 大字标题 ；[pl.] an important or sensational piece of news 头版头条新闻

联想 • head(头部 )+line(行 )→写在文章第一行的内容 →大字标题

例句 • What sort of national events make headlines in your country? (IELTS3,T3,S3)在贵国 ，什么类型的国内事件会成为头条新闻呢 ？

headquarters [’hedˌkwɔːtəz]

释义 • n. a center of operations or administration 总部，总店 ；the offices of a commander, as of a military unit, from which orders are issued 指挥部

词根 • head(头 )+quarters(部分 )→总部 ，总店

例句 • By 1906 the WSPU headquarters, called the Women’ s Press Shop, had been established in Chafing Cross Road and in spite of limited communications (no radio or television, and minimal use of the telephone) the message had spread around the country, with members and branch officers stretching to as far away as Scotland. (IELTS3,T4,R2) 到 1906年 ，WSPU在 Chafing Cross路建立了总部 ，命名为 “妇女印刷社”。尽管通讯有限 ，没有收音机 、电视 ，也极少有电话 ，但消息传遍全国 ，WSPU的会员和分支机构已远达苏格兰 。

heady [’hedɪ]

释义 • adj. likely to make people drunk quickly; potent 易使人醉的，烈性的 ；having a quick effect on the senses; very exciting 使人兴奋的

例句 • Notable exceptions are the heady song-like choruses of bowhead whales in summer and the complex, haunting utterances of the humpback whales. (IELTS4,T1,R3) 明显的例外是北极露背鲸在夏天高亢的吟唱和驼背鲸复杂的 、萦绕于心的窃窃私语 。

hedge [hedʒ]

释义 • n . a fence or boundary formed by closely growing bushes or shrubs树篱；保护手段

同义 • fence, safeguard, shield, buffer

例句 • The maze is made out of hedges which are too tall for young children to see over them. (IELTS11,T1, L2) 迷宫用树篱建造，树篱很高，挡住了小孩们的视线。

heaven [’hevən]

释义 • n. a place believed to be the home of God and the angels and of good people after death 天堂，天国 ；the sky, as seen from the earth 苍天

例句 • Water, which was once regarded as a free gift from heaven , is becoming a commodity which must be bought and sold on the open market just like oil. (IELTS6,TA,R3) 水曾经被看作是上天给人类的免费礼物 ，现在却变成了一种商品 ，像油一样在开放市场中买卖 。

hiccup [’hɪkʌp]

释义 • n. a small problem or temporary delay 暂时性的小问题；短暂的停顿 ；a sharp, usually repeated, sound made in the throat, that is caused by a sudden movement of the diaphragm and that you cannot control打嗝

例句 • But if play is not simply a developmental hiccup , as biologists once thought, why did it evolve? (IELTS4,T2,R3) 但是 ，如果像生物学家曾经认为的那样 ，玩耍不是简单的发育暂停 ，那么它为什么会演变呢 ？

hierarchy [’haɪrɑːkɪ]

释义 • n. a body of persons having authority 领导层 ；a system with grades of authority or status from the lowest to the highest 层次，等级

词根 • hier(神圣 )+archy(统治 )→统治 →领导层

派生 • hierarchical1 adj. 等级的 ，层次的

hierarchically8 adv. 等级地 ，层次地

例句 • Other uniforms denoted a hierarchy —chefs wore white because they worked with flour, but the main chef wore a black hat to show he supervised. (IELTS3,TB,R3) 其他制服体现等级 ——厨师穿白色衣服 ，因为他们和面粉打交道 ，主厨戴黑色的帽子来显示他们的主管地位 。

hiker [’haɪkə]

释义 • n. a person who hikes 徒步旅行者

联想 • 穿着耐克 (Nike)运动鞋的人 (er)去徒步旅行 (hike)了

派生 • hike v. 徒步旅行 ；提高 (价格等 ) n. 猛增

例句 • Packed full of information for the avid hiker , this book is a must. (IELTS5,TA,R1) 这本书涵盖了狂热的徒步旅行者需要的信息 ，是他们的必备之物 。

hindquarters [’haɪndˌkwɔːtəz]

释义 • n. the back part of an animal with four legs 后腿；后半部

词根 • hind(后面 )+quarters(部分 )→后腿 ，后半部

例句 • And one ostrich produces a lot of meat—from around 30 to 50 kg, mostly from the hindquarters of the bird. (IELTS3,T3,L4) 一只鸵鸟能提供大量的肉 ——约从 30千克到 50千克不等 ，主要从鸵鸟的后腿上获得 。

hindrance [’hɪndrəns]

释义 • n. a thing or person that hinders 障碍物；障碍，妨碍

同义 • barrier, obstruction, impediment

派生 • hinder v. 阻碍 ，妨碍

例句 • Associating a number as one of the qualities of a specific object is a great hindrance to the development of a true number sense. (IELTS6,T2,R3) 将数字与某个特定物体的性质联系在一起是建立真正的数字意识的严重障碍 。

homogenous [hə’mɒdʒɪnəs]

释义 • adj. formed of parts that are all of the same type 同种类的

词根 • homo(同类的 )+gene(基因 )+ous→同种类的

派生 • homogeneity1 n. 同种 ，同质

例句 • The last 30 years, however, have seen an increasing emphasis on their role in projecting the image of an organisation and in uniting the workforce into a homogeneous unit—particularly in customer facing industries, and especially in financial services and retailing. (IELTS3,TB,R3) 然而 ，在过去 30年中 ，制服在表现公司形象和团结员工并使之成为一个同质的整体这两方面的作用增强了 ——尤其是在面对顾客的行业中 ，如金融服务业和零售业 。

honoraria [ɒnə’rærɪə]

释义 • n. a voluntary payment made for professional services for which a fee is not normally paid or required by law 谢礼

例句 • And she also has a few ,000 honoraria to offer in exchange for doctors’ attendance at her company’ s next educational lecture. (IELTS6,T4,R1) 为了医生们来参加公司的下一次教育报告 ，她准备了几份价值 1，000美金的谢礼 。

hormonal [hɔː’məʊnəl]

释义 • adj. of a hormone or hormones 荷尔蒙的，激素的；内分泌的

派生 • hormone14 n. 荷尔蒙 ，激素 ；内分泌

例句 • One theory for the age-related change is that it is due to hormonal changes. (IELTS5,TA,R3) 与年龄相关的变化的一种理论是将衰老归因于内分泌的变化 。

hospitality [ˌhɒspɪ’tælɪtɪ]

释义 • n. friendly and generous reception and entertainment of guests or strangers, esp. in one’ s own home 好客，盛情，招待礼节

词根 • hospi(客人 )+tal+ity→好客 ，盛情

派生 • hospitable adj. 好客的 ，殷勤的 ，招待周到的

例句 • Hospitality and Kitchen Staff (IELTS6,TB,R1)好客与厨房人员

hostile [’hɒstaɪl]

释义 • adj. showing strong dislike or enmity; very unfriendly 不友好的，敌对的，怀有敌意的

联想 • host(主人 )+ile→主人设下鸿门宴 →不友好的

派生 • hostility1 n. 敌意 ，敌对 ；[pl.]战斗 ，战争行动

例句 • To casual observers, as well as to influential natural scientists and regional planners, the luxuriant forests of Amazonia seem ageless, unconquerable, a habitat totally hostile to human civilization. (IELTS3,T3,R2) 对于普通的观察者 、著名的自然科学家和区域规划者来说 ，亚马逊茂盛的森林似乎永远那么年轻 、不可征服 ，是一块完全不受人类文明影响的自然环境 。

hover [’hɒvə]

释义 • v. to remain in the air in one place 飞翔，盘旋 ；to wait in a timid and uncertain manner 徘徊

派生 • hovercraft2 n. 气垫船

例句 • The main purpose is to show how hovercrafts work, and how things hover around on just a cushion of air. (IELTS4,T4,L3) 主要目的是展示飞翔机是怎样工作的 ，以及物体是怎样在气垫上飞翔 。

hunch [hʌntʃ]

释义 • n. idea based on intuition or instinct and not on evidence 基于直觉的想法，直觉，预感

例句 • On a hunch , he started gradually moving the feeding dish further and further away and noticed as he did so, that the dances of the returning scout bees also started changing. (IELTS4,TB,R3) 凭直觉 ，他开始逐步将喂养盘放得越来越远 ，而后他发现 ，回来的侦察蜂的舞蹈也开始改变 。

hurdle [’ˈhɜ:dl]

释义 • n. a portable barrier over which contestants must leap in certain running races, usually a wooden frame with a hinged inner frame that swings down under impact to prevent injury to a runner who does not clear it 障碍，困难

例句 • Getting invited to an interview means you have passed the first hurdle —your application must have made a good impression. (IELTS10,TB,R2) 被通知去参加一场面试 ，即意味着你已经通过了第一关 ——你的求职申请必定令人印象深刻 。

hydropower [’haɪdrəʊpaʊə]

释义 • n. hydroelectric power 水力发电，水电站

词根 • hydro(水 )+power(力 )→水力发电

例句 • Unprecedented construction of tens of thousands of monumental engineering projects designed to control floods, protect clean water supplies, and provide water for irrigation and hydropower brought great benefits to hundreds of millions of people. (IELTS7,T1,R2) 为了控制洪水 、保护干净的水供应 、提供灌溉用水和发电用水 ，成千上万史无前例的巨型工程项目被开发 ，它们给千千万万的人带来了利益 。

hype [haɪp]

释义 • n. misleading and exaggerated publicity 天花乱坠的宣传报道 v. to publicize sth. in a wildly exaggerated way 言过其实的宣传

例句 • And it is not always hype . (IELTS5,T3,R3) 这并不一定都是天花乱坠的宣传报道 。

hypnotic [hɪp’nɒtɪk]

释义 • adj. of or producing hypnosis or a similar condition 催眠术的，安眠的

词根 • hypno(睡眠 )+tic(……的 )→催眠的

派生 • hypnotism n. 催眠术

hypnosis5 n. 催眠

例句 • But it is worth trying, for to understand the initial shock of those images is to understand the extraordinary power and magic of cinema, the unique, hypnotic quality that has made film the most dynamic, effective art form of the 20th century. (IELTS6,T3,R1) 但是这值得我们去试一试 ，因为要了解这些图像带来的冲击 ，就等于了解电影非凡的力量和魔力 ，正是这种独特的 、令人眩晕的品质使电影成为 20世纪最具活力 、最为有效的艺术形式 。

hypothetical [ˌhaɪpə’θetɪkəl]

释义 • adj. of, relating to, or based on a hypothesis 假设的，假定的

词根 • hypo(在 ……下面 )+thesis(论点 )→thetical→非真实论点的 →假设的 ，假定的

派生 • hypothesis18 (pl. hypotheses4 ) n. 假设 ，假定 ，假说

hypothetic1 adj. 假设的 ，假定的

例句 • Second, it lacked the grammatical resources required to represent the world in an objective and impersonal way, and to discuss the relations, such as cause and effect, that might hold between complex and hypothetical entities. (IELTS5,T2,R3) 第二 ，它缺乏一种客观的 、非个人的方式描述世界的语法结构功能 ，因此在讨论复杂和假设的实体之间的关系时 ，例如因果关系 ，显得不足 。

iconic [aɪ’kɒnɪk]

释义 • adj. of, relating to, or characteristic of an icon 图标的；符号的

派生 • icon n . 图标 ，符号

例句 • We offer three different tours of this iconic building. (IELTS10,TA,R1)对于这栋地标性的建筑 ，我们提供了三种不同的旅游路线 。

idiom [’ɪdɪəm]

释义 • n. a speech form or an expression of a given language that is peculiar to itself grammatically or cannot be understood from the individual meanings of its elements, as in keep tabs on惯用语，成语，习语

同义 • tongue, language, expression

例句 • Another difference from conventional teaching is the evidence that students can regularly learn 1000 new words of a foreign language during a suggestopedic session, as well as grammar and idiom . (IELTS7,T1,R3) 与传统教学相比 ，另外一个不同点就是学生可以在一个暗示法学习期间学会 1000个外语单词以及语法和习语 。

idiosyncratic [ˌɪdɪəsɪn’krætɪk]

释义 • adj. a person’ s particular way of thinking, behaving, etc. that is clearly different from that of others 独特的，怪癖的

派生 • idiosyncracy n. (个人特有的 )习性 ，癖好

例句 • I decided to test whether various lines of motion were apt ways of showing movement or if they were merely idiosyncratic marks. (IELTS4,T1,R3) 我决定测试各种运动线条是适合展示各种动作 ，还是它们只是风格独特的符号 。

idyllic [ɪ’dɪlɪk]

释义 • adj. of or having the nature of an idyll 田园风光的，质朴宜人的

例句 • They investigated chic so-called boutique hotels in the heart of downtown business districts, stately mansions located in the depths of beautiful countryside, and plush hotels built at the edge of tropical beaches surrounded by palm trees and idyllic blue ocean. (IELTS7,T3,L4) 他们调查那些设在城镇商业中心的所谓的华丽的宾馆 ， 那些坐落于风景优美的郊区的高档 别墅 ，还有那些建在热带海边被棕榈树和蓝色海水环绕的豪华酒店 。

illusion [ɪ’luːʒən]

释义 • n. false idea, belief or impression; delusion 幻觉，幻想；错误的信仰或观念

词根 • il(against)+lus(玩耍 )+ion→(错认为可以 )玩弄某人 →错觉

搭配 • cherish/habor an illusion存有幻想

create/produce an illusion 产生幻想

dispel an illusion 消除幻想

同义 • vision, delusion, fantasy, misconception

派生 • illusive adj. 幻影的 ，错觉的 ；迷惑人的 ，虚假的 ，不牢靠的

例句 • the end of an illusion (IELTS4,T4,R3) 幻想的终结

imitation [ˌɪmɪ’teɪʃən]

释义 • n. imitating 模仿，仿制 ；the thing produced as a copy of the real thing 仿制品，赝品

同义 • copy, simulation, duplication, reproduction

派生 • imitate2 v. 仿效 ，模仿 ；仿造 ，伪造

imitator n. 模仿者 ，伪造者

imitative adj. 模仿的 ，伪造的

搭配 • by imitation 通过模仿 ，模仿地

in imitation of … 仿效

例句 • This could have been an imitation of earlier vessels. (IELTS6,T3,L4) 这可能是早期船只的一种仿制品 。

immerse [i’mə:s]

释义 • v . to dip or submerge in a liquid 浸，泡

词根 • im(in)+merse (沉 ) →沉在里面 →浸没

搭配 • immerse oneself in … =be immersed in … 专心于

派生 • immersion n. 沉浸 ，浸没

例句 • As a student at the City of London School, Perkin became immersed in the study of chemistry. (IELTS9,T1,R1) 作为伦敦城市学校的一名学生 ，珀金沉浸于化学学习之中 。

immigration [ˌɪmɪ’greɪʃən]

释义 • n. moving of people from one country to come to live in another country permanently 移居；外来的移民，移民总称

词根 • im(在 ……内 )+migr(迁移 )+ation(n .)→外面迁徙而来的人 →移民

派生 • immigrate v. 移民

immigrant3 n. 移民 ，侨民

例句 • Information sessions: including such topics as accommodation, health, religious matters, welfare, immigration , study skills, careers and other essential information. (IELTS5,TB,R2) 信息板块包括诸如食宿 、健康 、宗教 、福利 、移民 、学习技巧 、职业以及其他的生活必要信息 。

immobile [ɪ’məʊbɑɪl]

释义 • adj. unable to move or be moved 固定的，不动的，不能动的

词根 • im(否定 )+mobile(移动的 )→不能移动的

派生 • immobility n. 不能移动性

例句 • When pain strikes, we attempt to keep the back as immobile as possible, which makes the muscles tense up. (IELTS3,T1,L4) 当疼痛发作时 ，我们会努力保持背部不动 ，这使得肌肉紧张起来 。

impartial [ɪm’pɑːʃəl]

释义 • adj. not favouring one person or thing more than another; fair or neutral 公平的，不偏不倚的

词根 • im(否定 )+partial(偏袒一方的 )→不偏袒的

派生 • impartiality n. 公正 ，公正性

例句 • Yet a green organisation opposing such a weakening is seen as altruistic, even if an impartial view of the controls in question might suggest they are doing more harm than good. (IELTS5,T1,R3) 但是 ，绿色环保组织反驳弱化污染控制的观点被看成是利他主义 ，即使对问题公正的分析可能会发现他们的行为是弊大于利的 。

impede [ɪm’pi:d]

释义 • vt. to delay or prevent (someone or something) by obstructing them; to hinder 妨碍，阻碍，阻止

词根 • im(into)+pede (脚 )→放进一只脚 →妨碍

同义 • obstruct, block

派生 • impediment n. 妨碍 ，障碍物

例句 • This is where most people are impeded from being an iconoclast. (IELTS9,T2,R3) 这就是为什么大多数人没能成为标新立异者的原因 。

imperative [ɪm’perətɪv]

释义 • adj. absolutely necessary or required; unavoidable 必要的，不可避免的

同义 • compulsory, critical, crucial, essential, indispensable, obligatory, urgent, vital

例句 • However, a new imperative —sustainable development—offers an opportunity for adapting the EU’ s common transport policy. (IELTS10,T1,R2)然而 ，可持续发展这个新要求为调整欧盟的通用交通运输政策提供了契机 。

impetus [’ɪmpɪtəs]

释义 • n. a thing that encourages a process to develop more quickly 动力，推力

词根 • im(on)+pet(寻求 )+us→为寻求而激起的动力 →推动

搭配 • gain (an) impetus to do sth.获得做某事的动力

under sb’ s impetus 在某人的推动下

例句 • The impetus behind the development of these early plastics was generated by a number of factors. (IELTS5,T2,R1)早期塑料的发展背后的动力是由很多因素构成的 。

impinge [ɪm’pɪndʒ]

释义 • v. to have an effect on sth. 对……产生作用，影响

词根 • im(into)+pinge(撞击 )→撞击某物 →影响

同义 • influence, affect

例句 • They can turn down applications from scientists they believe will work against their interests, or research projects that will impinge too much on their daily lives and traditional activities. (IELTS6,T1,R3) 他们不理会那些他们认为与自身利益背道而驰的科学家们的研究申请 ，也拒绝那些对他们的日常生活和传统活动产生过多影响的研究项目 。

implementation [ˌɪmplɪmen’teɪʃən]

释义 • n. putting (sth.) into effect; carrying out 实施，运用

词根 • im(使 ……)+ple(满 )+ment+ation→使圆满 ，使生效 →实施

派生 • implement11 v. 使生效 ，实施

例句 • In Dr Leake’ s opinion, the reputation of AI suffered as a result of premature implementation . (IELTS5,T3,R3) 从 Leake博士的观点来看 ，因为不成熟的运用 ，人工智能的名声受损 。

implicate [’ɪmplɪkeɪt]

释义 • v. to show that sb. is involved in sth., esp. a crime 使牵连其中，涉嫌，涉及 ；to have as a consequence or an inference; imply 暗示

词根 • im(in)+plic(折 )+ate(v .)→折在里面 →暗含在里面 →暗示

派生 • implication13 n. 暗示 ，暗指 ，言外之意 ；牵连

例句 • PM10, a sub-category of particulate matter measuring ten-millionths of a metre across, has been implicated in thousands of deaths a year in Britain alone. (IELTS3,T4,R1) 千万分之一米长的 PM10是一种颗粒物质 ，仅在英国一年就会引起几千人的死亡事件 。

implicit [ɪm’plɪsɪt]

释义 • adj. implied,unquestioning or unreserved; absolute 不言明的；无疑问的，绝对的

词根 • im(里面 )+plicit(折叠 )→向里折叠 →不直接表达 →不言明的 ，含蓄的

同义 • implied, latent, tacit, unspoken

例句 • But despite an implicit recognition that the spread of good reproductions can be culturally valuable, museums continue to promote the special status of original work. (IELTS10,T2,R3)虽然有一个不言而喻的认识 ，即高质量仿品的传播有重要的文化意义 ，但是博物馆继续推崇原始作品的特殊地位 。

importation [ˌɪmpɔː’teɪʃən]

释义 • n. the act or business of importing 进口，输入

词根 • im(in)+port(运送 )+ation(n .)→运送进来 →进口 ，输入

派生 • import15 v. 引进 ，进口 n. 进口 ，输入 ；(pl.)进口商品

importer n. 从事进口的公司或人

例句 • Since the seventeenth century, with the advent of trading companies exporting manufactured textiles to North America and Asia, the importation of cheap goods has often contributed to the destruction of local skills and indigenous markets. (IELTS3,T3,R1) 自 17世纪以来 ，随着贸易公司将机械制造的纺织品出口到北美以及亚洲 ，廉价商品的进口便对本土技术和本土市场造成了冲击 。

impoverished [ɪm’pɒvərɪʃt]

释义 • adj. reduced to poverty; poverty-stricken 贫困的，赤贫的

词根 • im(in)+pover(贫困 )+ish(使 )+ed(adj .)→贫困的

派生 • impoverish v. 使穷困

impoverishment n. 贫困

例句 • There is a need to recognise the importance of access to credit for impoverished young people seeking to fulfil economic needs. (IELTS4,T3,R1) 有必要认识到信贷机会对那些试图满足经济需求的贫困年轻人的重要性 。

improvise [’ɪmprəvaɪz]

释义 • v. to compose or play (music), speak or act without previous preparation (即兴、即席地)创作(演奏、讲话)

词根 • im(not)+pro(前 )+vise(看 )→没有提前看过 →即兴发挥

例句 • The students do not focus their attention on trying to remember the vocabulary, but focus on using the language to communicate (e.g. through games or improvised dramatisations). (IELTS7,T1,R3) 学生们没有把注意力放在记忆单词上 ，而是放在用语言进行交流上 (比如通过游戏或者即兴创作的剧本等方式 )。

inaccessible [ˌɪnək’sesəbəl]

释义 • adj. very difficult or impossible to reach, approach, or be contacted (by sb.); not accessible 达不到的，难得到的；不可进入的，不易接近的

词根 • in(not)+accessible(可得到的 )→达不到的

例句 • Prior to the start of MIRTP the Makete district was almost inaccessible during the rainy season. (IELTS7,T2,R3) 在 MIRTP开始之前 ，Makete地区在雨季几乎不能进入 。

inaccurate [ɪn’ækjərɪt]

释义 • adj. having errors; not correct or accurate 不准确的

词根 • in(not)+accurate(准确的 )→不准确的

例句 • Radar is an inaccurate term when referring to bats. (IELTS7,T1,R1) 当提到蝙蝠时 ，雷达是个不准确的术语 。

inaugurate [ɪ’nɔːɡjʊreɪt]

释义 • v. to introduce a new public official or leader at a special ceremony为……举行就职典礼； to officially open a building or start an organization with a special ceremony 为……举行仪式，为……举行落成(开幕)仪式； to introduce a new development or an important change 开创，创始

词根 • in(in)+augurate(预兆 ，预示 )→预示 ……的来临 →为 ……举行就职典礼

派生 • inauguration n. 就职仪式

inaugural adj. 就职的 ，就任的 ；开幕的 ，创始的

例句 • In 1665 a new scientific journal, Philosophical Transactions, was inaugurated . (IELTS5,T2,R3) 1665年 ，一本新的科学期刊 《哲学会报 》正式出版了 。

incapacitated [ˌɪnkə’pæsɪteɪtɪd]

释义 • v. to make sb. unable (to do sth.); to weaken or disable sb. 使无能力，使失去能力

词根 • in(not)+capacitate(具有能力 )→使失去能力

派生 • incapable adj. 无能力的 ，不能胜任的

例句 • The most recent available figures show that about a quarter of a million people are incapacitated with back pain every day. (IELTS3,T1,L4) 最新得到的数据表明 ，约 25万人对背痛无能为力 。

incineration [ɪnˌsɪnə’reɪʃən]

释义 • n. destroy (sth.) completely by burning; burn to ashes 焚化，火化，焚烧

词根 • in(in)+ciner(灰 )+ation(n .)→焚烧

派生 • incinerate v. 焚化 ，火化

例句 • The production of recycled glass and paper uses much less energy than producing them from virgin materials, and also recycling reduces greenhouse gas emissions from landfill sites and incineration plants. (IELTS5,T3,L4)对玻璃和纸张的循环利用比用原材料来生产这些东西耗费较少的能量 ，同时循环利用还减少了温室气体的排放 。

inclination [ˌɪnklə’neɪʃən]

释义 • n. the degree of sloping; slant 倾斜，点头 ；bending or bowing movement 弯腰 ； a tendency to do sth. 趋向，趋势，倾向 ；a feeling that makes sb. want to behave in a particular way; disposition 爱好，癖好

词根 • in(towards)+clin(e)(倾斜 )+ation→倾向

派生 • incline v. 使倾斜 ，使倾向

例句 • One’ s first inclination might be to argue that there must be some sort of built-in animal aggression instinct that was activated by the experiment. (IELTS5,T1,R2) 一开始 ，大家可能都倾向于认为这个实验激发了动物内在的富于攻击性的天性 。

incompatible [ˌɪnkəm’pætəbəl]

释义 • adj. not able to live or work happily with sb. 合不来的，不能和睦相处的 ；not consistent or in logical agreement with sth. 不相符的，不相配的，不相容的

词根 • in(否定 )+compatible(相容的 )→不相容的

派生 • incompatibility n. 不兼容性

例句 • While two fifths of the students provided the information that the rain forests provide oxygen, in some cases this response also embraced the misconception that rainforest destruction would reduce atmospheric oxygen, making the atmosphere incompatible with human life on Earth. (IELTS4,T1,R2) 虽然有五分之二的学生认为热带雨林能给人类提供氧气 ，但是在某些情况下 ，这种反应也导致了人们的误解 ，即认为热带雨林的破坏会减少大气中的氧气 ，从而使得大气不适合地球上人类的生活 。

incongruous [ɪn’kɒŋgrʊəs]

释义 • adj. strange because not in harmony with the surrounding features; out of place 不合适的，不相称的，不协调的，不一致的

派生 • incongruity1 n. 不合适 ，不相称 ，不协调

incongruously adv. 不合适地 ，不协调地

例句 • If participation and the culture are incongruous , employees are likely to perceive the participation process as manipulative and be negatively affected by it. (IELTS6,T3,R2) 如果职工参与性与企业文化不相容 ，职员们就会把参与过程看成是被人操纵的 ，并由此产生负面影响 。

incredible [ɪn’kredəbəl]

释义 • adj. difficult to believe; amazing or fantastic 难以置信的，不可思议的

词根 • in(not)+credible(可信的 )→不可思议的

派生 • incredibly2 adv. 非常地 ，极端地 ，异乎寻常地 ，难以置信地

例句 • Looking back, it now seems quite incredible that in the national health systems that emerged in many countries in the years immediately after the 1939-45 World War, it was assumed without question that all the basic health needs of any community could be satisfied, at least in principle. (IELTS4,T4,R3) 回顾过去 ，1939至 1945年二战后 ，在许多国家建立的国家健康体制里 ，人们居然认为所有的基本健康需求至少在理论上是都可以得到满足的 ，这种观点现在看来多么不可思议 。

increment [’ɪnkrəmənt]

释义 • n. increase, esp. in money paid as a salary; added amount 增加物，增长物；增值

派生 • incremental adj. 增加的

例句 • Billing increments are in 30-second units. (IELTS7,TB,R1) 收费是以 30秒为单位的 。

indiscriminate [ˌɪndɪ’skrɪmənɪt]

释义 • adj. acting without careful judgement 不加区别的，不加选择的，不加鉴别的，不分好坏的

例句 • In the face of the escalating perils from indiscriminate applications of pesticides, a more effective and ecologically sound strategy of biological control is fast gaining popularity. (IELTS8,T4,R2) 面对滥用杀虫剂而产生的不断升级的危险 ，一种有效并对生态有益的生物控制策略很快流行起来 。

inedible [ɪn’edəbəl]

释义 • adj. not suitable to be eaten 不可食用的

词根 • in(not)+ed(=eat)+ible(能 ……的 )→不可食用的

派生 • inedibility n. 不适于食用

例句 • Without the beetles to dispose of the dung, cow pats would litter pastures making grass inedible to cattle and depriving the soil of sunlight. (IELTS3,T2,R1) 没有甲虫来处理粪便 ，牛粪堆就会堆满草场 ，使牛无法吃到草 ，也使土壤得不到阳光的照射 。

infancy [’ɪnfənsɪ]

释义 • n. the state or period of being an infant; early childhood 幼年期，孩提时期 ；the early stage of development or growth 初期

派生 • infant14 n. 婴儿 ，幼儿

例句 • The women were asked how many children they had given birth to and how many of them had died in infancy . (IELTS6,T4,R2) 这些女性被问到她们生了几个孩子 ，以及有几个孩子在婴儿期夭折了 。

infect [ɪn’fekt]

释义 • v. to cause sb./sth. to have a disease; contaminate sb./sth. 传染，感染 ；to fill (sb ’ s mind) with undesirable ideas 使受影响

词根 • in(in)+fect(做 )→做进去 →传染 ，感染

搭配 • be infected with感染上

同义 • contaminate, communicate, affect, catch, get, influence

派生 • infection9 n. 传染

infectious adj. 传染的

例句 • Despite your best efforts, unsolicited email or spam can clutter up the most organised inbox and infect your computer system with viruses. (IELTS7,TB,R2) 尽管你努力抵制 ，不请自来的电邮或垃圾邮件可能会堆满你井井有条的收件箱 ，并且通过病毒感染你的电脑系统 。

infirmity [ɪn’fɜːmətɪ]

释义 • n. a bodily ailment or weakness, especially one brought on by old age 体弱，虚弱，衰弱

词根 • in(not)+firm(坚定的 )+ity→不坚定 →衰弱

派生 • infirm adj. 体弱的 ，虚弱的 ，意志薄弱的

例句 • As researchers on aging noted recently, no treatment on the market today has been proved to slow human aging—the build-up of molecular and cellular damage chat increases vulnerability to infirmity as we grow older. (IELTS6,T3,R3) 正如研究人类衰老问题的研究者最近所指出的那样 ，目前市场上任何治疗都不能延缓人的衰老 ，这是因为随着年龄的增长 ，身体内的分子和细胞逐渐损坏 ，从而使我们更容易虚弱无力 。

inflation [ɪn’fleɪʃən]

释义 • n. a persistent increase in the level of consumer prices or a persistent decline in the purchasing power of money, caused by an increase in available currency and credit beyond the proportion of available goods and services 通货膨胀

词根 • in(进入 )+flation(膨胀 )→通货膨胀

派生 • inflate v. 通货膨胀

反义 • deflate v. 通货紧缩

例句 • In 1965, for instance, Japan used approximately 13 million gallons of water to produce million of commercial output; by 1989 this had dropped to 3.5 million gallons (even accounting for inflation )—almost a quadrupling of water productivity. (IELTS7,T1,R2) 例如在 1965年 ，日本使用 1300万加仑的水来生产 100万美元的商业产品 ；到 1989年 ，生产 100万美元的商业产品用水降到了 350万加仑 (即便考虑到通货膨胀 )——几乎使水的生产力翻了两番 。

inflict [ɪn’flɪkt]

释义 • v. to afflict 予以(打击) ；to cause (a blow, penalty, etc.) to be suffered (by sb.) 使遭受，强加于；施刑，处罚

词根 • in(on)+flict(打击 )→在 ……上打击 →施加打击

搭配 • inflict … on 使遭受 ，把 ……强加于

inflict oneself on sb. 打扰某人

派生 • infliction n. 施加 (痛苦 、损失 、惩罚等 )

例句 • Their electrical fury inflicts death or serious injury on around 500 people each year in the United States alone. (IELTS8,T3,R1) 仅仅在美国 ，每年有大约 500人因受到电击而死亡或严重受伤 。

influenza [ˌɪnflʊ’enzə]

释义 • n. infectious virus disease causing fever, muscular pain and catarrh 流行性感冒 (flu)

例句 • In 1990, smoking caused more than 84,000 deaths, mainly resulting from such problems as pneumonia, bronchitis and influenza . (IELTS3,T1,R2) 1990年 ，吸烟导致了 84000多人死亡 ，其中主要是由肺炎 、支气管炎及流行性感冒等疾病引发的 。

inhale [ɪn’heɪl]

释义 • v. to breathe sth. in吸入，吸气

词根 • in(in)+hale(呼吸 )→吸入

派生 • inhalation1 n. 吸入 ，吸入物

反义 • exhale v. 呼出

例句 • There is a philosophical question as to whether people should have to inhale others’ smoke. (IELTS3,T1,R2) 关于人们是不是非得吸入二手烟涉及到一个哲学上的问题 。

innate [ɪ’neɪt]

释义 • adj. in one’ s nature; possessed from birth 天生的，固有的

例句 • A number of pests are now born with an innate immunity to some pesticides. (IELTS8,T4,R2) 现在 ，许多害虫从出生开始就对杀虫剂有内在的免疫力 。

innocent [’ɪnəsənt]

释义 • adj. knowing nothing of evil or wrong 天真的，幼稚的 ；not guilty (of wrongdoing) 清白的

词根 • in(否 ，不 )+noc(伤害 )+ent(……的 )→不曾受过伤的心灵 →天真的

派生 • innocence n. 天真 ，清白 ，单纯 ，简单

例句 • It’ s not just a matter of companies making bigger profits than they should do, but of events which may affect the lives of innocent people. (IELTS4,T2,L4) 这不仅仅是公司赚取了更多利润的问题 ，而是它可能影响很多无辜的人的生活 。

instalment [ɪn’stɔːlmənt]

释义 • n. any one of the parts of a payment spread over a period of time 分期付款 ；any one of the separate but connected parts in which a story is presented over a period of time (连载或连播的)一集

搭配 • in/by instalments 以分期付款的方式

例句 • He was to be paid ￡1,575 in instalments . (IELTS5,T1,R1) 他将以分期付款的方式收到总计 1575英镑 。

intent [ɪn’tent]

释义 • n. intention; purpose 意图 adj. full of eager interest and concentration 专注的，集中的；急切的

联想 • in(towards)+tent(帐篷 )→深夜摸进帐篷 ，意图不纯

搭配 • to all intents and purposes在任何一方面 ；实际上

例句 • It contains no glass and is therefore unbreakable to all intents and purposes. (IELTS3,T4,L2) 它不含玻璃 ，因此无论出于何种意图和目的都是打不破的 。

interchangeable [ˌɪntə’tʃeɪndʒəbəl]

释义 • adj. things that are interchangeable can be used instead of each other 可以互相交换的

词根 • inter(相互 )+change+able→可以互相交换的

派生 • interchangeability n. 可以相互交换性

例句 • By the seventh century, the word teon had become interchangeable with the tachund or hund of the Anglo-Saxon language, and so 100 was denoted as hund teontig, or ten times ten. (IELTS6,T2,R3) 到 7世纪的时候 ，teon这个词跟盎格鲁 · 撒克逊语言中的 tachund和 hund是可以互换的 ，因而 100就描述为 hund teontig 或者 10乘以 10。

interdependence [ˌɪntədɪ’pendəns]

释义 • n. a situation in which people or things depend on each other 互相依赖，互助

词根 • inter(互相 )+dependence(依赖 )→互相依赖

派生 • interdependent adj. 互相依赖的

例句 • interdependence of natural resources (IELTS6,TA,R3)自然资源的相互依赖

interface [’ɪntəfeɪs]

释义 • n. a surface common to two areas 界面，分界面 ；a place where two subjects, etc. meet and affect each other 结合部位，交接处；边缘区域

词根 • inter(互相 )+face(脸 ，面 )→互相接触的面 →界面 ，分界面

例句 • Judging from the way it watches and tracks airborne flying fish, it can apparently see fairly well through the air-water interface as well. (IELTS4,T1,R3) 从它观察和跟踪飞鱼的方式来看 ，很显然它也可以看透空气和水的交界面 。

interference [ˌɪntə’fɪərəns]

释义 • n. an act of interfering 干涉，干预 ；the act or an instance of hindering, obstructing, or impeding 妨碍，打扰

词根 • inter(between)+fere(打 )+ence→打入中间 →干扰 ，干预

派生 • interfere9 v. 干涉 ，干预 ；妨碍 ，打扰

例句 • Interference with the ecosystem can have a severe effect on both local rainfall patterns and water run-off. (IELTS6,TA,R3) 对生态系统的干预会对当地的降雨模式和水流带来严重的影响 。

interminable [ɪnˈtɜ:mɪnəbl]

释义 • adj. endless, nonstop 冗长的；没完没了；无止境的

词根 • in-(not)+termin(界限)+-able（能）→画不出界限的→无止境的

例句 • There is nothing that these meaningless streams of air cannot do: from sighing the interminable boredom of existence to unravelling the fundamental order of the universe. (IELTS11,T4, R3) 这些原来无意义的气流声无所不能：下至感叹生活的不尽无聊，上至揭示宇宙的基本秩序。

intermittently [ˌɪntə’mɪtəntlɪ]

释义 • adv . at irregular intervals; not continuously or steadily 间歇地；断断续续地

词根 • inter（between）+mit（送）+-ent（adj. ）+ly(adv. ) →间隔着送的→间歇地

例句 • Deane continued diving on the site intermittently until 1840. (IELTS11,T2,R1) 一直到1840年，迪恩在该地区断断续续完成了几次潜水。

intermix [ˌɪntə’mɪks]

释义 • v. to mix together; intermingle 混杂，混合

词根 • inter(between)+mix→混杂 ，混合

例句 • Intermixed with the development of a number sense is the development of an ability to count. (IELTS6,T2,R3) 与人的数字意识一同发展的是人的计算能力 。

intermodal [ˌɪntə(ː)’məʊdl]

释义 • adj. relating to transportation by more than one means of conveyance, as by truck and rail 联合运输的

词根 • inter(between)+mode(模式 ，形式 )+al(adj .)→在不同的交通工具间传送 →联合运输的

例句 • But, behind the scenes, a series of technological innovations known broadly as containerisation and intermodal transportation has led to swift productivity improvements in cargo-handling. (IELTS6,T1,R2) 但是在这些背景之下 ， 一系列的技术革新已经迅速提高了货物的运输效率 ， 这些革新包括广为人知的集装箱运输和联合运输等 。

internationalist [ˌɪntə’næʃənəlɪst]

释义 • n. the belief that nations should work together and help each other 国际主义者 adj .国际主义的

派生 • international56 adj. 国际的

例句 • We establish links and access to the organization’ s agencies and other inter-nationalist organisations and their resources. (IELTS3,TB,R2)我们与机构的代理中心和其他国际主义组织合作 ，并有权使用他们的资源 。

interpreter [ɪn’tɜːprɪtə]

释义 • n. one who translates orally from one language into another 口译员，翻译器

词根 • inter(between)+pre(价值 )+er(人 )→在两种价值之间转换的人 →口译员

派生 • interpret8 v. 口译 ，翻译 ；解释 ，说明

interpretation9 n. 翻译 ；解释

例句 • With a bilingual informant, or through use of an interpreter , it is possible to use translation techniques. (IELTS4,T3,R3) 通过双语的仪器或者翻译器的使用 ，使用翻译技术是可能的 。

interruption [ˌɪntə’rʌpʃən]

释义 • n. to stop someone from continuing what they are saying or doing by suddenly speaking to them, making a noise etc. 打断，中断，暂停

词根 • inter(between)+rup(断 )+ion(n .)→打断

派生 • interrupt4 v. 打断 ，中断 ；打扰

例句 • Researchers have proposed several explanations for why interruption of glucose processing and ATP production might retard aging. (IELTS6,T3,R3) 研究者已经提出了几种说法来解释为什么打断葡萄糖合成和 ATP产生过程可以延缓衰老 。

intervene [ˌɪntə’viːn]

释义 • v. to interfere so as to prevent sth. happening or to change the result 干涉，干预 ；to come or be between 介入

词根 • inter(between)+ven(来 )+e→来到中间 →干涉

派生 • intervention6 n. 干涉 ，干预 ，介入

例句 • Although the lives of the Siriono have changed in the intervening decades, the image of them as Stone Age relics has endured. (IELTS3,T3,R2) 尽管 Siriono人的生活在这些年发生了改变 ，但是他们作为石器时代遗迹的形象却没变 。

interviewee [ˌɪntəvjuː’iː]

释义 • n. the person who answers the questions in an interview 被采访人；面试者

词根 • interview+ee(被 ……的人 )→被采访人

派生 • interview45 n. 面试

interviewer1 n. 采访人 ，面试官

例句 • The other requirement is the number of interviewees . (IELTS6,T3,L3) 另外一个要求就是面试者的数量 。

intrusion [ɪn’truːʒən]

释义 • n. intruding 侵入，闯入；侵扰，干扰

词根 • in(in)+trusion(插入 )→插进来 →侵入

派生 • intrude v. 侵入 ，闯入 ；干扰

intruder n. 闯入者

intrusive adj. 入侵的

例句 • We are much more able to tune out chronic background noise, even if it is quite loud, than to work under circumstances with unexpected intrusions of noise. (IELTS7,T4,R3) 与在一些有意外噪音的情况下坚持工作相比 ，我们更有能力对长期噪音听而不闻 ，即便它是很大的噪音 。

inundation [ˌɪnən’deɪʃən]

释义 • n. the state of receiving so much of something that you cannot easily deal with it all淹没，泛滥

派生 • inundate v. 涌来 ，充满 ；淹没 ，泛滥

例句 • The flashy brochures and pamphlets left by the sales reps are often followed up with meals at expensive restaurants, meetings in warm and sunny places, and an inundation of promotional gadgets. (IELTS6,T4,R1) 推销员在发放完花哨的宣传单和宣传册之后 ，就是在价格不菲的饭店进餐 ，或是在一个温暖而充满阳光的地方开会 ，然后促销的小物品也开始泛滥 。

invalid [ɪn’vælɪd]

释义 • adj. not usable; not officially acceptable (because of an incorrect detail or details); not legally recognized 无效的 ；state of being an invalid 残废的

词根 • in(无 )+val(价值 )+id→无效的

派生 • invalidate v. 使作废 ，证明错误

invalidity n. 病弱 ，年老体弱

例句 • The data is sometimes invalid . (IELTS4,T2,L3) 数据有时是无效的 。

invaluable [ɪn’væljʊəbəl]

释义 • adj. of value too high to be measured; extremely valuable 无价的

词根 • in(无 )+valuable(有价值的 )→无价的

例句 • Both were sold throughout the country and proved an invaluable way of informing members of meetings, marches, fundraising events and the latest news and views on the movement. (IELTS3,T4,R2) 两者都是在全国销售的 ，而且被证明是用来告知成员有关会议 、游行 、募捐 、及时的新闻以及时事评论等的极好的方式 。

inventory [’ɪnvəntrɪ]

释义 • n. a detailed list, e.g. of goods, furniture, jobs to be done 目录，存货

词根 • in(进来 )+vent(来 )+ory(物 )→关于进来的货物的登记 →目录

例句 • Increasingly, the big suppliers are becoming managing agents, which means they offer a total service to put together the whole complex operation of a company’ s corporate clothing package—which includes reliable sourcing, managing the inventory , budget control and distribution to either central locations or to each staff member individually. (IELTS3,TB,R3) 渐渐地 ，大供应商就变成运营代理商 ，这意味着他们要提供整套服务来把公司整体运作打包统筹起来 ，包括可靠的供货 、存货的管理 ，财务控制及发货到中心位置或单独的每个员工 。

irony [’aɪərənɪ]

释义 • n. expression of one’ s meaning by saying the direct opposite of one’ s thoughts in order to be emphatic, amusing, sarcastic, etc. 反语，讽刺 ；situation, event, etc. that is desirable in itself but so unexpected or ill-timed that it appears to be deliberately perverse 出人意料的事情

联想 • iron(铁 )+y→像铁一样冷冰冰的话 →反语 ，讽刺

派生 • ironically4 adv. 讽刺地

ironical adj. 讽刺的

例句 • Researchers, executives and marketing people are now using the expression without irony or inverted commas. (IELTS5,T3,R3) 研究者 、公司高管以及营销人员现在使用这个表达方式已经不含任何讽刺意义了 。

irrelevant [ɪ’reləvənt]

释义 • adj. not connected (with sth.); not relevant (to sth.) 不相关的，离题的

词根 • ir(not)+relevant(相关的 )→不相关的

派生 • irrelevance n. 不相关

例句 • It is in the light of an expectation that some observations are held to be relevant and some irrelevant . (IELTS3,T1,R3)根据预测 ，有些观察被认为是相关的 ，有些是无关的 。

irresistible [ˌɪrɪ’zɪstəbəl]

释义 • adj. too strong to be resisted 不可抗拒的 ；too delightful or attractive to be resisted 无法抑制的，富有诱惑力的

词根 • ir(not)+resistible(可抗拒的 )→不可抗拒的

例句 • During quiet periods, volcanoes cap themselves with their own lava by forming a powerful cone from the molten rocks slopping over the rim of the crater; later the lava cools slowly into a huge, hard, stable plug which blocks any further eruption until the pressure below becomes irresistible . (IELTS4,T3,R2) 在火山休眠期 ， 火山溢出的熔岩堆积成一个强大的锥体 ， 把火山用自身的熔岩盖了起来 ； 随后 ， 这些熔岩慢慢冷却 ， 之后形成一个巨大的 、 坚硬的 、 稳定的石块来阻止火山的进一步爆发 ， 除非下面的压力大到不可抗拒 。

irrevocable [ɪ’revəkəbəl]

释义 • adj. impossible to retract or revoke 无法取消的，不能改变的

词根 • ir(not)+revocable(可取消的 )→无法取消的

例句 • Therefore, it was felt that the Museum should acquire materials representing people whose art or material culture, ritual or political structures were on the point of irrevocable change. (IELTS3,T3,R1) 因此 ，人们认为博物馆要吸收对一个民族具有代表性的物品 ，因为该民族的艺术或物质文化 、仪式或政治结构正面临着不可逆转的变革 。

irrigate [’ɪrɪgeɪt]

释义 • v. to supply (land or crops) with water (by means of streams, reservoirs, channels, pipes, etc.) 灌溉

词根 • ir(进入 )+rig(水 )+ate→把水引进 →灌溉

派生 • irrigation19 n. 灌溉

例句 • At present, average efficiency in the use of irrigated water in agriculture may be as low as 50%. (IELTS6,TA,R3) 目前 ，农业中灌溉用水的平均效率低至 50%。

irritable [’ɪrɪtəbəl]

释义 • adj. easily annoyed or made angry; touchy 易怒的，急躁的

词根 • irritate(使烦躁 )+able→易怒的

派生 • irritate v. 使烦躁 ，使疼痛

irritation2 n. 激怒 ，刺激 ；刺激物 ，恼人事

irritability2 n. 易怒性

irritant adj. 刺激性的

例句 • When there is a thunderstorm brewing, some people complain of the air being heavy and of feeling irritable , moody and on edge. (IELTS3,T3,R3) 当暴风雨在酝酿时 ，一些人抱怨空气凝重 ，觉得易怒 、伤感 、处在崩溃的边缘 。

以r 为词首的形容词，其反义词通常在其前加ir：

irreconcilable adj. 不能和解的，不能调和的

irreducible adj. 不能减少的，不可简化的

irreparable adj. 无法修复的，不能挽回的

irrepressible adj. 不能抑制的

irrespective adj. 不考虑的，不顾及的

irresponsible adj. 不负责任的

irretrievable adj. 不能复得的

irreverent adj. 不虔诚的

irreversible adj. 不能反转的

itinerary [aɪ’tɪnərərɪ]

释义 • n. a plan for, or record of, a journey, including the route and the places that you visit 旅行计划或记录，旅行路线

例句 • I will be distributing leaflets at the end where you can find out more information, but just for the moment I’ ll outline the itinerary , the main high points of the holiday. (IELTS7,T3,L2) 最后我将发放传单 ，你可以找到更多信息 。但是现在我要简单地讲一下旅行路线 ，以及假日的主要亮点 。

jealously [’dʒeləslɪ]

释义 • adv. if you do something jealously, you are feeling jealous when you do it 妒忌地，猜疑地

派生 • jealous adj. 妒忌的 ，猜疑的

jealousy n. 妒忌 ，猜疑

例句 • In Canada, where the Inuit people are jealously guarding their hard-won autonomy in the country’ s newest territory, Nunavut, they believe their best hope of survival in this changing environment lies in combining their ancestral knowledge with the best of modern science. (IELTS6,T1,R3)在加拿大 ，因纽特人小心地捍卫着他们来之不易的 、令人羡慕的新确立的自治区 ——努纳武特地区 。因纽特人相信他们在这个不断变化的环境中生存下来的最大的希望 ，就是要把祖上传下来的知识与现代科学方法结合起来 。

jeopardise [’dʒepədaɪz]

释义 • v. to cause (sth.) to be harmed, lost or destroyed; to put in danger 危及，危害

同义 • endanger, injure

派生 • jeopardy n. 危害

例句 • The consequences of our water policies extend beyond jeopardising human health. (IELTS7,T1,R2) 我们的水资源政策产生的后果不仅是危害人类健康这么简单 。

jerky [’dʒɜːkɪ]

释义 • adj. characterized by jerks or jerking 忽动忽停的；结结巴巴的；颠簸不稳的

派生 • jerk3 v. 猛地摇晃 ，急拉 ，急抽

例句 • jerky movement (IELTS4,T1,R3)颠簸的运动

jet lag [’dʒetˌlæg]

释义 • n. a temporary disruption of bodily rhythms caused by high-speed travel across several time zones typically in a jet aircraft 时差，飞行时差反应

例句 • Melatonin pills contain a synthetic version of the hormone and are commonly used for jet lag as well as for sleep disturbance. (IELTS5,TA,R3)褪黑激素药片含有一种人工合成的褪黑激素 ，通常用于治疗时差反应和其他睡眠问题 。

jolt [dʒəʊlt]

释义 • v. to move or to make sb./sth. move suddenly and roughly 摇动，晃动

例句 • “With the eaves extending out on all sides like balancing poles,” says Mr Ishida, “the building responds to even the most powerful jolt of an earthquake with a graceful swaying, never an abrupt shaking.”(IELTS7,T2,R1) Ishida先生说 ，“四面的屋檐都向外伸出 ，就像平衡柱 ，建筑物面对地震产生的最有力的摇晃也只是轻微地摇摆 ，不会突然摇晃 。

judicious [dʒuː’dɪʃəs]

释义 • adj. having or exhibiting sound judgment; prudent 明智的，有见识的

词根 • judic(判断 )+ious→判断力强的 →明智的 ，有见识的

派生 • judiciously adv. 明智地

judiciousness n. 明智 ，有见识

例句 • Archaeology makes clear that with judicious management, selected parts of the region could support more people than anyone thought before. (IELTS3,T3,R2) 考古学家指明 ，有了明智的管理 ，选定的区域可能会养活比任何人先前想象的都多的人 。

judo [’dʒuːdəʊ]

释义 • n. a sport and method of physical training similar to wrestling, developed in Japan in the late 19th century and using principles of balance and leverage adapted from jujitsu 柔道

例句 • Do you have judo classes? (IELTS6,T1,L1)你上柔道课吗 ？

junction [’dʒʌŋkʃən]

释义 • n. the act or process of joining or the condition of being joined 连接，接合； a place where two things join or meet, especially a place where two roads or railway routes come together and one terminates 交叉点，接合处，枢纽站

词根 • junct(连接 )+ion(n .)→连接

搭配 • at the junction of 在 ……的汇合处

同义 • joint, connection, intersection

例句 • A ‘ keep clear’ sign will be erected at the junction . (IELTS8,T4,L2) 在连接处会立着一个 “请勿靠近”的标语 。

jury [’dʒʊərɪ]

释义 • n. a group of people in a lawcourt who have been chosen to listen to the facts in a case and to decide whether the accused person is guilty or not guilty 陪审团

例句 • Essentially the jury is out on that. (IELTS4,T3,L4) 重要的是 ，陪审团会把那件事公开化 。

justice [’dʒʌstɪs]

释义 • n. right and fair behaviour or treatment 正义，公正 ；the law and its administration 司法

词根 • just(正义的 )+ice(n .)→正义 ，公正

搭配 • bring sb. to justice 将 ……绳之以法

do sb./sth. justice 展示某人或某物的优良品质

例句 • In the past, the case for public transport has been made on the basis of environmental and social justice considerations rather than economics. (IELTS6,T2,R1) 过去 ，这个公共交通方案是在考虑环境和社会公正性的基础上做出的 ，而不是建立在经济基础上 。

justification [ˌdʒʌstɪfɪ’keɪʃən]

释义 • n. an acceptable reason (for doing sth.) 正当理由 ；as a defence (of sb./sth.) 辩白，辩护

词根 • justi (正当的 )+fic(做 )+ation→要做得公平 →正当理由 ，辩护

派生 • justify1 v. 证明 ……是正当的 ，为 ……辩护

justified2 adj. 正当的 ，有正当理由的

例句 • The term is being applied, with some justification , to products that depend on technology that was originally developed by AI researchers. (IELTS5,T3,R3)该词被很正当地用在了最初由人工智能研究者们研发的技术产品上 。

kidney [’kɪdnɪ]

释义 • n. either of a pair of organs in the body that remove waste products from the blood and produce urine 肾，肾脏

例句 • In addition to being responsible for more than 85 percent of lung cancers, smoking is associated with cancers of, amongst others, the mouth, stomach and kidneys , and is thought to cause about 14 percent of leukemia and cervical cancers. (IELTS3,T1,R2) 除了造成 85%的肺癌 ，吸烟还与嘴部 、胃部和肾部的癌症相关 ，并且 14%的白血病和宫颈癌都是由吸烟引起的 。

心heart 肝 liver

脾 spleen 肺 lung

肾 kidney

kit [kɪt]

释义 • n. an equipment needed for a particular (esp. sporting) activity, situation or trade 成套工具 v. to equip sb. 装备

例句 • Small loans are provided initially for purchasing fixed assets such as bicycles, shoe shine kits and basic building materials for a market stall. (IELTS4,T3,R1) 最初提供的是小额贷款 ， 用来购买固定资产 ， 如自行车 、 擦鞋工具和建立市场摊位需要的基本建筑材料 。

knowledgeable [’nɒlɪdʒəbəl]

释义 • adj. well-informed有丰富知识的，消息灵通的

派生 • knowledge67 n. 知识

例句 • How can we possibly account for this vast discrepancy between what calm, rational, knowledgeable people predict in the comfort of their study and what pressured, flustered, but cooperative teachers actually do in the laboratory of real life? (IELTS5,T1,R2) 一方面是平静 、理性 、知识丰富的人在舒适的书房里做出的预测 ，一方面是有压力的 、不知所措但可以合作的老师在真实的实验室里的情况 。我们怎么能够解释他们之间的巨大差异呢 ？

laden [’leɪdn]

释义 • adj. loaded or weighted 装满的，满载的；饱含，充溢着(某种味道的)

搭配 • be laden with 装满 ，饱含

例句 • But by the time the sediment has come to rest in the fields and lagoons, it is laden with municipal, industrial and agricultural waste from the Cairo region, which is home to more than 40 million people. (IELTS5,T3,R2) 但是 ，当沉积物在田地和泻湖中沉淀下来时 ，它就被有 4，000万人居住的开罗地区的城市 、工业和农业的废物所充斥 。

释义 • adj. fairly large相当大的

词根 • large+ish(有 ……倾向的 )→倾向于大的 →相当大的

例句 • Forty percent of the respondents were in favour, but a largish minority were strongly against. (IELTS4,T3,L4) 40%的被调查者表示赞成 ，但是相当多的少数派强烈反对 。

-ish: 加在形容词之后，表示含有某种程度的、略…的、稍…的：

coldish adj. 略寒的

greenish adj. 略带绿色的

warmish adj. 稍暖的

yellowish adj. 微黄的

oldish adj. 略老的

reddish adj. 略红的

wettish adj. 略湿的

lash [læʃ]

例句 • Units will include maintaining employment standards, salon management duties, providing facial massage and skin care, instruction on make-up, lash and brow treatments, artificial nail structures and ear piercing. (IELTS4,TA,R2) 内容包括遵守雇佣标准 ， 维持沙龙管理责任 ， 提供脸部按摩和皮肤护理 ， 提供化妆 、 修理睫毛和眉毛 、 美甲和打耳洞等方面的指导 。

派生 • law10 n. 法律

(IELTS4,TA,R3) 电影改变很大的其他国家有 ……和日本 ，在那里 ，电影主要是在传统的戏剧或者其他不太重要的艺术形式的基础上发展起来的 ，并逐渐地接受了西方的影响 。

lightweight [’laɪtˌweɪt]

(IELTS5,T1,R1) Samuel Johnson 博士是 18 世纪文人的楷模 ， 不仅在他那个时代出名 ， 而且在我们这个时代也一样出名 。 他在中产阶级的鼎盛时期出版了其编纂的大辞典是极其适时的 。

malaria [mə’leəriə]

释义 • n. any of a group of diseases, usually intermittent or remittent, characterized by attacks of chills, fever, and sweating: formerly supposed to be due to swamp exhalations but now known to be caused by a parasitic protozoan, which is transferred to the human bloodstream by a mosquito of the genus Anopheles and which occupies and destroys red blood cells 疟疾

例句 • There were improvements in agriculture that wiped out malaria , but these were small gains. (IELTS10,T2,R1)农业方面取得了进步 ，消灭了疟疾 ，但这些只是小小的胜利 。

manifest [’mænɪfest]

(IELTS11,T4, L4) 她与她的学生正在测试从废物中产生的堆肥对碳储量的影响。这些废物包括粪便和玉米杆，以及花园中的树叶、树枝和草坪剪裁物。

mechanics [mɪ’kænɪks]

mess [mes]

释义 • n. a difficult or confused state or situation; disorder 混乱，杂乱 ；a dirty or untidy state 脏乱；困境 v. to put (sth.) into an untidy, etc. state 弄脏，弄乱

(IELTS7,T2,R2) 我们以三种方式来支付廉价的食物 ：首先通过柜台 ，其次通过税收提供的巨额补贴来维持现代密集型耕作 ，之后处理现代农业耕作遗留的问题 。

miniature [’mɪnɪtʃə]

派生 • miniaturize v. 使微型化

例句 • The Dynamic figures are painted in miniature . （IELTS8,T4,L4）活跃的人物被涂成微型人物 。

minus [’maɪnəs]

释义 • n. the mathematical symbol 减号，负号 ；disadvantage or drawback 不利，不足，缺点 adj. negative 负的，不利的

词根 • min(小 )+us→减少的

例句 • On the minus side, our testers did not like the fact that the side of the cot did not drop down, making it difficult to pick up newborn babies. (IELTS5,T1,L2) 不利的一面是 ，试验者不喜欢婴儿床的一边不能放下这一点 ，因为这样使得抱起婴儿较为困难 。

misfortune [mɪs’fɔːtʃən]

释义 • n. bad luck 不幸，灾难，灾祸

词根 • mis(不好的 ，错误的 )+fortune(运气 )→不幸 ，灾难

例句 • They think their misfortune is an accident or that it’ s the fault of no-one. (IELTS4,T2,L4) 他们认为自身的不幸是偶然的或者并非人为的错误 。

同根词：mis- → bad, wrong

mislead v. 误导

mishandle3 v. 错误处理，虐待

mismanagement1 n. 错误管理，错误经营

misunderstand v. 误解

mitigate [’mɪtɪgeɪt]

释义 • v. to lessen in force or intensity, as wrath, grief, harshness, or pain; moderate 使缓和，使减轻

派生 • mitigation n . 缓和 ，减轻

同义 • alleviate, ease, lessen, mollify, reduce, relieve, soothe, weaken

例句 • Many of her students said that faced with a risky situation, they first tried to calm themselves down, then looked for a way to mitigate the danger. （IELTS10,T4,R2）她的许多学生说 ，当面对危险时 ，他们首先试图平静下来 ，然后再寻求缓解危险的办法 。

mock [mɒk]

释义 • v. to make fun of (sb./sth.), esp. by mimicking him/it contemptuously; ridicule 愚弄，嘲弄；使受挫折 adj. not real; substitute 仿制的，模拟的

同义 • laugh at, make fun of, fool; artificial, fake, false

派生 • mockery n. 讥笑 ，嘲笑 ，笑柄

mocking n. 嘲弄 ，愚弄

mocker n. 嘲笑者 ，模仿者

搭配 • make a mock of 使 ……成为笑柄

mock at 嘲笑 ，嘲弄

例句 • There’ s a mock camp site where you can see inside an Antarctic tent and imagine yourself sleeping there. (IELTS7,T2,L3) 有一个仿制的野营地 ，在里面你可以看到南极的帐篷 ，并且想象自己在里面睡觉 。

momentum [məʊ’mentəm]

释义 • n. a force that increases the rate of development of a process; impetus 动力，冲力，势头；动量

词根 • moment(瞬间 )+ um →冲力在瞬间迸发 →冲力 ，动力

搭配 • gain / gather momentum发展加快 ，势头增大

例句 • In the following century much of this momentum was lost as German established itself as the leading European language of science. (IELTS5,T2,R3) 在随后的几个世纪里 ，这种势头渐渐消失 ，因为德语逐渐成为欧洲科学界的主导语言 。

monotonous [mə’nɒtənəs]

释义 • adj. not changing and therefore uninteresting; boring or tedious 无变化的，单调乏味的

词根 • mono(单个的 )+ton(声音 )+ous→单调的

派生 • monotony n. 单调 ，无变化

例句 • The sperm whale apparently produces a monotonous series of high-energy clicks and little else. (IELTS4,T1,R3) 抹香鲸发出一系列明显而单调的高强度咔嗒声 ，除此之外几乎没有其他的 。

moody [’muːdɪ]

释义 • adj. given to frequent changes of mood; temperamental 喜怒无常的，易怒的 ； expressive of a mood, especially a sullen or gloomy mood 情绪不好的

派生 • mood11 n. 心情 ，情绪 ；(动词的 )语气

搭配 • be (not) in the mood (for sth./to do sth.)有 /没有做某事的心情

be in a good mood情绪好

be in a bad mood情绪不好

例句 • When there is a thunderstorm brewing, some people complain of the air being heavy and of feeling irritable, moody and on edge. (IELTS3,T3,R3) 当雷雨在酝酿时 ，一些人就抱怨空气凝重 ，感觉易怒 、伤感 、处于崩溃的边缘 。

multiple [’mʌltɪpəl]

myriad [’mɪrɪəd]

释义 • n. an extremely large number of sth.无数, 极大数量 adj. 无数的

例句 • As their eyes adjusted to the darkness they saw myriad lights reflecting off the water. (IELTS5,TB,R3) 随着他们的眼睛适应了黑暗 ，他们看到了水面反射出无数光亮 。

mystical [’mɪstɪkəl]

释义 • adj. unintelligible; cryptic 神秘的，奥秘的

词根 • myst (谜 ) + ical(形容词后缀 )→神秘的 ，奥秘的

例句 • They meet a strange old lady who tells them of the mystical powers of the house and how previous owners have been able to travel back through the centuries to meet their ancestors. (IELTS5,TB,R1) 他们遇见了一个奇怪的老妇人 ，这个老妇人告诉了他们这个房子的神秘力量 ，以及这个房子先前的主人如何穿越好几个世纪去见他们的祖先 。

mystify [’mɪstəfaɪ]

释义 • v. to make (sb.) confused through lack of understanding; to puzzle; to bewilder 使迷惑

词根 • myst(谜 )+ify(动词后缀 )→使困惑不解 ，使迷惑

搭配 • be mystified at sth. 对 ……感到迷惑

例句 • Japanese scholars have been mystified for ages about why these tall, slender buildings are so stable. (IELTS7,T2,R1) 几十年来日本的学者们都对这些高耸的 、纤细的建筑物为什么能够平稳矗立而感到迷惑不解 。

释义 • n. myths collectively 神话，神话集

例句 • In the mythology of giftedness, it is popularly believed that if people are talented in one area, they must be defective in another. (IELTS8,T3,R2) 在关于天赋的神话集中 ，人们普遍认为一个人在某一方面有才能 ，那么在另一方面肯定有缺陷 。

naive [nɑɪ’iːv]

释义 • adj. showing lack of experience, wisdom or judgement 幼稚的 ；natural and innocent in speech and behaviour; unaffected 天真的

联想 • native意为原始的 ，土著的 ，再去掉 t，本来已经很原始了 ，现在更幼稚

派生 • naively adv. 幼稚地 ，天真地

naivety n. 幼稚 ，天真 ，缺乏阅历

例句 • Where is your naive , pure and objective researcher now? (IELTS3,T1,R3) 你天真 、纯洁和客观的研究者现在在哪里呢 ？

nasty [’nɑːstɪ]

naturalistic [ˌnætʃərə’lɪstɪk]

negotiation [nɪˌgəʊʃiː’eɪʃən]

niggle [’nɪgəl]

nitrogen [’naɪtrədʒən]

释义 • n. a colorless, odorless, gaseous element that constitutes about four-fifths of the volume of the atmosphere and is present in combined form in animal and vegetable tissues, especially in proteins: used chiefly in the manufacture of ammonia, nitric acid, cyanide, explosives, fertilizer, dyes, as a cooling agent, etc. 氮

例句 • But before letting its leaves go, the tree dismantles their chlorophyll molecules and ships their valuable nitrogen back into the twigs. (IELTS10,T3,R2)但是在树叶掉落之前 ，树木会分解其体内的叶绿素分子 ，将宝贵的氮气输送到枝干中去 。

nomadic [nəʊ’mædɪk]

派生 • nomad n. 游牧部落中的一员 ，流浪者

例句 • Over the past 40 years, most have abandoned their nomadic ways and settled in the territory’ s 28 isolated communities, but they still rely heavily on nature to provide food and clothing. (IELTS6,T1,R3) 在过去 40多年来 ，他们中的大多数已经摆脱了游牧生活 ，定居在领土内 28个孤立的社区中 ，但是他们仍然在很大程度上依赖大自然为他们提供食物和衣物 。

nominal [’nɒmɪnəl]

派生 • nominate1 v. 提名

nonpolitical [ˌnɒnpə’lɪtɪkəl]

词根 • non(非 )+political→非政治的

nonrefundable [ˌnɒnrɪ’fʌndəbl]

例句 • Deposits and payments are nonrefundable and non-transferable. (IELTS3,TA,R2) 存款和付款是不能退回和转账的 。

nonsense [’nɒnsəns]

释义 • n. foolish talk,ideas, etc. 胡闹，胡说

词根 • non(非 ，没 )+sense(意义 )→没有意义的话 →胡说 ，胡闹

派生 • nonsensical adj. 胡说的

例句 • But most modern humour theorists have settled on some version of Aristotle’ s belief that jokes are based on a reaction to or resolution of incongruity, when the punchline is either a nonsense or, though appearing silly, has a clever second meaning. (IELTS5,T2,R2) 但是大多数幽默理论家承袭了亚里士多德的某种观点 ：幽默是建立在人们对不协调的反应或解决的基础上的 ，当妙语表面上看起来是胡闹或者很愚蠢 ，它却有很聪明的第二个层面上的意思 。

notational [nəʊ’teɪʃənəl]

词根 • note(笔记 )+ation(做 )+al(……的 )→记号的 ，标记的

派生 • notation n. 记号 ，标记

例句 • When the number 4 can be registered in the mind as a specific word, independent of the object being referenced, the individual is ready to take the first step toward the development of a notational system for numbers and, from there, to arithmetic. (IELTS6,T2,R3) 当数字 4能够被当作特定的词汇印在脑中 ，与所指的事物不再有关系时 ，个人便开始建立数字的标记系统 ，并由此建立几何系统 。

noticeably [’nəʊtɪsəblɪ]

numerate [’njuːmərɪt]

释义 • v. to count, calculate 计数，计算

innumerable adj. 无数的

例句 • The numeration system of the Tsimshian language in British Columbia contains seven distinct sets of words for numbers according to the class of the item being counted: for counting flat objects and animals, for round objects and time, for people, for long objects and trees, for canoes, for measures, and for counting when no particular object is being numerated. (IELTS6,T2,R3)在英属哥伦比亚的钦西安语中 ，根据要数的东西的类型 ，可以用 7组不同的单词来表示数目 ：用来数扁平的物体和动物 ，用来数圆形的物体和时间 ，用来数人 ，用来数长的物体和树 ，用来数船 ，用来数测量的东西 ，用来数不具体的事物 。

obedient [ə’biːdənt]

obnoxious [əb’nɒkʃəs]

obsession [əb’seʃən]

oddly [’ɒdlɪ]

释义 • adv. in a strange or unusual way 奇妙地，奇怪地

派生 • odd3 adj. 奇特的 ，古怪的

同义 • strange, queer, eccentric, peculiar

反义 • normal, usual, ordinary

例句 • Oddly enough, half the glass that’ s collected is green, and a lot of that is imported, so more green glass is recycled than the UK needs. (IELTS5,T3,L4)奇怪的是 ，回收的玻璃一半都是绿色的 ，而且其中很多是进口而来 ，于是回收的绿色玻璃远多于英国所需要的 。

offence [ə’fens]

释义 • n. the act of breaking of a rule or law; an illegal act; a crime 违法行为；冒犯

词根 • of (against)+fen(d) (打击 ) +ce(n .)→对着打 →冒犯 ，得罪

派生 • offend v. 冒犯 ，犯罪

offensive1 adj. 令人不快的 ，冒犯的

offender1 n. 违反者 ，冒犯者

同义 • violation, insult

例句 • Victimised pupils are more likely to experience difficulties with interpersonal relationships as adults, while children who persistently bully are more likely to grow up to be physically violent, and convicted of anti-social offences . (IELTS6,T4,R3)受过伤害的小学生长大后很容易产生人际交往障碍 ，而那些一直欺人者长大后则更有可能变得很暴力 ，甚至因违法而被判刑 。

oftcited [’ɒfsaɪtɪd]

释义 • adj. that is often cited 经常被引用的

词根 • oft(经常 )+ cite(引用 )+ (e)d(adj .)→经常被引用的

例句 • “The athlete must choose his parents carefully,” says Jesus Dapena, a sports scientist at Indiana University, invoking an oftcited adage. (IELTS4,T4,R1) 杰色斯 · 达普诺是印第安纳大学的一位体育研究专家 ，他说了一句经常被人们引用的箴言 ，“运动员一定要慎重选择自己的父母”。

oily [’ɒɪlɪ]

释义 • adj. of or like oil油的，油滑的

派生 • oil n. 油

例句 • Discovered in the early 1800s and named nicotianine, the oily essence now called nicotine is the main active ingredient of tobacco. (IELTS5,T2,L1) 这种油性物质发现于 19世纪早期 ，当时被命名为烟草香素 ，现在被称为尼古丁 ，是烟草主要的活跃成分 。

onset [’ɒnset]

释义 • n. the beginning of sth., especially sth. unpleasant 开始

同义 • beginning, start, outset

例句 • With the onset of statehood, however, the State of Alaska took over management of its own fisheries, guided by a state constitution which mandates that Alaska’ s natural resources be managed on a sustainable basis. (IELTS7,T4,R2) 阿拉斯加政府一成立 ，就接管了自己的渔业 ，按照州立法律的规定 ，阿拉斯加的自然资源开发要遵循可持续发展的道路 。

onshore [ˌɒn’ʃɔː]

释义 • adj./adv. blowing from the sea towards the land (指风)向岸(的)，向陆(的)； on or near the shore 在岸上(的)；近岸(的)

词根 • on(在 ……上 )+shore(滨 ，岸 )→在岸上的

例句 • Well the information is transferred direct to onshore meteorological stations. (IELTS7,T3,L3)信息直接被传到岸边的气象台 。

onslaught [’ɒnslɔːt]

释义 • n. a fierce attack突击，猛击，猛攻

词根 • on(在 ……上 )+slaught(打击 )→猛击

同义 • assault

例句 • There are still huge gaps in our environmental knowledge, and despite the scientific onslaught , many predictions are no more than best guesses. (IELTS6,T1,R3) 我们对环境还知之甚少 ，虽然在不停地进行科学研究 ，但是很多预测只不过是一些比较合理的猜想而已 。

opulence [’ɒpjʊləns]

释义 • n. having or showing signs of great wealth 富裕，富饶

派生 • opulent1 adj. 富饶的 ，富足的

同义 • abundance

例句 • As audiences grew, so did the places where films were shown, finishing up with the “great picture palaces” of the 1920s, which rivalled, and occasionally superseded, theatres and opera-houses in terms of opulence and splendour. (IELTS4,TA,R3) 随着观众人数的增加 ， 放映电影的场所也增加了 ， 最终呈现出 20 世纪 20 年代的 “ 商店影院 ” 景象 。 这些 电影院的豪华陈设和华丽气势都与当时的剧院形成了竞争 ，有时甚至取代了它们 。

ornamental [ˌɔːnə’mentl]

ornamentation n. 装饰 ，点缀

同义 • decorative

例句 • If you look out here to the south, you can see a circular ornamental pond. (IELTS7,T4,L2) 如果你从这儿向南看 ，你会看见一个圆形的 、装饰精美的小池塘 。

outdated [ˌaʊt’deɪtɪd]

词根 • out (向外的 ，出外的 ，超出的 )+date(日期 ，时代 )+(e)d(adj .)→过期的

例句 • But they are suffering from having to work with outdated production machinery and that could cost a lot to put right. (IELTS5,T4,L3) 但是他们忍受着必须使用过时的生产机器进行工作的痛苦 ，这也花费了他们很多时间和精力去纠正错误 。

outer [’aʊtə]

outing [’aʊtɪŋ]

释义 • n. a trip that you go on for pleasure or education, usually with a group of people and lasting no more than one day 短途旅行，远足

例句 • But you may have a particular interest you wish to pursue or you may wish to participate in outings or trips if you don’ t know many people at the moment. (IELTS3,T2,L2)但是也许你有个自己很想追求的特殊爱好 ，如果此刻你认识的人不多 ，你可以参加一些远足或者短途旅行活动 。

overcrowded [ˌəʊvə’kraʊdɪd]

overdone [’əʊvə’dʌn]

词根 • over(过多 ，过于 )+done(被做 )→做过头的

派生 • overdo v. 做过头 ，做过火 ，做过分

例句 • Neatness can suggest efficiency but, if it is overdone , it can spill over and indicate an obsession with power. (IELTS3,TB,R3)简洁可以提高效率 ，但是如果做过头了的话 ，就可能影响其他方面 ，同时它也是痴迷于权利的表现 。

overload [ˌəʊvə’ləʊd]

释义 • v. to put too great a load on or into (sth.) 使(某物)装载过重

词根 • over(超过 )+ load(装载 ，负载 )→超载

例句 • In particular, the problem of information overload , exacerbated by the growth of e-mail and the explosion in the number of web pages, means there are plenty of opportunities for new technologies to help filter and categorise information—classic AI (artificial intelligence) problems. (IELTS5,T3,R3) 尤其重要的是 ，信息负载过量的问题随着电子邮件和网页的增多而加剧 ，这也就意味着 ，它为帮助过滤和分类信息的新技术提供了大量的机会 ，这就是典型的人工智能问题 。

overly [’əʊvəlɪ]

释义 • adv. too; excessively 太，过度

例句 • It may be costly to be overly optimistic—but more costly still to be too pessimistic. (IELTS5,T1,R3) 过度的乐观可能要付出很大的代价 ，但是过度悲观付出的代价更大 。

overlying [ˌəʊvə’laɪɪŋ]

派生 • overlie v. 放上面 (覆盖在 ……上面 ，叠加 )

例句 • Even though the mantle rocks are kept solid by overlying pressure, they can still slowly “flow” like thick treacle. (IELTS4,T3,R2) 即使上面的压力会使地幔岩石保持坚固 ，但它们还是会像粘稠的糖浆一般缓慢流动 。

overnight [ˌəʊvə’naɪt]

词根 • over(超过 )+night(晚上 )→超过一个晚上

overshadow [ˌəʊvə’ʃædəʊ]

overstaffed [ˌəʊvə’stɑːft]

overstate [ˌəʊvə’steɪt]

词根 • over(超过 )+state(陈述 )→过多地陈述 →夸大

派生 • overstatement n. 夸大 ，言过其实

例句 • Understandably, perhaps, they sometimes overstate their arguments. (IELTS5,T1,R3) 可以理解的是 ，也许有时候他们夸大了论据 。

词根 • over (超过的 ，过多的 )+use(使用 )→过多使用

ownership [’əʊnəʃɪp]

词根 • own(拥有 )+er (人 )+ship (n. 表示关系 )→所有权

例句 • State ownership of railways and airlines, regulation of freight rates and toleration of anti-competitive practices, such as cargo-handling monopolies, all keep the cost of shipping unnecessarily high and deter international trade. (IELTS6,T1,R2)铁路和航空的国有性质 、运费的规定以及对反竞争行为的放任 ，如货物装卸的垄断等 ，所有这些都导致水运费用极高 ，并且阻碍了国际贸易的发展 。

painstaking [’peɪnzˌteɪkɪŋ]

peninsula [pɪ’nɪnsjʊlə]

perceptual [pə’septjʊəl]

peril [’perɪl]

periodic [ˌpɪərɪ’ɒdɪk]

词根 • peri(一周 ，周围 )+od(way道路 )+ic(adj .)→定期的

派生 • periodical2 adj. / n. / adv. 定期出版的 ；期刊 ；定期地 ，周期地

同义 • recurrent, intermittent, regular

例句 • Periodic check-ups of the child’ s educational and sensory development (hearing and vision) were made to detect possible handicaps that interfere with growth and development. (IELTS5,T3,R1)他们对儿童的教育发展和感官发展 (听觉和视觉 )进行定期检查 ，以此来检测儿童成长和发展过程中可能出现的障碍 。

peripherally [pə’rɪfərəlɪ]

释义 • adv. of or on a periphery 外围地，边缘地

词根 • peri (周围 )+pher(带 )+al(adj .)+ly(adv .)→周围地带的 →周边的

派生 • peripheral5 adj. 外围的 ，边缘的 ；次要的 ，不重要的

periphery n. 外围 ，边缘

例句 • Besides the laboratory evidence for this, we know from our experience that we often remember what we have perceived peripherally , long after we have forgotten what we set out to learn. (IELTS7,T1,R3) 除了来自实验室的证据 ，我们根据经验也可以知道 ：如果过了很长一段时间 ，那么我们往往早已忘记了最开始时要学的东西 ，但却记住了当时我们不经意间留意到的东西 。

perish [’perɪʃ]

释义 • v. to be destroyed; die 丧生，消亡，死亡 ；(cause sth. to) rot; (cause rubber to) lose its elasticity 损坏，腐烂

词根 • per(away)+ish(走 )→走开 →消失

搭配 • perish from/with … 因 ……而丧生

perish in 在 ……中丧生

派生 • perishable adj. 可消亡的 ；会腐败的

perishing adj. 非常冷的

例句 • Colder, much wetter weather descended on Europe between 1315 and 1319, when thousands perished in a continent-wide famine. (IELTS8,T2,R2) 1315年到 1319年期间 ，更冷更湿的天气降临欧洲 ，许多人丧生于遍及整个欧洲的饥荒 。

perquisite [’pɜːkwɪzɪt]

释义 • n. money or goods given or regarded as a right in addition to one’ s pay (工资以外的)补贴，津贴，奖金 ；special advantage or right enjoyed as a result of one’ s position (随职位而得到的)好处，利益，特权，优待

词根 • per(完全 ，彻底 )+quisite(求得 ，要求 )→完全得到的东西 →特权

例句 • These and other perquisites of status are often frowned upon, but… (IELTS3, T2, R3) 这些以及其他一些代表社会地位的特权经常让人感到反感 ，但是 ……

persevere [ˌpɜːsɪ’vɪə]

释义 • v. to continue trying to do sth., esp. in spite of difficulty 坚持不懈，不屈不挠

词根 • per(彻底 )+severe(严格 )→彻底地严格 →坚持不懈

派生 • perseverance2 n. 坚持不懈 ，不屈不挠

例句 • And finally, with potentially tens of thousands of hiding places for drugs, the dog must persevere and maintain focus for hours at a time. (IELTS7,TA,R3) 最后 ，毒品的窝藏处可能有成千上万个 ，警犬必须毫不松懈 ，持续保持警觉长达好几个小时 。

persistently [pə’sɪstəntlɪ]

释义 • adv. refusing to give up 坚持地，不屈不挠地 ；continuing without interruption 持续不断地

词根 • per(一直 ，从头到尾 )+sist(站立 )+ent(adj .)+ ly(adv .)→坚持地

派生 • persistent6 adj. 坚持的 ，不屈不挠的 ；持续不断的

persist v. 坚持到底 ，持久

同义 • constantly, incessantly, perpetually, continuously, continually, endlessly

例句 • Victimised pupils are more likely to experience difficulties with interpersonal relationships as adults, while children who persistently bully are more likely to grow up to be physically violent, and convicted of anti-social offences. (IELTS6,T4,R3) 受过伤害的小学生长大后更容易经历人际交往障碍 ，而那些长期欺人者长大后则更有可能变得很暴力 ，甚至因违法而被判刑 。

personalise [’pɜːsənəlaɪz]

释义 • v. to cause (sth.) to become concerned with personal matters or feelings 使(某事物)针对个人，带有个人感情或个人化

派生 • personal52 adj. 个人的 ，私人的

personally3 adv. 个人地 ，私人地

personality7 n. 人格 ，个性

例句 • Managers could use their knowledge of each employee to personalise the rewards over which they have control. (IELTS6,T3,R2) 经理们控制奖金 ，他们可以根据对每一位员工的了解 ，针对个人给予不同的奖金 。

peruse [pə’ruːz]

释义 • v. to read (sth.), esp. carefully or thoroughly 细阅，审阅 ；to read (sth.) quickly and without concentrating 浏览

例句 • While perusing a book on the monuments of Egypt, she noticed a hieroglyph that showed a row of men standing in odd pastures. (IELTS7,T4,R1) 当她在读一本关于埃及纪念碑的书时 ，她注意到一个象形字 ，这个象形字表现的是一排人站在奇怪的牧场上 。

pervasive [pə’veɪsɪv]

释义 • adj. spread throughout 普遍的

派生 • pervade v .遍及 ，弥漫

例句 • “The principle of social proof is so pervasive that we don’ t even recognise it.” says Cialdini. (IELTS10,T1,R3) Cialdini说 ：“社会验证原则如此普遍 ，以致于我们都没有辨别出来它 。”

perversely [pə’vɜːslɪ]

释义 • adv. deliberately continuing to behave in a way that is wrong, unreasonable or unacceptable 任性地，固执地，一意孤行地

词根 • per(完全 ，从头到尾 )+verse(转 ，转向 ，改变 )+ly(adv .)→固执地

派生 • perverse adj. 任性的 ，固执的 ，一意孤行的

例句 • A second reason for writing in Latin may, perversely , have been a concern for secrecy. (IELTS5,T2,R3) 用拉丁文写的第二个原因也许偏偏就是出于保密的考虑 。

physiology [ˌfɪzɪ’ɒlədʒɪ]

派生 • physiological5 adj. 生理的

physiologist n. 生理学家

例句 • The fifth resolution relaunched the European research network on the physiology of trees, called Eurosilva. (IELTS7,T1,R3) 第五个解决方案使欧洲研究网络重新回到对树木的生理研究上来 ，这就是 Eurosilva研究项目 。

pickings [’pɪkɪŋz]

释义 • n. profits or gains that are easily or dishonestly earned or obtained 轻易挣得的或来路不正的财物、好处、利益等；收集，收获

例句 • Farming is out of the question and nature offers meagre pickings . (IELTS6,T1,R3)耕作根本不可能 ，大自然给予的是非常贫瘠的收获 。

pictorial [pɪk’tɔːrɪəl]

picturesque [ˌpɪktʃə’resk]

词根 • picture(图片 )+sque(adj .)→美丽如画的

派生 • picturesquely adv. 迷人地 ；奇特地

picturesqueness n. 迷人 ，美丽

例句 • The Waikato river, the longest river in New Zealand, flows through the centre of the city, providing a picturesque and park-like setting of riverside walks and gardens. (IELTS3,TA,R2) 怀卡托河是新西兰最长的河流 ，它穿过城市的中心 ，风景如画 ，河岸和花园都像公园中的景色一样 。

piercing [’pɪəsɪŋ]

词根 • pierce(刺穿 ，穿透 )+ing(adj .)→穿透的

派生 • pierce v. 刺穿 ，穿透

例句 • Units will include maintaining employment standards, salon management duties, providing facial massage and skin care, instruction on make-up, lash and brow treatments, artificial nail structures and ear piercing . (IELTS4,TA,R2) 内容包括遵守雇佣标准 ，沙龙管理责任 ，提供面部按摩和皮肤护理 ，指导化妆 、修理眉毛和睫毛 、安装假指甲和穿耳洞 。

pinprick [’pɪnˌprɪk]

例句 • This doesn’ t require a prohibitive amount of energy: a male’ s tiny pinprick of light can be seen by a female from some distance on a dark night … (IELTS7,T1,R1) 这不需要多大的能量 ：在漆黑的夜晚 ，一只雄性萤火虫身上发出的针尖大小的亮光都可以被一定距离外的雌性看到 。

plagiarise [’pleɪdʒəraɪz]

派生 • plagiarism n. 剽窃 ，抄袭

plagiarist n. 剽窃者 ，抄袭者

例句 • How to incorporate it into your own work in an acceptable way. How not to plagiarise other people’ s articles, books etc. (IELTS6,TB,R2) 怎样以可接受的方式将它运用到你自己的作品中 ，怎样不抄袭他人的文章 、书籍等 。

playmate [’pleɪmeɪt]

plight [plaɪt]

同义 • difficulty, dilemma

例句 • The plight of the rainforests has largely been ignored by the media. (IELTS4,T1,R2)雨林所处的困境已经完全被媒体忽略了 。

plunge [plʌndʒ]

释义 • v. to cast or thrust forcibly or suddenly into something, as a liquid, a penetrable substance, a place, etc.; immerse; submerge 跳入

例句 • Tanya Streeter’ s passion is freediving—the sport of plunging deep into the water without tanks or other breathing equipment. (IELTS10,T4,R2)Tanya Streeter的兴趣是自由潜水 ——一项不携带氧气箱或其他呼吸设备而直接潜入深水中的运动 。

plush [plʌʃ]

释义 • adj. luxuriously smart 豪华的；漂亮的

例句 • They investigated chic so-called boutique hotels in the heart of downtown business districts, stately mansions located in the depths of beautiful countryside, and plush hotels built at the edge of tropical beaches surrounded by palm trees and idyllic blue ocean. (IELTS7,T3,L4) 他们调查了商业区中心的所谓的华丽宾馆 ，坐落在美丽郊区的高档别墅 ，以及建在热带海边上 、有棕榈树和蓝色海水环绕的豪华酒店 。

poised [pɒɪzd]

释义 • adj. in a state of physical tension, ready for action (指人、动物等)身体处于紧张状态；准备行动

派生 • poise n. 姿势 ，动作

例句 • After years in the wilderness, the term “artificial intelligence” (AI) seems poised to make a comeback. (IELTS5,T3,R3) 被人们遗忘了几年之后 ，“人工智能”这个术语似乎已经准备好要卷土重来了 。

poisoning [’pɒɪzənɪŋ]

派生 • poison3 n. 毒药

poisonous adj. 有毒的

例句 • One cost is to human health, every year some 10,000 people die from pesticide poisoning , almost all of them in the developing countries, and another 400,000 become seriously ill. (IELTS3,T2,R2) 使用杀虫剂的一个代价就是危害人类的健康 ， 每年大概有一万人死于杀虫剂中毒 ， 而这几乎都发生在发展中国家 ， 另外还有四十万人严重中毒 。

pole [pəʊl]

派生 • polar3 adj. 极地的

例句 • Nunavut is 1.9 million square kilometres of rock and ice, and a handful of islands around the North Pole . (IELTS6,T1,R3) 努勒维特面积为 190万平方千米 ，由石块 、冰块以及北极附近的一些岛屿组成 。

poll [pəʊl]

释义 • n. a survey of public opinion by putting questions to a representative selection of people 民意测验

例句 • Yet opinion polls suggest that many people nurture the belief that environmental standards are declining and four factors seem to cause this disjunction between perception and reality. (IELTS5,T1,R3) 然而民意调查显示 ，很多人认为环境标准在下降 ，似乎有四个因素导致了这种观念和现实之间的差距 。

populace [’pɒpjələs]

词根 • popul(人 )+ace(n .)→平民 ，百姓

popular adj. 受人们欢迎的 ，流行的

popularize v. 使受欢迎

例句 • Although the exhibition officially charts the years 1906 to 1914, graphic display boards outlining the bills of enfranchisement of 1918 and 1928, which gave the adult female populace of Britain the vote, show what was achieved. (IELTS3,T4,R2) 虽然展览记述的正式时间是 1906年到 1914年 ，但是图片展示板介绍了 1918至 1928年的自由选举法案 ，这个法案让英国普通成年女性获得了选举权 ，图片展板同时也展示了所取得的成就 。

porous [’pɔːrəs]

释义 • adj. allowing liquid or air to pass through, esp. slowly 能使液体或气体(尤指缓慢地)穿透的，能渗透的

派生 • pore n. 毛孔 ，气孔 ，小孔

例句 • Some processed meats, such as sausages, have non-porous casings. (IELTS7,TA,R1) 一些加工过的肉类 ，例如香肠 ，是无孔密封包装的 。

portrayal [pɔː’treɪəl]

释义 • n. the action of portraying 画像；描述，描写 ；description or representation 临摹

词根 • por(前面 )+tray(画 )+al(n .)→画像

派生 • portray4 v. 画像 ；描绘

portrait n. 画像 ，肖像

例句 • However far from reality such portrayals are, they capture the essential truth that archaeology is an exciting quest—the quest of knowledge about ourselves and our past. (IELTS4,T4,R2) 不论这样的画像和现实有多大差别 ，他们都抓住了最本质的东西 ，那就是考古学是一种激动人心的探索 ，它探寻着我们自己和我们的过去 。

pragmatic [præg’mætɪk]

释义 • adj. treating things in a sensible and realistic way; concerned with practical results 务实的，实事求是的，注重实效的

派生 • pragmatically adv. 务实地 ，实事求是地

pragmatism n. 实用主义

pragmatist n. 实用主义者

例句 • The impetus behind the development of these early plastics was generated by a number of factors—immense technological progress in the domain of chemistry, coupled with wider cultural changes, and the pragmatic need to find acceptable substitutes for dwindling supplies of “luxury” materials such as tortoiseshell and ivory. (IELTS5,T2,R1) 推动早期塑料发展的因素有很多 ：化学领域的巨大技术进步 ，文化的巨大变化 ，找到取代龟壳和象牙这类日益减少的 “奢侈”材料的现实需要 。

precarious [prɪ’keərɪəs]

释义 • adj. depending on chance; uncertain 不确定的 ；unsteady; unsafe 不稳固的；不安全的

词根 • prec(祈祷 )+arious(adj .)→祈求平安的 →不确定的

派生 • precariously adv. 不稳定地

同义 • insecure

例句 • They live in precarious balance with one of the toughest environments on earth. Climate change, whatever its causes, is a direct threat to their way of life. (IELTS6,T1,R3) 他们住在地球上环境最恶劣 、最不安全的地方 。不管什么原因引起的气候的变化都会对他们生活方式造成直接的威胁 。

precedent [’presɪdənt]

preceding adj. 在前的 ，在先的

predicate [’predɪkɪt]

例句 • The “Missouri” programme was predicated on research showing that working with the family, rather than bypassing the parents, is the most effective way of helping children get off to the best possible start in life. (IELTS5,T3,R1) “密苏里”项目断言 ，对孩子最好最有效的早期教育是与家庭合作 ，而不是绕开父母 。

predominate [prɪ’dɒməneɪt]

preferably [’prefərəblɪ]

释义 • adv. rather than anything, anywhere, etc. else 更好地，更合适地，更可取地

词根 • pre(之前 )+fer(拿 )+abl(e)(adj .)+(l)y(adv .)→更可取地

派生 • prefer23 v. 更喜欢

preferable adj. 更可取的 ，更称心的

preference5 n. 喜爱 ，偏爱 ；优惠 ，优待

例句 • If you always study in the same place, preferably a room of your own, you will find it easier to adjust mentally to the activity when you enter that area. (IELTS4,TB,R2) 如果你总是在一个地方学习 ，尤其是在你自己的房间里 ，你会发现进入那个环境后 ，你能更快调整好心态来学习 。

premature [ˌpremə’tjʊə]

释义 • adj. happening before the proper or expected time 提前的；过早的；未到期的 ；acting or done too soon; hasty 仓促的

词根 • pre(提前 ，之前 )+mature(成熟 )→提前成熟的

派生 • prematurely adv. 过早地 ；草率地

搭配 • be premature in doing sth. 仓促做某事

例句 • premature implementation (IELTS5,T3,R3) 仓促执行

premium [’priːmɪəm]

释义 • n. an additional payment, e.g. one added to wages or interest payments; bonus 奖金；额外费用 ；an amount or instalment (to be) regularly paid for an insurance policy 保险费
