同义 • bonus, reward

搭配 • put/place a premium on sth. 奖励 /鼓励 /助长某事

例句 • Furthermore, the price premium would put the produce out of reach of many poorer consumers. (IELTS7,T2,R2) 而且 ，额外费用导致很多不富裕的消费者根本买不起这个 产品 。

preoccupation [priːˌɒkjə’peɪʃən]

释义 • n. a state of being preoccupied; absent-mindedness 占据思想 ；a state of constantly thinking or worrying about sth.; obsession 全神贯注；缠在心头

词根 • pre(提前 ，之前 )+ oc(at在 ……地方 )+cup(y)(seize逮住 ，抓住 )+ ation (n .)→全神贯注

派生 • preoccupy v. 先占 ，先取 ；全神贯注于

preoccupied adj. 全神贯注的 ；心事重重的

例句 • We’ ve seen that the preoccupation in Western society with crime and with lawlessness is part of a long and continuous tradition, rather than something which is new and unique to modern society. (IELTS4,T2,L4) 我们看到西方社会关注犯罪和违法现象 ，这是他们长久以来的传统的一部分 ，而不是现代社会新出现的 、特有的东西 。

prepay [priː’peɪ]

释义 • v. to pay (sth.) in advance 预付

词根 • pre(提前 ，之前 )+pay(支付 )→预付

派生 • prepayment n. 预付

例句 • Users prepay for Library, Computer Lab or SRC (Student Representative Council) services by adding value to their Prepaid Services Card. (IELTS4,TB,R2) 使用者通过向他们的预支服务卡内充值来提前支付费用给图书馆 、计算机实验室或是学生代表委员会 。

presently [’prezəntlɪ]

释义 • adv. after a short time; soon 不久，立刻 ；at the present time; now 现在，目前

词根 • pre(在 ……前面 )+sent (存在 )+ly (adv .)→现在 ，目前

例句 • You can take up this opportunity if you are：… presently enrolled, or finishing this year, or you have deferred a year of study. (IELTS5,TA,R2)以下情况你可以获得这个机会 ：目前注册在校 ，或即将毕业 ，或延期一年 。

pretender [prɪ’tendə]

释义 • n. a person whose claim (to a throne, title, etc.) is disputed 觊觎高位者

词根 • pre (在 ……之前 )+tend(拉伸 ，延伸 )+er(n .)→把胳膊伸到上级之前 →觊觎高位者

派生 • pretend1 v. 假装 ；自称 ，自命

pretension n. 自命不凡 ；虚荣

pretentious adj. 自负的 ，自命不凡的

例句 • We’ ve had a tradition of doctors being fairly powerful and I guess they are pretty loath to allow any pretenders to their position to come into it. (IELTS4,T2,R2) 我们的一个传统是医生很有权利 ，我猜想他们很不愿意让任何觊觎他们职位的人走上医生岗位 。

preventative [prɪ’ventətɪv]

释义 • adj. preventing or intended to prevent sth.; precautionary 预防的

词根 • pre(在 ……之前 )+vent(来 )+ative (adj .)→在来之前的 →预防的

派生 • prevent10 v. 阻止 ，预防

preventable3 adj. 可预防的

prevention14 n. 预防 ，阻止

例句 • Dr. Patrick Store, President of the Royal College of General Practitioners, concurs that orthodox doctors could learn a lot about bedside manner and advising patients on preventative health from alternative therapists. (IELTS4,T2,R2) 皇家全科医师学会会长帕瑞克 · 斯托博士同意这样的观点 ：传统医生可以从非传统医生那学到很多知识 ，比如如何对待病人 ，以及如何在预防疾病方面给予病人一些建议 。

primal [’praɪməl]

释义 • adj. first or original; primeval 最初的，原始的 ；chief or most important; fundamental; primary 主要的，首要的

词根 • prim(e)(第一 ，首要 )+al (adj .)→首要的

派生 • prime n. 最初 ；第一 ，首要

同义 • primary, fundamental, main, primitive, principal

例句 • One’ s first inclination might be to argue that there must be some sort of built-in animal aggression instinct that was activated by the experiment, and that Milgram’ s teacher-subjects were just following a genetic need to discharge this pent-up primal urge onto the pupil by administering the electrical shock. (IELTS5,T1,R2) 有人一开始也许会倾向于这样的论点 ：某种动物内在的攻击本能通过实验会被激发出来 ，Milgram实验中的被试教师群体只是出于某种本能通过电击的方式向学生释放出这种被压抑的原始动力 。

pristine [’prɪsti:n]

释义 • adj. of or relating to the earliest period or state; primitive 原始的

同义 • primitive

例句 • But the Archaeological Survey of India began restoring it in the 1960s, and today it is in pristine condition. (IELTS10,T1,R1)但是印度考古局在20世纪60年代开始修复工作 ，现在已经恢复到最初的状态 。

privacy [’prɪvəsɪ]

释义 • n. the freedom from interference or public attention 私人权利；个人自由，隐私

词根 • priv(私有的 )+acy(n .)→隐私

派生 • private adj. 私人的 ，私有的

privately adv. 私下地 ，悄悄地

搭配 • achieve privacy 拥有隐私 ，得以独处

disturb privacy 打扰某人的清净

infringe on one’ s privacy 侵犯某人的隐私

in / with privacy 私下地 ，秘密地

例句 • The house and its grounds became the family haven and their escape to privacy and quiet. (IELTS6,T3,L2) 这间房子和它的院子成了这一家人的憩息处 ，是他们远离喧扰 、享受私人空间和宁静的处所 。

probe [prəʊb]

释义 • n. the act of probing探索，调查 ；a tool for examining a place whichcannot be reached otherwise, esp. a thin implement with a blunt end used by a doctor for examining a wound 探针，探测器 v. to investigate or examine (sth.) closely 探索 ；to explore or examine (sth.) with or as if with a probe 用探针(或探测器等)探查，探测

例句 • This has prompted some researchers to argue that the future lies not in collecting more evidence for telepathy, but in probing possible mechanisms. (IELTS8,T1,R3) 这促使一些研究者们开始争论未来不在于收集更多的心理感应的证据 ，而在于探索可能的机制 。

processor [’prəʊsesə]

释义 • n. one that processes, especially an apparatus for preparing, treating, or converting material 加工者，处理器

词根 • pro(向前 )+ cess(go走 )+or(n .)→处理器

派生 • process n. /v. 进程 ，过程 ；处理 ，加工

例句 • HNC claim that their system, based on a cluster of 30 processors , could be used to spot camouflaged vehicles on a battlefield or extract a voice signal from a noisy background … (IELTS5,T3,R3) HNC声称他们的系统建立在由 30个处理器组成的集群上 ，可以用来识别战场上经过伪装的车辆 ，或从一个嘈杂的背景中识别某个声音信号 ……

procrastination [prəˌkræstə’neɪʃən]

释义 • n. procrastinating 拖延，耽搁；因循

派生 • procrastinate v. 拖延 ，耽搁 ；因循

同义 • delay, postponement

习语 • Procrastination is the thief of time. 拖延就是浪费时间 。

例句 • Two of the key components of the course are time management and overcoming procrastination . (IELTS4,T3,L3) 这门课程的两个主要内容是管理时间和克服拖拉的习惯 。

procurement [prə’kjʊəmənt]

释义 • n. the act of procuring, or obtaining or getting by effort, care, or the use of special means 采购

例句 • In recent years, the Southern California region has improved building codes, evacuation procedures, and procurement of new technology. (IELTS10,T4,R1)近年来 ，南加利福尼亚地区已经完善了建筑条例 、疏散程序和新技术的采购 。

prodigious [prə’dɪdʒəs]

释义 • adj. very great in size, amount or degree, so as to cause amazement or admiration; enormous 巨大的，(在体积、 数量或程度上)大得令人惊叹

派生 • prodigiously adv. 令人吃惊地

例句 • Prodigious efforts, accelerated during two world wars, were required before the technology of primitive rocketry could be translated into the reality of sophisticated astronauts. (IELTS3,T1,R1) 把火箭技术转化成训练有素的宇航员 ，人们需要付出极大的努力 ，这种努力在两次世界大战中加速了进程 。

profitably [’prɒfɪtəblɪ]

释义 • adv. bringing profit or advantage; beneficial 可获利润或好处地，有利可图地，有益地

词根 • pro(往前 )+fit(做 )+able(能够 )+ly(adv .)→能够继续做下去的 →有利的

派生 • profit3 n. 利益 ，利润 ，好处

profitable5 adj. 有利可图的 ，有益的

同义 • advantage, benefit, gain, bonus

搭配 • make profit 获利

profit by/from 从 ……中获利

例句 • profitably moved from road to light rail transport system (IELTS6,T2,R1)从公路运输转向轻轨运输可以获利

progressively [prə’gresɪvlɪ]

释义 • adv. increasingly; by degrees 逐渐地，逐步地

词根 • pro(向前 )+gress(走 )+ive(adj .)+ly(adv .)→前进性地 →逐渐的

派生 • progress v. 前进 ，进展

progressive adj. 前进的 ，进步的 ，有进展的

progression n. 进展 ，进程 ，进步

例句 • In the next two stages, sleep gets progressively deeper. (IELTS5,TA,R3) 在之后的两个阶段里 ，睡眠逐渐变得越来越沉 。

prohibitive [prə’hɪbɪtɪv]

释义 • adj. intended to or tending to prevent the use or purchase of sth. 禁止的 ；so high that one cannot afford to buy (指价格等)高得买不起的

派生 • prohibit v. 禁止 ，阻止

prohibition n. 禁止 ，禁令

prohibitively1 adv. 禁止地

例句 • This doesn’ t require a prohibitive amount of energy: a male’ s tiny pinprick of light can be seen by a female from some distance on a dark night … (IELTS7,T1,R1) 这不需要多大的能量 ：在漆黑的夜晚 ，一只雄性萤火虫身上发出的针尖大小的亮光都可以被一定距离外的雌性看到 ……

projector [prə’dʒektə]

释义 • n. a piece of equipment for projecting photographs or films/movies onto a screen 投影机，幻灯机，放映机

词根 • pro(向前 )+ject(投掷 )+or(n .)→向前投 →投影机

派生 • project v./n. 投射 ；设计 ；方案 ，计划

projection2 n. 投影 ，发射 ；设计 ，计划

例句 • the film projector (IELTS6,T2,L1) 电影放映机

proliferate [prə’lɪfəreɪt]

释义 • v. to increase rapidly in numbers 激增 ；to produce new growth or offspring rapidly; multiply (迅速)繁殖，增生，扩散

派生 • proliferation n. 扩散

例句 • Temperatures climbed more rapidly in the twentieth century as the use of fossil fuels proliferated and greenhouse gas levels continued to soar. (IELTS8,T2,R2) 由于化石燃料的使用量猛增以及温室气体排放量的增加 ，20世纪温度上升得更迅速 。

prominence [’prɒmənəns]

释义 • n. the state of being prominent 突出，明显；卓越；重要

词根 • pro(向前 )+min(突出 )+ence(n .)→向前突出 →卓越

派生 • prominent adj. 突出的 ，显著的 ；重要的

例句 • Given the prominence of scientific English today, it may seem surprising that no one really knew how to write science in English before the 17th century. (IELTS5,T2,R3)鉴于科学英语在今天的重要性 ，可能人们会很惊讶 ，在 17世纪以前 ，居然没有人知道怎样用英语来记述科学 。

pronunciation [prəˌnʌnsɪ’eɪʃən]

释义 • n. the way in which a language is spoken 发音，读音；宣告

词根 • pro(向前 )+nunci(报告 )+ation(n .)→宣告 ；发音

派生 • pronounce v. 发音 ；宣布

例句 • Often, the researcher wishes to obtain information about just a single variable, in which case a restricted set of questions may be used: a particular feature of pronunciation , for example, can be elicited by asking the informant to say a restricted set of words. (IELTS4,T3,R3)通常 ，研究者希望获得关于某个单音的信息 ，这时他们可能会使用一套严格的问题 ：如通过让被调查者说一组固定的词语来推导其发音特点 。

prop [prɒp]

释义 • v ./n . a rigid support, esp. a piece of wood, used to prevent sth. from falling or sagging 支柱，支撑

同义 • support, back

例句 • A long cylindrical tube was propped up by two sticks and fastened to the top of the launcher, thereby allowing the rockets to be inserted and lit from the other end. (IELTS3,T1,R1) 一个长长的圆柱形的管道由两根棍子支撑着 ，并被系在发射器的顶部 ，这样便可以让火箭从一头插入并在另一头被点燃 。

propellant [prə’pelənt]

释义 • n. a propelling agent, e.g. an explosive that propels a bullet from a weapon, a fuel that provides thrust for a rocket, or compressed gas that forces out the contents of an aerosol container 推进剂；推动者

词根 • pro(向前 )+pell(驱使 )+ant(n .)→向前推进的人 →推动者

派生 • propel v. 推进 ，驱使

propulsion n. 推进 (力 )

propulsive adj. 推进的 ，有推进力的

propeller1 n. 螺旋桨，推进器

例句 • A rocket motor’ s ‘ bullets’ are minute, high-speed particles produced by burning propellants in a suitable chamber. (IELTS3,T1,R1) 火箭的推动子弹是一些微小的高速粒子 ，这些粒子是由推进剂在某个合适的空间内燃烧生成的 。

prospectus [prə’spektəs]

释义 • n. a printed document, leaflet, etc. giving details of and advertising sth., e.g. a private school or a new business 企业计划书，内容说明书；简介，广告宣传手册

词根 • pro(向前 )+spect(看 )+us(n .)→向前看 →计划书

派生 • prospect2 n. 前途 ，希望 ；预料

prospective adj. 预期的 ，未来的 ；可能的

例句 • So, Andrew, have you seen our diploma course prospectus yet? (IELTS5,T1,L3)安德鲁 ，你看见我们的毕业课程计划书了吗 ？

proximity [prɒk’sɪmɪtɪ]

释义 • n. nearness in space or time; closeness 邻近，接近

词根 • proxim(接近 )+ity(n .)→邻近

搭配 • proximity of blood 近亲

in (the) proximity to 在 ……附近 ，靠近

例句 • Proximity to the city is an issue… (IELTS4,T1,L3) 靠近城市是一个问题 ……

proxy [’prɒksɪ]

释义 • n. the authority to represent sb. else 代表权，代理权(尤指投票) ；a person authorized to act on behalf of another 代理人，代表

例句 • For the time before records began, we have only proxy records’ reconstructed largely from tree rings and ice cores, supplemented by a few incomplete written accounts. (IELTS8,T2,R2) 在记录开始之前 ，我们只有一些 “替代记录”，而这些记录主要来自年轮和冰芯 ，再加上一些不完整的手写记录构成 。

puff [pʌf]

释义 • n. a short light blowing of breath or wind 一口气，一阵风，一阵喷烟；喷气，喘气

派生 • puffy adj. 膨胀的 ；肿胀的

例句 • Passive smoking, the breathing in of the side-stream smoke from the burning of tobacco between puffs or of the smoke exhaled by a smoker, also causes a serious health risk. (IELTS3,T1,R2) 被动吸烟 ，即吸入正在燃烧着的香烟烟雾或者其他吸烟者吐出的烟雾 ，同样也会严重危害健康 。

pulse [pʌls]

释义 • n. the regular beating of the arteries as blood is pumped through them by the heart, esp. as felt at the wrist 脉搏 ；a single vibration of sound, light, electric current, etc. 脉冲波 v. to move with strong regular movements; beat or throb 强烈而有规律地跳动，搏动，振动

例句 • So within any one area each species will differ from its neighbours in some way, for example in the colour or pattern of its light, how long the pulses of light last, the interval between pulses and whether it displays in flight or from the ground. (IELTS5,TB,R3) 因此在任何一个区域内每一个物种 (萤火虫 )发出的光和它周围的物种都是不一样的 ，例如光的色彩和形式 ，发光的持续时间 ，两次发光之间的间歇时间 ，以及它是在飞行中发光还是在伏地不动时发光等 。

pulverised [’pʌlvəˌraɪzd]

释义 • adj. grind or smash (sth.) to powder or dust 被粉碎的，被摧毁的

词根 • pulver(粉末 )+ise(v .)+(e)d(adj .)→被摧毁的

派生 • pulverise v. 将 (某物 )磨成粉或捣成末 ；粉碎 ，摧毁

例句 • Superclean coal has the potential to enhance the combustion efficiency of conventional pulverised fuel power plants. (IELTS3,TA,R3) 超净煤有可能会提高传统电厂粉末燃料的燃烧效率 。

puncture [’pʌŋktʃə]

释义 • v. to make a puncture in 在(某物)上穿孔；刺穿 ；n. a small hole made by a sharp point, esp. one made accidentally in a tyre 孔，洞

同义 • pierce

例句 • Kant and Freud felt that joke-telling relies on building up a psychic tension which is safely punctured by the ludicrousness of the punchline. (IELTS5,T2,R2) 康德和弗洛伊德感到讲笑话依赖于建立一种精神紧张状态 ，而这又被笑话的荒诞结尾给打破 。

puppetry [’pʌpɪtrɪ]

释义 • n. the art of making and handling puppets 制作木偶或演木偶剧的技艺

派生 • puppet4 n. 玩偶 ，木偶

puppeteer3 n. 演木偶剧的人 ，操纵木偶的人

例句 • Now, water puppetry is amazing! (IELTS4,T3,L2) 现在 ，水中木偶技艺令人惊叹 ！

purist [’pjʊərɪst]

释义 • n. a person who pays great attention to correctness, esp. in the use of language or in the arts 纯粹主义者，力求纯正的人

词根 • pure(纯净的 )+ist(n .)→纯粹主义者

派生 • purify1 v. 使纯净 ，净化

purity n. 纯净

例句 • The purists are suggesting that this isn’ t a circus at all. (IELTS4,T3,L2) 纯粹主义者表示这根本就不是马戏表演 。

purse [pɜːs]

释义 • n. a small bag for money 小钱袋，小钱包 ；the money available for spending; funds or resources 备用款；资金 ；a sum of money collected and given as a gift or prize 财源；款项

习语 • hold the purse-strings 控制开支

例句 • It is also accepted that this right generates an obligation or duty for the state to ensure that adequate health-care resources are provided out of the public purse . (IELTS4,T4,R3) 这项权利使得政府有义务或责任从公用款中拨出足够的资金来保证民众的健康医疗 ，这一点是被认可的 。

pyrotechnics [ˌpaɪrəʊ’teknɪks]

释义 • n. the art of making fireworks 烟火制造术 ；a public display of fireworks as an entertainment 放烟火，放烟花

词根 • pyro(火 )+technics(技术 )→烟火制造技术

例句 • Prior to this, rockets were used only in pyrotechnic displays. (IELTS3,T1,R1) 在这之前 ，火箭只是用于燃放烟火的表演中 。

quest [kwest]

释义 • n . a long search for sth., especially for some quality such as happiness 寻求，寻找 v . to search for sth. that is difficult to find 寻找；探索

同义 • search, pursuit, exploration

搭配 • in request of 为了寻求 ，为了探索

例句 • However far from reality such portrayals are, they capture the essential truth that archaeology is an exciting quest —the quest of knowledge about ourselves and our past. (IELTS4,T4,R2)不管这些画像离现实多么遥远 ，他们都抓住了最本质的东西 ，那就是考古学是一种令人激动的探索 ，它探寻着我们自己和我们的过去 。

quiz [kwɪz]

释义 • n. a competition, esp. on TV or radio, in which people try to answer questions to test their knowledge 竞赛，比赛

派生 • quizzical adj. 疑问的 ，探询的

例句 • Entertainment is laid on nearly every night with tour leaders on hand to organise lectures, games, quizzes and respond to any special requests from guests. (IELTS4,T4,L2)几乎每晚都有娱乐节目 ，领队的人会组织一些讲座 、游戏 、竞赛问答等 ，并回应客人的各种特殊要求 。

quoted [’kwəʊtɪd]

释义 • adj. repeat in speech or writing 引用的，引述的

派生 • quote7 v. 引用 ，引述 ，引证

quotation2 n. 引用 ，引述 ，引证

同义 • cite, mention

搭配 • quote from引用 ，引证

例句 • Which column of the bar chart represents the figures quoted ? (IELTS3,T1,L1)哪一列柱形图代表被引用的数字 ？

random [’rændəm]

释义 • adj. proceeding, made, or occurring without definite aim, reason, or pattern 任意的；随机的

例句 • Silent genes accumulate random mutations, they reasoned, eventually rendering them useless. (IELTS10,T4,R3)他们推理 ，隐性的基因不断发生随机的突变 ，最后使它们失去作用 。

rash [ræʃ]

释义 • adj. acting or done without careful consideration of the possible consequences; impetuous 急躁的，鲁莽的，轻率的 n. a sudden widespread appearance of sth. unpleasant (a rash of) 频发，连续发生

例句 • Over the following decade the 40-storey Brisbane block suffered a rash of failures. (IELTS5,T4,R2) 在接下来的 10年里 ，四十层的 Brisbane街区连续发生倒塌事件 。

rationale [ˌræʃə’naːl]

释义 • n. the fundamental reason for or logical basis of sth. 基本原理，理论基础的说明，原理的阐述

例句 • I want to talk about the rationale behind what I decided to do. (IELTS8,T2,L4) 我想讲一下我决定要做事情的基本原理 。

reactive [rɪ’æktɪv]

释义 • adj. characterized by reaction 反应的

词根 • re(又 ，再 )+act(作用 )+ive(adj. )→再次作用的 →反应的

派生 • reactant1 n. 反应物

react v. 对 ……反应

reaction n. 反作用力 ；反应

例句 • High levels of serotonin in certain areas of the nervous system make people more active and reactive and, possibly, more aggressive. (IELTS3,T3,R3) 神经系统中某些区域的复核胺含量越多 ，人就会越活跃 ，反应越快 ，或者可能越好斗 。

realm [relm]

释义 • n. a country ruled by a king or queen 王国，国土 ；a field/sphere of activity or interest领域

例句 • It is strange that the rocket was generally ignored by writers of fiction to transport their heroes to mysterious realms beyond the Earth. (IELTS53,T1,R1) 奇怪的是 ，科幻作家们在书中很少用火箭把他们的英雄送到地球之外的神秘世界 。

reassure [ˌriːə’ʃʊə]

释义 • v. to remove sb’ s fears or doubts; to make sb. confident again 使……安心，再保证，使……恢复信心

词根 • re(→ again再 )+as(→to朝向 )+sur(安全的 )→ 使 ……安心 ，再保证

例句 • What should I do in this period, keep in touch with you and reassure you? (IELTS5,T3,L2) 在这个时候我应该做些什么来跟你保持联系并且使你放心呢 ？

rebound [rɪ’baʊnd]

释义 • v . to bounce back after hitting sth. 弹回;反弹 n . a ball that hits sth. and bounces back 反弹球；回弹球

词根 • re(又 ，再 )+bound(弹跳 ，跳跃 )→反弹

例句 • It’ s a mass extinction, and whether we will ever rebound from the loss is difficult to know. (IELTS4,T2,L1) 我们的损失惨重 ，至于能否挽回损失还很难说 。

recede [rɪ’si:d]

释义 • v . to go or move away; retreat; go to or toward a more distant point; withdraw 后退

词根 • re（往后 ）+cede（走 ）→往后走 →后退

派生 • recession n . 衰退

例句 • As their name suggests, stepwells comprise a series of stone steps descending from ground level to the water source (normally an underground aquifer) as it recedes following the rains. (IELTS10,T1,R1)正如其名所示 ，阶梯井由一系列石头台阶组成 ，这些石阶从地平线一直延伸到水源 （通常是地下蓄水层 ），下雨时台阶就缩短了 。

reciprocity [ˌresə’prɒsɪtɪ]

释义 • n. the principle or practice of mutual exchange, esp. of making concessions or granting privileges, etc. in return for concessions or privileges received 相互作用，相互性；互给，互惠

派生 • reciprocal2 adj. 相互的 ，往复的

reciprocate v. 互换 ，互给

例句 • He points out that play often involves complex assessments of playmates, ideas of reciprocity and the use of specialised signals and rules. (IELTS4,T2,R3) 他指出 ，玩耍通常包括对玩伴复杂的评价 、互惠的想法和专门的信号和规则的运用 。

reclaim [rɪ’kleɪm]

释义 • v. to recover (raw material) from waste products 要求收回 ；to make (land) suitable for cultivation, e.g. by draining or irrigating it 开拓(荒地)，开垦；纠正 ；to win sb. back or away from sin, error, etc; reform sb. 教化，改造

词根 • re(back)+claim(喊叫 )→喊回来 →要求收回

例句 • Several hundred pieces of baggage are rushed from the plane onto a conveyor belt in the baggage reclaim annexe. (IELTS7,TA,R3) 几百个包裹被从飞机上匆匆地卸下来 ，并随后放到包裹回收附属物的传送带上 。

-claim:

claim v. 要求，声称

exclaim v. 呼喊，惊叫，大声说

proclaim v. 宣告，宣布，声明

disclaim v. 放弃（权力），否认（责任）

acclaim v. 欢呼，喝彩

recourse [’rɪ’kɔːs]

释义 • n. the possible source of help, e.g. in an emergency 求助的对象

词根 • re(back)+course(流 )→流回 →求助

搭配 • have recourse to 依靠 ，求助于

例句 • But a linguist’ s personal judgements are often uncertain, or disagree with the judgements of other linguists, at which point recourse is needed to more objective methods of enquiry, using non-linguists as informants. (IELTS4,T3,R3) 但是语言学家的个人判断通常是不确定的 ，或者与其他语言学家的判断有差别 。这时就需要求助于更加客观的询问方法 ，将非语言学家当作信息提供者 。

rectify [’rektɪfaɪ]

释义 • v. to put (sth.) right; to correct 改正，矫正

词根 • rect(直的 )+ify(使 )→使 ……直 →纠正

例句 • It is a mistake that can take decades to rectify —and even threaten the future of a promising business. (IELTS7,TA,R2) 错误需要几十年的时间来纠正 ，甚至威胁到本来很有前途的生意 。

recur [rɪˈkɜ:(r)]

释义 • v. occur again periodically or repeatedly复发；重现；再发生；回想

词根 • re-（back）+cur（跑）→跑回来→重头来→重复

派生 • recurrence n . 再发生，反复 recurrent adj . 重发的

例句 • What’ s more, appealing pieces both abstract and representational, show signs of ‘ fractals’ — repeated motifs recurring in different scales. (IELTS11,T2,R3) 更重要的是，无论是抽象的还是具象的好作品，都显示出“分形”的迹象，即以不同的大小重复相同的主题。

referendum [ˌrefə’rendəm]

释义 • n. referring of a political issue to a general vote by all the people of a country for a decision; vote thus taken 公民投票，(外交使节)请示书

例句 • Local pressure groups forced a referendum over whether to spend the money on light rail instead. (IELTS6,T2,R1) 当地的施压组织强行举行公投来决定是否要花钱建轻轨 。

refrain [rɪ’freɪn]

释义 • v. to stop yourself from doing sth., especially sth. that you want to do 节制，避免，制止 n. a comment or complaint that is often repeated 经常重复的评价（或抱怨） ；lines of a song or poem which are repeated, esp. at the end of each verse 重复，叠句

搭配 • refrain sb. from doing sth. 制止某人做某事

例句 • “There is no bullying at this school” has been a common refrain . (IELTS6,T4,R3) “这所学校没有欺凌弱小的现象”曾经是一句常听到的话 。

regime [reɪ’ʒiːm]

释义 • n. a method or system of government 政体，政权

词根 • reg(统治 )+ime(n .)→统治

同义 • government, authorities,system

例句 • The Little Ice Age has given way to a new climatic regime , marked by prolonged and steady warming. (IELTS8,T2,R2) 小冰期已经让步给新型气候体系 ，其特点是长期和持续的变暖 。

rekindle [riː’kɪndl]

释义 • v. to light again 重新点燃

例句 • In New Zealand, classes for children have slowed the erosion of Maori and rekindled interest in the language. (IELTS4,T2,R1) 在新西兰 ，针对儿童开设的课堂减慢了毛利语的消亡 ，并重新点燃了对该语言的兴趣 。

relish [’relɪʃ]

释义 • n. great enjoyment of food, etc; zest 滋味，美味；乐趣，(大量的)享受，快乐 v. to enjoy or get pleasure out of 欣赏，享受，爱好

同义 • enjoyment, fondness, inclination

搭配 • with a relish 津津有味地 ，有趣地

例句 • Electrical manufacturers seized on its insulating properties, and consumers everywhere relished its dazzling array of shades. (IELTS5,T2,R1) 电器生产商利用了它的绝缘特性 ，而各地的消费者则喜欢它眩目的色彩 。

repatriate [riː’pætrɪeɪt]

释义 • v. to send or bring sb. back to his own country 把(某人)遣送回国，遣返

例句 • Many of the Arctic tourist destinations have been exploited by outside companies, who employ transient workers and repatriate most of the profits to their home base. (IELTS4,TA,R2) 北极的许多旅游点被外部的公司开发 ，他们雇佣临时工人 ，并把绝大部分利润汇回国内总部 。

repository [rɪ’pɒzətri]

释义 • n. a receptacle or place where things are deposited, stored, or offered for sale 仓库

例句 • As repositories of unique historical objects, art museums are often called ‘ treasure houses ’ . (IELTS10,T2,R3) 作为独特的历史遗迹仓库 ， 艺术博物馆通常被称作是 “ 财富屋 ”。

reputable [’repjətəbəl]

释义 • adj. having a good reputation; respected or trustworthy 著名的，出名的

派生 • reputation4 n. 名声 ，声望

reputed adj. 号称的 ；公认的

搭配 • be reputable for 因 ……而出名

例句 • All students complete vocational assignments which are integrated with work experience with reputable companies. (IELTS4,TA,R2) 所有的学生都完成了假期作业 ，而且都在著名公司收获了工作经验 。

resilience [rɪ’zɪlɪəns]

释义 • n. the quality of being springy 弹回；弹性，恢复力，适应力

词根 • re(again)+sil(弹 ，跳 )+ience→能弹回来 →弹性

派生 • resilient adj. 有弹性的

例句 • But this does not totally explain the great resilience of Japanese pagodas. (IELTS7,T2,R1) 但是这点不能够完全解释日本塔极大的适应性 。

resonance [’rezənəns]

释义 • n. the quality of being resonant 反响，共鸣

派生 • resonant adj. 引起共鸣的 ，响彻的

例句 • Psychologist Vinod Goel investigated humour using the new technique of single event functional magnetic resonance imaging. (IELTS5,T2,R2) 心理学家 Vinod Goel运用具有单一事件功能的磁共振成像这一新技术来研究幽默 。

reticence [’retɪsns]

释义 • n. the state of being reticent, or reserved, especially with regard to speaking freely; restraint 沉默

派生 • reticent adj . 沉默的

例句 • Inherently introverted, he realised early on that as an academic, his reticence would prove disastrous in the lecture hall. (IELTS10,T4,R2)他很早就意识到自己天生内向 ，作为一名讲师 ，自己的沉默将在讲堂上引发灾难性的后果 。

revolve [rɪ’vɒlv]

释义 • v. to go round in a circle; to rotate 旋转，环绕，转动

词根 • re(又 ，再 )+volve(卷 )→反复卷 →旋转

搭配 • revolve around 以 ……为中心

revolve round/about围绕 ……旋转

例句 • He says that while there is no single format for jokes, many revolve around a sudden and surprising conceptual shift. (IELTS5,T2,R2) 他说 ，尽管笑话没有一种固定形式 ，但是很多笑话都是以突然的 、令人惊讶的概念转换为中心的 。

rift [rɪft]

释义 • n. a split, crack, break, etc. 裂缝 v. to cause to split open or break 使裂开

例句 • Eruptions have rifted continents, raised mountain chains, constructed islands and shaped the topography of the earth. (IELTS4,T3,R2) 火山爆发使得大陆裂开 ，耸起了连绵山脉 ，建立了岛屿 ，形成了地球表面的地貌 。

rig [rɪg]

释义 • v. to fit (a ship or boat) with masts, spars, ropes, sails, etc. 给(船、桅杆)装配帆及索具

例句 • So they rigged up a tent-shaped scaffold directly above the tip of the horizontal column, with pulleys suspended from the scaffold’ s apex. (IELTS7,T4,R1) 所以他们在水平柱的顶端直接搭起帐篷状的脚手架 ，滑轮从脚手架的顶点悬挂下来 。

rigid [’rɪdʒɪd]

释义 • adj. stiff; not bending or yielding 刚硬的，僵硬的，不弯曲的 ；strict; firm; unchanging 严格的，死板的，不变的

派生 • rigidity n. 僵硬 ，死板

同义 • hard, stiff, firm; strict, hardy, hard, stern

例句 • They may have rigid rules about increasing density of development. (IELTS7,TA,R2) 他们可能会有针对发展速度的严格规定 。

rumour [’ruːmə]

释义 • n. a piece of information spread by being talked about but not certainly true 留言，谣言，传闻

记忆 • 谐音记忆 rumour可谐音为 “辱没”，被谣言所辱没 。

例句 • Productivity often suffers, as employees spend their time sharing rumours and providing one another with moral support rather than focusing on their jobs. (IELTS5,T3,R2) 当员工互传谣言 ，只是互相提供道德上的支持而不关注自己的本职工作时 ，生产率就会受损 。

sabbatical [sə’bætɪkl]

释义 • n. a period of paid leave granted to a university teacher for study or travel, traditionally one year for every seven years’ work 高校休假期，高校公休假

例句 • Staff who complete 25 years’ service can enjoy paid sabbatical leave of up to six months. (IELTS9,TA,R2) 已工作 25年的员工可以享有长达 6个月的带薪休假 。

sack [sæk]

释义 • n. any large bag of strong material used for storing and carrying e.g. cement, coal, flour, potatoes 布袋，麻袋 ；dismissal from a job 解雇 v. to dismiss (sb.) from a job; to fire 解雇

例句 • During a routine mail screen that can take hours, the dogs stay so focused that not even a postcard lined with 0.5 grams of heroin and hidden in a bulging sack of letters escapes detection. (IELTS7,TA,R3) 在持续几个小时的常规邮件检查过程中 ，狗都可以保持很好的注意力 ，隐藏在一满袋信中的含有 0.5克海洛因的明信片也逃不出它们的法眼 。

sale [seɪl]

释义 • n. the act of selling or being sold 卖，出售；销售业务；营业；推销 ；the amount sold 销售额 ；an occasion when goods are sold at lower prices than usual (尤指季节性或存货的)廉价出售

派生 • salespeople5 n. 店员 ，售货员 (无男女性之别 )；推销员

sell7 v. 卖 ，出售 ；(以 ……价格 )售出

例句 • Best available seats are on sale for￡6 from one hour before the performance for people eligible for Saver and Supersaver discounts and thirty minutes before for all other customers. (IELTS6,TB,R1)从演出开始前一小时开始 ，符合条件的观众可以买折扣和超级折扣票 ，最好的座位仅售 6英镑 ；从演出前 30分钟开始 ，其他观众可以买 6英镑的折扣票 。

salient [ˈseɪliənt]

释义 • adj. most noticeable or important 显著的，突出的

词根 • sal（跳）+-ient（adj .）→跳出来的→突出的

派生 • salience n . 突显

例句 • For example, a particular musical theme associated with an individual character or situation may be repeated at various points in a film in order to remind the audience of salient motifs or ideas. (IELTS11,T4, R2) 与某个角色或情景相关的特定的音乐主题可能在影片的不同节点反复出现，以提醒观众某些显著的主题或想法。

salon [’sælɒn]

释义 • n. a large room, such as a drawing room, used for receiving and entertaining guests 客厅，会客室；(轮船上的)交谊厅 ；a regular gathering of notable guests at the house of a lady of high society; a room used for this 名流社交聚会，沙龙

联想 • 汉语中的英译词 ，沙龙

例句 • Units will include maintaining employment standards, salon management duties, providing facial massage and skin care, instruction on make-up, lash and brow treatments, artificial nail structures and ear piercing. (IELTS4,TA,R2)内容包括遵守雇佣标准 ，沙龙管理职责 ，提供如何进行面部按摩和皮肤护理 ，指导化妆 、修理睫毛和眉毛 、指甲美容和穿耳洞 。

sampling [’sæmplɪŋ]

释义 • n. the act, process, or technique of selecting an appropriate sample 取样，抽样(检验) ；a small portion, piece, or segment selected as a sample 样品

联想 • 简单的 (simple)的样品 (sample)

派生 • sample28 n. 样品 ，货样 ；标本 ；实例 ；榜样 v. 抽样 ；尝试

例句 • For larger studies, scrupulous attention has been paid to the sampling theory employed, and in all cases, decisions have to be made about the best investigative techniques to use. (IELTS4,T3,R3)对于更大型的研究而言 ，选用的抽样理论得到了极大的重视 ，在任何情况下 ，都要对所使用的调查技术做出最好的选择 。

sanitary [’sænɪtərɪ]

释义 • adj. free from dirt or substances that may cause disease (有关)卫生的，关于(环境)卫生的；(保持)清洁的，干净的，消过毒的

词根 • sanit(健康 )+ary(……的 ，与 ……有关的 )→与健康有关的 →卫生的 ，干净的

派生 • sanitation5 n. 公共卫生 (设施 )

sanitize v. 使卫生 ，减少 ……的有害成分

同义 • clean, healthful, hygienic

例句 • Those who could afford to live in more pleasant surroundings moved out, the area became one where the vast majority of people lived in extreme poverty, and suffered from appalling sanitary conditions. (IELTS6,T1,L4)那些能够承担起更好居住环境费用的人搬走了 ，生活在这个地区的大多数人都极端贫穷 ，忍受着极度糟糕的卫生条件 。

satisfactory [ˌsætɪs’fæktərɪ]

释义 • adj. good enough for a purpose 令人满意的 ； 圆满的；符合要求的

词根 • satisfac(满意 )+ory(……的 )→满意的 →圆满的 ；符合要求的

派生 • satisfy v. 使满足 ，使满意

satisfaction4 n. 满意 ，满足 ；令人满意的事物

satisfied4 adj. 满意的 ，满足的

satisfying adj. 令人满意的

反义 • unsatisfactory

例句 • Saving languages from extinction is not in itself a satisfactory goal. (IELTS4,T2,R1)拯救濒临灭绝的语言本身并不是一个令人满意的目标 。

scamper [’skæmpə]

释义 • v. to run quickly and often playfully as children and some small animals do (孩子等)蹦蹦跳跳；(受惊的动物)奔逃；匆忙游览；浏览；涉猎

搭配 • scamper about; scamper off, scamper away

同义 • dash, hasten, hustle

例句 • In the first type, a returning scout scampered in circles, alternating to right and left, stopping occasionally to regurgitate food samples to the excited bees chasing after her. (IELTS4,TB,R3) 在第一种类型 ( 的舞蹈 ) 中 ， 侦查回来的蜜蜂会跳起圆圈形舞 ， 身体轮流向左或向右旋转 ， 而且时 不时停下来把食物样本喷射到追随她左右的兴奋的同伴身上 。

scavenge [’skævəndʒ]

释义 • v. to search for decaying flesh as food; to use decaying flesh for food (动物)食腐肉；清除污物(或垃圾) ；to search through waste for items that one can use 从……中搜寻有用之物

派生 • scavenger n. 食腐肉的动物 ；捡垃圾的人

例句 • Mostly, they swim at the bottom of the ocean, scavenging and picking up food that’ s lying on the ocean floor. (IELTS4,T3,L4)大部分时间 ，它们 (指鲨鱼 )都潜入海底 ，以那些沉入海底的腐物为食 。

scenic [’siːnɪk]

释义 • adj. having or showing beautiful natural scenery 风景优美的，天然景色的

词根 • scen(风景 、景色 )+ic(……的 ，具有 ……特性的 )→scenic (风景优美的 )

派生 • scene11 n. 景色 ，景象 ；布景 ，场景

scenery1 n. (总称 )风景 ，景色

同义 • picturesque, spectacular

例句 • Detailed guides to 15 scenic car tours that will take you onto fascinating wilderness tracks and along routes that you could otherwise have missed. (IELTS5,TA,R1) 15个汽车旅游景区的详细指南将带您到迷人的原野 ，并为您提供沿途路线 ，否则你可能迷路 。

sceptic [ˈskeptɪk]

释义 • n . a person inclined to question or doubt accepted opinions多疑者；怀疑宗教的人

派生 • skeptical adj. 怀疑论的

skepticism n. 怀疑主义

例句 • Sceptics believe that people claim to like such works simply because they are famous. (IELTS11,T2,R3) 对此持怀疑态度的人认为人们宣称喜欢这些作品仅仅是因为它们很著名。

scoop [skuːp]

释义 • n. a deep shovel-like tool used for picking up and moving grain, flour, sugar, coal, etc. 铲斗，勺子 ；a piece of news made public by a newspaper, radio station, etc. before its rivals 抢先报道的新闻 v. to lift sth. with, or as if with, a scoop 舀出 ；to act before (a rival, etc.) to get a scoop 抢在(对手等)之前的报道新闻

例句 • Studies carried out by Turner of many thousands of New and Old World specimens, both ancient and modern, suggest that the majority of prehistoric Americans are linked to Northern Asian populations by crown and root traits such as incisor shoveling (a scooping out on one or both surfaces of the tooth), single-rooted upper first premolars and triple-rooted lower first molars. (IELTS7,T3,R2) Turner对古代和现代成千上万新世界和旧世界标本进行了研究 ，研究表明史前大多数美国人与北亚洲人的牙冠和牙根相似 ，如都有门齿铲 (一个或两个牙齿表面的突出 )，单根上颌第一前臼齿和三根下颚第一大臼齿 。

scratch [skrætʃ]

释义 • v. to make marks on or in (a surface) with a sharp tool, nails, claws, etc; to make a shallow wound in (the skin) in this way 搔，抓，扒

例句 • The cleverly concealed drugs don’ t fool super-sniffer Florence, and her persistent scratching at the case alerts her handler. (IELTS7,TA,R3) 被巧妙地隐藏的毒品也瞒不过超级嗅探犬 Florence，她不断地抓咬那个箱子引起主人注意 。

scrub [skrʌb]

释义 • n. underdeveloped trees or shrubs 矮树，矮人，渺小之物 ；an act of scrubbing 用力擦洗 v. to clean sth. thoroughly by rubbing hard, esp. with a brush and soap and water (用硬刷子等)刷洗，用力刷洗，擦洗(污垢、污迹等)

搭配 • scrub away/ off/ out 擦洗掉

同义 • bush; buff, massage, polish, rub, scour

例句 • Australia’ s native dung beetles are scrub and woodland dwellers, specialising in coarse marsupial droppings and avoiding the soft cattle dung in which bush flies and buffalo flies breed. (IELTS3,T2,R1)澳大利亚当地的屎壳郎居住在矮树和灌木区中 ，专攻有袋动物的粗粒粪便 ，而并不理会那些滋生灌木丛苍蝇和水牛苍蝇的松软牛粪 。

scrupulous [’skruːpjələs]

反义 • unscrupulous

(IELTS6,T1,R1)他们与位于墨尔本的微技术公司合作研究中心合作 ，共同开发可嵌入运动员衣服或跑鞋里的微型传感器 ，用以监控心率 、排汗情况 、产生的热量以及其他可能对运动员赛跑能力造成影响的因素 。

(IELTS7,T3,R2) Turner 对古代和现代成千上万新世界和旧世界标本进行了研究 。 研究表明史前大多数美国人与北亚洲人牙冠和牙根相似 ， 如门齿铲 ( 一个或两个牙齿表面的突出 )， 单根上颌第一前臼齿和三根下颚第一大臼齿 。

(IELTS5,T1,R2)所谓的学生实际上是由 Milgram雇来的演员 ，他们通过发出一系列呻吟 、尖叫和挣扎来模仿受到电击后的反应 ，还胡乱说话 、骂骂咧咧 ，谴责实验和实验者 ，同时身体痛苦地翻滚 。

sniff [snɪf]

例句 • Then it needs a strong hunting instinct and the stamina to keep sniffing at the taxing rate of around 300 times per minute. (IELTS7,TA,R3) 它需要很强的捕猎本能 ，以及每分钟嗅 300次的耐力 。

socialism [’səʊʃəlɪzəm]

释义 • n. a set of political and economic theories advocating that a country’ s land, transport, natural resources and chief industries should be owned and controlled by the whole community or by the State, and that wealth should be equally distributed 社会主义

词根 • social (社会的 )+ism (……的主义 )→socialism (社会主义 )

派生 • social78 adj. 社会的 ，有关社会的 ；有利于交际的 ，合群的

socialize3 v. 与 ……交往 ，联谊

society66 n. 社会

sociology2 n. 社会学

sociological1 adj. 社会学 (上 )的 ；针对社会问题的

sociable adj. 合群的

例句 • Back in 1928 the British writer George Bernard Shaw wrote in his Intelligent Women’s Guide to Socialism and Capitalism that “A man is supposed to understand politics, economics and finance and is therefore unwilling to accept essential instruction.” (IELTS5,T1,S4)早在 1928年英国作家萧伯纳在 《智慧女人的社会主义与资本主义指南 》中写道 ，“人类自认为懂政治 、经济和金融 ，因此不愿意接受这方面的基本教育”。

派生 • solemn adj. 庄严的 ，严肃的

solemnity n. 庄严 ，严肃

例句 • In the first part, the music is classical (Mozart, Beethoven, Brahms) and the teacher reads the text slowly and solemnly , with attention to the dynamics of the music. (IELTS7,T1,R3) 第一部分是经典音乐 (莫扎特 、贝多芬 、勃拉姆斯 )，教师缓慢庄严地念着文本 ，并注意着音乐节奏 。

specialisation [ˌspeʃəlaɪ’zeɪʃən]

释义 • n. to develop so as to become adapted to a specific function or environment 专门化，专业化，分工

词根 • special(特殊的 ，专门的 )+ise(使 ……化 )+ation(行为 ，过程 ，结果 )→specialisation (特殊化 ，专门化 ) →分工

派生 • special70 adj. 特殊的 ，特别的 n. 特别的东西 ；特价

specialist17 n. 专家 ，行家

specially4 adv. 特别地

例句 • There will be an increasing specialisation in the marketplace, predicts Mr. Blyth, Customer Services Manager of a large UK bank. (IELTS3,TB,R3)布莱斯先生是英国一家大银行的客户服务经理 ，他预测市场将会进一步分工 。

speculate [’spekjʊleɪt]

释义 • v. to form opinions without having definite or complete knowledge or evidence; to guess 思索，沉思，猜测 ；to buy and sell goods or stocks and shares in the hope of making a profit through changes in their value, but with the risk of losing money 投机倒把，做投机生意

派生 • speculation2 n. 思索 ，沉思 ，猜测 ；投机买卖

speculative adj. 投机的 ，冒风险的 ；推理的 ，推测的

同义 • contemplate, conjecture, reflect, suppose, ponder

例句 • It has been speculated that, as the blowholes evolved and migrated to the top of the head, the neural pathways serving sense of smell may have been nearly all sacrificed. (IELTS4,T1,R3)据推测 ，当呼吸孔进化并转移到头顶时 ，为嗅觉服务的神经感官系统都退化了 。

spin [spɪn]

释义 • v. to make sth. turn round and round rapidly 旋转

例句 • Nearly one fifth of all the electricity generated worldwide is produced by turbines spun by the power of falling water. (IELTS7,T1,R2) 全世界大概五分之一的发电量是由水在下落过程中产生的力带动涡轮产生的 。

spinal [’spaɪnl]

释义 • adj. of or relating to the spine 脊柱的

词根 • spine (脊柱 )+al(……的 )→脊柱的

派生 • spine6 n. (人或动物的 )脊柱 ，脊椎

例句 • If your bed doesn’ t give enough support, back muscles and ligaments work all night trying to correct spinal alignment, so you wake up with a tired aching back. (IELTS3,T1,L4)如果您的床没有给予足够的支持 ，那么背部的肌肉和韧带整晚都试图纠正脊柱的姿势 ，所以你醒来时就会背部疲惫酸痛 。

spiral [’spaɪərəl]

释义 • n. a shape or design, consisting of a continuous curved line that winds around a central point, with each curve further away from the centre(围绕中心点的)螺旋形 adj. advancing or ascending in a continuous curve that winds round a central point 螺旋形的 v. to move in a spiral course 盘旋移动，螺旋形地上升或下降

例句 • The others would then troop out of the hive and fly in spiraling circles sniffing in the wind for the promised food. (IELTS4,TB,R3)然后其他蜜蜂成群飞出蜂窝 ，以螺旋状飞行 ，并在风中闻嗅 ，以便寻找那些探明的食品 。

splendour [’splendə]

词根 • splend(发光 )+our→ splendour(杰出 ，华丽 )

(IELTS4,TA,R3)随着观众的增多 ，对放映场地的需求随之加大 ，这就导致了20世纪20年代大电影院的出现 ，其豪华和壮观方面能与剧场和歌剧院相媲美 ，甚至超过了它们 。

sponge [spʌndʒ]

释义 • n. a piece of artificial or natural material that is soft and light and full of holes and can hold water easily, used for washing or cleaning 海绵 ；a simple sea creature with a light body full of holes, from which natural sponge is obtained 海绵动物 v. to wash sb./yourself/sth. with a wet cloth or SPONGE (用海绵或海绵状物)擦拭, 清除

联想 • 发音记忆 ：“死胖子”→海绵吸饱水像死胖子

派生 • spongy adj. 海绵似的 ，松软多孔的

释义 • adv. happening or seen only occasionally or in a few places; occurring irregularly 偶尔发生地；零星地，分散地

sprint [sprɪnt]

例句 • For the so-called power events—that require a relatively brief, explosive release of energy, like the 100-metre sprint and the long jump—times and distances have improved ten to twenty percent. (IELTS4,T4,R1)对于力量赛事而言 ——这需要一个相对短时间的爆发力 ，如 100米短跑和跳远 ——时间和距离已提高百分之十至百分之二十 。

stagnant [’stægnənt]

释义 • adj. not flowing and therefore dirty and smelling unpleasant; still and stale (尤指水)不 流动的，停滞的，有臭味的 ；showing no activity (and therefore not developing or progressing); sluggish 不发展的，不景气的

派生 • stagnate v. 停滞 ，不流动

stagnation n. 停滞

stainless [’steɪnləs]

stake [steɪk]

释义 • n. a strong wood or metal stick, pointed at one end, that can be driven into the ground, e.g. to support a young tree, as a post for a fence, etc. or as a marker 桩，柱 ；money, etc. invested by sb. in an enterprise so that he has an interest or share in it 股份；利害关系 ；money, etc. risked or gambled on the unknown result of a future event (e.g. a race, a card-game) 赌注，(用于赛马的)赌金 v. to gamble or risk (money, one’ s hopes, one’ s life, etc.) on sth. 把(金钱)押下打赌 ；to support (sth.) with a stake 用桩支撑，把……系在桩上

搭配 • at stake 在危险中 ，利害攸关

staple [’steɪpəl]

释义 • n. the main product that a country or district trades in 主要产物 ；the main or principal item or element (esp. of a diet) 主要要素；原料，主食 adj. main or principal; standard 主要的，重要的 v. sort 分类，选择

例句 • Dried cod and herring were already the staples of the European fish trade, but changes in water temperatures forced fishing fleets to work further offshore. (IELTS8,T2,R2) 鳕鱼干和鲱鱼干已经成为欧洲鱼类贸易的主要货物 ，但是水温的变化使得渔船要开往离海岸更远的地方 。

stare [steə]

惯用 • stare at 盯着 ，凝视

同义 • gaze

例句 • A different but equally impressive sight is the life-size model of Quetzalcoatlus northropi, which stares down at visitors in the Museum of Flying in Santa Monica, California. (IELTS6,TB,R3)另一种完全不同 、但同样令人印象深刻的是 Quetzalcoatlus northropi真人大小的模型 ，它俯视着加州圣莫尼卡飞行博物馆的游客 。

starkly [staːklɪ]

sticky [’stɪkɪ]

(IELTS5,T2,R1) 1885年 ，Baekelands开始对塑料感兴趣 。作为比利时一名年轻的化学专业学生 ，他着手研究酚醛树脂 ，即苯酚 (石炭酸 )结合的醛 (一种类似酒精的挥发性液体 )产生的粘性物质 。

stir [stɜː]

释义 • v. to move a spoon, etc. round and round in (a liquid or some other substance) in order to mix it thoroughly 调和，搅拌 ；to excite or arouse (a person or his feelings, etc.) 激起，使激动

搭配 • stir up 惹起 (麻烦 )，煽动 ；搅拌

例句 • For foods that cannot be stirred , e.g. pizza, the centre should be cut with a knife to test it is well heated through. (IELTS7,TA,R1) 对于比萨饼那样不能被搅拌的食物 ，必须用刀子切开中间部分来检验其是否全部受热 。

stitch [stɪtʃ]

释义 • n. a single passing of a needle and thread into and out of cloth, etc. in sewing, or into and out of skin tissue, etc. in surgery (缝纫中的)一针 ；a particular pattern of stitches or way of stitching (in sewing, knitting or crochet) 针法，织法 v. to sew sth.; to use a needle and thread to mend, join, or decorate pieces of fabric 缝，缝合，缝补

同义 • mend, sew

例句 • Liz Stuart, Martina Scott and Helen Stranger are available daily by appointment to help you with dressings, ear syringing, children’ s immunizations, removal of stitches and blood tests. (IELTS6,TA,R1)莉兹 · 斯图尔特 、玛蒂娜 · 斯科特和海伦 · 赛特让尔三位护士每天可接受预约给您敷药 、进行耳朵注射 、儿童疫苗接种 、拆线和验血 。

storm [stɔːm]

释义 • n. an occasion of violent weather conditions, with strong winds and usu. rain or snow or thunder, etc. 暴风雨 v. to capture sth. by a violent and sudden attack 猛烈攻击，突然袭击

例句 • In addition, huge quantities of water are consumed because used water from sewage pipes, storm drains and factories is merely flushed away and discharged into rivers or the sea. (IELTS6,TA,R3)另外 ，大量的水被浪费掉了 ，因为下水管 、暴雨排水道和工厂中使用过的水被直接冲走 ，然后排放到河或海中 。

stout [staʊt]

释义 • adj. rather fat; solidly built 胖的，粗壮的 ；strong and thick 粗的，结实的 ；determined, brave and resolute 坚定的，勇敢的，坚决的

联想 • 联想记忆 ：st (=stand 站 )+out( 出来 )→ 站在那 ， 小肚子都出来了 → 胖的 ， 粗壮的 ， 结实的

派生 • stoutly adv. 结实地 ；坚决地

例句 • The British rocket differed from the Indian version in that it was completely encased in a stout , iron cylinder, terminating in a conical head, measuring one meter in diameter and having a stick almost five meters long and constructed in such a way that it could be firmly attached to the body of the rocket. (IELTS3,T1,R1)英国火箭与印度火箭的不同之处在于 ，它完全隐藏在一个结实的铁制圆柱体中 ，终端是一个直径一米长的圆锥体 ，有近五米长的杆子 ，这样的结构使它可以牢牢地附着在火箭箭体上 。

straightaway [’streɪtə’weɪ]

例句 • That’ s brilliant. Thanks very much, Mrs. Collins, I’ ll send it off … straightaway . (IELTS3,T3,S3)太好了 ，非常感谢 ，柯林斯太太 ，我马上把它寄出去 。

streamline [’striːmlaɪn]

stricken [’strɪkən]

stringent [’strɪndʒənt]

stripe [straɪp]

释义 • n. a long narrow band (usu. of the same width throughout its length) on a surface that is usu. different from it in colour, material or texture (与底色不同的)条纹，条带 ；a badge (often in the shape of a V) that is worn on the uniform of a soldier, policeman, etc. as a mark of rank; chevron 军服袖子上表示军衔的条纹

派生 • striped adj. 有不同颜色条纹的

例句 • The number of stripes on your arm or pips on your shoulder is a very precise role definition which allows you to do certain very prescribed things in certain situations. (IELTS3,T2,R3)你制服袖上的条纹数或是肩章上的星星数都有极其确切的角色意义 ，它们允许你在某些情况下去履行某些明确规定的职责 。

submarine [’sʌbməriːn]

词根 • sub(在下面 )+marine(海 )→海底的

例句 • Another slight concern is submerged debris floating into the blades. (IELTS9,T3,R2) 另一个小问题就是水中的碎屑会卷入叶片 。

subordinate [sə’bɔːdɪnət]

释义 • v. to treat sth. as of lesser importance (than sth. else) 使……处于次要位置，使从属于 n. a person who is subordinate to sb else 下级 adj. lower in rank or position 下级的，下属的，从属的

词根 • sub (在下面 )+ordin (“order”顺序 )+ate →顺序在下 →使 ……处于次要位置

派生 • subordination n. 次要 ，从属

同义 • inferior, subsidiary, dependent

例句 • Indeed, if you wish to change your roles you must find some outward sign that you are doing so or you won’ t be permitted to change—the subordinate will continue to hear you as his boss no matter how hard you try to be his friend. (IELTS3,T2,R3)事实上 ，如果你希望转换角色 ，你必须设法显示出某种迹象 ，表明你正在身体力行 ，否则你将很难改变 ——你的下属将一如既往地听命于作为老板的你 ，不管你付出多少努力来争取成为他的朋友 。

subscription [səb’skrɪpʃən]

释义 • n. money donated 捐款，会员费 ；a sum of money so raised 订阅费 ；a purchase made by signed order, as for a periodical for a specified period of time or for a series of performances 订购，订阅

词根 • sub(下面 )+scription (写 ) →写下订单 →订阅

派生 • subscribe v. 订阅 ，签署

subscriber n. 赞助人 ，捐款人

例句 • subscription fee (IELTS6,T1,L1)订阅费

subtitles [’sʌbˌtaɪtlz]

释义 • n. a printed translation of the dialogue of a foreign-language film shown at the bottom of the screen (外国电影片)对白译文，字幕

联想 • “subtitles”是 “subtitle”(副标题 )的复数形式 ，把副标题置于屏幕下端 ，就是字幕 。

例句 • Unfortunately, the sound on this early film was not very good and I believe they put subtitles on the film—that is, they printed the dialogue along the bottom of the film to compensate for this poor sound quality. (IELTS6,T2,R3)不幸的是 ，这一早期电影的声音不太好 ，我相信他们给电影配上了字幕 ，也就是把对话印在胶片的底部 ，以弥补声音质量的不足 。

subtlety [’sʌtltɪ]

释义 • n. cuteness 敏锐，机敏 ；agility 巧妙，狡猾 ；the quality or state of being subtle 微妙，(常用复数)微妙的思想，细微之处

派生 • subtle6 adj. 微妙的 ，难以捉摸的 ；狡猾的 ；敏感的 ，敏锐的

例句 • It took into account subtleties of meaning. (IELTS5,T1,R1)它考虑到了意思的微妙之处 。

successive [sək’sesɪv]

释义 • adj. coming one after the other in an unbroken series 连续的

派生 • success5 v. 成功 ；接着发生

succession1 n. 连续 ，继任

同义 • consecutive, continuous, sequent

例句 • The teacher-subject was told that whenever the pupil gave the wrong answer to a question, a shock was to be administered, beginning at the lowest level and increasing in severity with each successive wrong answer. (IELTS5,T1,R2)被研究的教师被告知只要学生给出错误的答案 ，他们就按开关电击学生 ，其强度从最低级开始 ，并随着学生给出连续的错误答案而增加 。

suckle [’sʌkəl]

释义 • v. to feed (a baby or young animal) with milk from the breast or udder 给……喂奶，给……哺乳

派生 • suckling n. 乳儿 ，仍在吃奶的婴儿 ，乳畜 ，乳兽

例句 • Across species, play tends to peak about halfway through the suckling stage and then decline. (IELTS4,T2,R3) 在所有动物中 ， 玩耍的高峰期大约在哺乳期的中间 ， 之后就会下降 。

suffice [sə’faɪs]

释义 • v. to be enough (for sb./sth.); to be adequate 足够；足够……之需，使满足

词根 • suf(在下面 )+fice (做 )→在下面先做好 →准备充分 →充足

派生 • sufficient10 adj. 足够的 ，充足的

sufficiently3 adv. 足够地 ，充分地

sufficiency1 n. 足够 ，充足

insufficient1 adj. 不足的

例句 • This basic approach is limited in the range of numbers that it can express, but this range will generally suffice when dealing with the simpler aspects of human existence. (IELTS6,T2,R3)这种基本的方法受到了它可表示的数字范围的限制 ，但在此范围内处理人类生存方面的更简单问题通常是足够的 。

surrender [sə’rendə]

释义 • v. to give up possession of sth/sb when forced by others or by necessity; to hand sth./sb. over 交出，放弃 ；to stop resisting an enemy, etc; to yield; to give up 投降，屈服 n. surrendering or being surrendered 投降，认输

词根 • sur(在 ……上 )+render(给予 )→传到 ……手上 →交出 →投降

同义 • abandon, submit, yield, resign

反义 • resist

例句 • Thus, in this explanation the subject merges his unique personality and personal and moral code with that of larger institutional structures, surrendering individual properties like loyalty, self-sacrifice and discipline to the service of malevolent systems of authority. (IELTS5,T1,R2)因此 ，在该解释中 ，对象将其独特的人格以及个人和道德的准则融入更大的制度结构中 ，放弃了个人特点 ，例如忠诚 、忘我和自我约束 ，来服务于恶意的权威系统 。

survivor [sə’vaɪvə]

释义 • n. a person who has survived 幸存者，生还者

词根 • sur(在 ……下 )+vive(生命 )+or(……的人 )→在 ……下活下来的人 →幸存者 ，生还者

派生 • survive34 v. 活下来 ，幸免于

survival29 n. 幸存 ，残存

例句 • This popular half-hour science magazine continues into its twenty-ninth year, proving itself to be a hardy survivor in the television world. (IELTS5,TB,R1)这部广受欢迎的半小时科学杂志进入其第 29个发展年头 ，这证明它在电视世界的冲击下坚强地生存了下来 。

sustenance [’sʌstənəns]

sustainable21 adj. (政策 、过程等 )能持续的 ，可持续的

swap [swɒp]

释义 • v. to give sth. in exchange for sth. else; to substitute sth. for sth. else 交换 n. an act of swapping; exchange 交换，交换物

例句 • Even more impressively, DNA analysis of the fungi suggests that the ants improve or modify the fungi by regularly swapping and sharing strains with neighbouring ant colonies. (IELTS7,T3,R1) 更加令人惊奇的是 ，对真菌的 DNA分析表明 ，蚂蚁通过定期与相邻的蚂蚁王国交换和分享品系来改进或改变真菌 。

swivel [’swɪvəl]

释义 • v. to link or pivot between two parts enabling one part to revolve without turning the other 使……旋转 n. a link or pivot between two parts enabling one part to revolve without turning the other (机械的)转节，旋轴，旋转接头

例句 • Looking side-on, Mason measures the distance between strokes. From above, he analyses how her spine swivels . (IELTS6,T1,R1) 从侧面看 ，梅森测量了每一次划动之间的距离 。利用上面的数据 ，他分析了这位运动员的脊柱是怎样转动的 。

symptom [’sɪmptəm]

词根 • sym(一起 )+ptom(降临 )→一起降临到身上的东西 →生病后出现的东西 →症状

aunt [tɔːnt]

同义 • ridicule, mock, deride

例句 • Bullying can take a variety of forms, from the verbal—being taunted or called hurtful names—to the physical—being kicked or shoved—as well as indirect forms, such as being excluded from social groups. (IELTS6,T4,R3) 欺凌可以有很多形式 ：语言上的嘲弄 ，身体上的踢打或推搡 ；还有间接形式 ，如被社会团体所排挤 。

emper [’tempə]

派生 • temperament1 n. 性情 ，性格 ，气质

enable [’tenəbəl]

词根 • ten(拿住 )+able→能够拿住的 →站得住脚的

enet [’tenɪt]

erminate [’tɜːmɪneɪt]

词根 • termin(界限 )+ate→定出界限 →停止

例句 • The British rocket differed from the Indian version in that it was completely encased in a stout, iron cylinder, terminating in a conical head, measuring one metre in diameter and having a stick almost five metres long and constructed in such a way that it could be firmly attached to the body of the rocket. (IELTS3,T1,R1) 英国火箭与印度火箭的不同在于 ，前者完全密封在一个结实的铁制圆柱体中 ，其终端呈圆锥体 ，还配置了一根近五米长的杆子 ，这样的结构使它可以牢牢地附着在火箭箭体上 。

errace [’terəs]

释义 • n. a raised level area of ground or a series of these into which a hillside is shaped so that it can be cultivated 梯田 ；a continuous row of similarly designed houses in one block 一排并列的房子，阳台

词根 • terr(地 )+ace→像地一样平整的地方 →阳台

例句 • In some hill-regions, this has led to a serious decline in farm output and a change in the local diet, because there is insufficient labour to maintain terraces and irrigation systems and tend to crops. (IELTS5,T4,R1) 在一些山区 ， 这导致了农业产量的严重下降和当地饮食的改变 ， 因为没有足够的劳动力维护梯田和灌溉系统 ， 没有足够的人手照看庄稼 。

estament [’testəmənt]

hatch [θætʃ]

他们的村庄只不过是一间间茅草屋 。

haw [θɔː]

释义 • v. to change from a frozen solid to a liquid by gradual warming 解冻，融化 n. the process of thawing 解冻期，融雪期

hreshold [’θreʃhəʊld]

释义 • n. the point of entering or beginning sth. 入门 ；a point separating conditions that will produce a given effect from conditions of a higher or lower degree that will not produce the effect, as the intensity below which a stimulus is of sufficient strength to produce sensation or elicit a response 极限

例句 • The normal noise threshold for private housing is 55 decibels. (IELTS3,T4,L4) 私人住宅的正常的噪音应低于 55分贝 。

hrifty [ˈθrɪfti]

派生 • thrift n . 节俭

例句 • What is so impressive about it, however, is not its lengthiness but rather the reverse — the thrifty compactness of its construction. (IELTS11,T4,R3) 然而，它最令人印象深刻的地方并不在于它的冗长，而恰恰相反，在于它构造的简洁性。

ickle [’tɪkəl]

释义 • v. to touch or stroke (sb.) lightly, esp. at sensitive parts, so as to cause a slight tingling sensation, often with twitching movements and laughter 使发痒 ；to please 使高兴，逗乐

例句 • People laugh on fairground rides or when tickled to flag a play situation, whether they feel amused or not. (IELTS5,T2,R2) 人们在游乐场中骑马时或被抓痒到直喊投降时 ，不管快乐与否 ，都会大笑 。

orch [tɔ:tʃ]

释义 • n. a light to be carried in the hand, consisting of some combustible substance, as resinous wood, or of twisted flax or the like soaked with tallow or other flammable substance, ignited at the upper end 火把，火炬

例句 • Sometimes it was bound in grass, ignited and used as a torch by night fishermen to attract fish. (IELTS10,TA,R3)有时候 ，渔民会在晚上用草把它捆起来 ，然后点燃 ，以此当火炬来吸引鱼群 。

opple [’tɒpəl]

out [taʊt]

rance [traːns]

ranquilliser [’træŋkwəlaɪzə]

ranquility n. 宁静

ranscend [træn’send]

(IELTS7,T3,R3)这意味着森林政策是极其重要的 ，它必须超越国界和时代 ，必须考虑到森林 、需求和政策方面出现的不可避免的变化 。

ransferable [træns’fɜːrəbl]

riumphant [traɪ’ʌmfənt]

派生 • triumph2 n. 胜利 ，成功 v. 获胜 ，取胜 ，成功

ropospheric [trɒpəʊ’sferɪk]

释义 • adj. of or related to troposphere 对流层的

例句 • However, the greenhouse effect is a natural phenomenon involving the increase in global surface temperature due to the presence of greenhouse gases—water vapour, carbon dioxide, tropospheric ozone, methane and nitrous oxide—in the atmosphere. (IELTS3,TA,R3) 然而 ，温室效应是一种自然现象 ，大气中的温室气体诸如水蒸气 、二氧化碳 、对流层中的臭氧和一氧化氮等的存在使得地球表面温度上升 。

大气(atmosphere) 的排序：

对流层(troposphere)

平流层(stratosphere)

中间层(mesosphere)

电离层(ionosphere)

热层(thermosphere)

外层(exosphere)

roublesome [’trʌbəlsəm]

释义 • adj. causing trouble or anxiety; worrisome 令人烦恼的，讨厌的

例句 • But there are limits to adaptation and loud noise becomes more troublesome if the person is required to concentrate on more than one task. (IELTS7,T4,R3) 但是适应力是有限的 ，如果一个人被要求同时专注于多项任务时 ，那么 ，高分贝噪音会变得更加讨厌 。

uck [tʌk]

释义 • v. to push or fold or turn the ends or edges (of cloth, paper, etc.) so that they are hidden or held in place 折起，卷起，叠起

搭配 • tuck away 存放 ，隐藏

uck up 卷起

uck … into 把 ……塞进

例句 • This patch of brain tucked behind the orbits of the eyes is associated with evaluating information. (IELTS5,T2,R2) 藏在眼窝后面的这部分大脑与信息评价相关 。

urbid [’tɜːbɪd]

释义 • adj. opaque or muddy; not clear 浑浊的 ；disordered or confused 紊乱的，混乱的

例句 • For example, vision is obviously more useful to species inhabiting clear open waters than to those living in turbid rivers and flooded plains. (IELTS4,T1,R3) 例如 ，与生活在浑浊的河水中和被洪灾侵袭过的平原上的物种相比 ，视觉显然对生存在清澈的开阔水域中的物种更有用 。

weak [twiːk]

释义 • v. to pinch, pluck, or twist sharply 拧，捏，扭，揪

例句 • The focus is on individuals, tweaking performances to squeeze an extra hundredth of a second here, an extra millimetre there. (IELTS6,T1,R1) 工作的核心是以人为本 ，其目的在于促进运动员发挥最大潜力 ，提高百分之一秒的速度或者是一毫米的成绩 。

ubiquitous [ju:ˈbɪkwɪtəs]

释义 • adj . present, appearing, or found everywhere无所不在的；普遍存在的

同义 • omnipresent, pervasive, universal, rife, prevalent

例句 • We are probably all familiar with background music in films, which has become so ubiquitous as to be noticeable in its absence. (IELTS11,T4,R2) 我们可能都很了解电影中的背景音乐，它已经变得无处不在，所以在没有背景音乐的时候，观众很容易察觉得到。

uncanny [ʌn’kænɪ]

释义 • adj. unnatural 异乎寻常的 ；beyond what is normal or expected; extraordinary 出乎意料的

词根 • un(not)+canny(安静的 )→异乎寻常的

派生 • uncannily adv. 出乎意料地

例句 • Blind humans sometimes seem to have an uncanny sense of obstacles in their path. (IELTS7,T1,R1) 盲人有时似乎对行进中的障碍有种异乎寻常的感觉 。

uncompromising [ʌn’kɒmprəmaɪzɪŋ]

释义 • adj. not ready to make any compromise; firm or unyielding 不妥协的，坚定的，不让步的

词根 • un(not)+compromising(妥协的 )→不妥协的

例句 • Archaeological traces of far more elaborate cultures have been dismissed as the ruins of invaders from outside the region, abandoned to decay in the uncompromising tropical environment. (IELTS3,T3,R2) 更为复杂的文化的考古痕迹由于外界侵略者的入侵变成了废墟 ，被遗弃在恶劣的热带环境中自生自灭 。

unconquerable [ʌn’kɒŋkərəbl]

释义 • adj. impossible to overcome or defeat 不可征服的

例句 • To casual observers, as well as to influential natural scientists and regional planners, the luxuriant forests of Amazonia seem ageless, unconquerable , a habitat totally hostile to human civilization. (IELTS3,T3,R2) 对于普通的观察者 、著名的自然科学家和区域规划者来说 ，亚马逊流域茂盛的森林似乎永远那么年轻 、不可征服 ，是一块完全不受人类文明影响的自然环境 。

underlie [ˌʌndə’laɪ]

释义 • v. to form the basis of (sb’ s actions, a theory, etc); account for 构成……的基础

词根 • under(下面 )+lie(位于 )→位于下面的 →构成 ……的基础

例句 • Unlike the multitude of elixirs being touted as the latest anti-aging cure, calorie restriction (CR) mimetics would alter fundamental processes that underlie aging. (IELTS6,T3,R3) 和许多宣称是最新的抗衰老药不同 ， 能量控制模型将改变衰老的基本过程 。

undue [ʌn’djuː]

释义 • adj. more than is right or proper; excessive 过分的，不当的

词根 • un(not)+due(恰当的 )→不当的

派生 • unduly adv. 过分地

例句 • There was undue optimism in the early 1980s, says David Leake, a researcher at Indiana University. (IELTS5,T3,R3) 印第安那大学的研究人员 David Leaker说 ，在20世纪80年代早期人们过于乐观 。

unfit [ʌn’fɪt]

释义 • adj. not of the required standard; unsuitable 不合适的 ；lacking the ability needed; incapable 不能胜任的

词根 • un(not)+fit(合适的 )→不合适的

同义 • inappropriate, unsuitable, incompetent, disqualified

搭配 • be unfit for 不合适

be unfit to do 不能胜任

例句 • Because the tropical forest has been depicted as ecologically unfit for large-scale human occupation, some environmentalists have opposed development of any kind. (IELTS3,T3,R2) 由于热带森林被描述为生态上不适合人类大规模居住 ，所以一些环境学家反对对它进行任何形式的开发 。

unfold [ʌn’fəʊld]

释义 • v. to open or spread out from a folded state 展开，摊开，打开 ；(cause sth. to) be revealed or made known 显示，说明，表明

词根 • un(not)+fold(折 )→把折的东西打开 →展开 ，打开

同义 • open, display, manifest, demonstrate, show

例句 • As the experiment unfolded , the pupil would deliberately give the wrong answers to questions posed by the teacher, thereby bringing on various electrical punishments, even up to the danger level of 300 volts and beyond. (IELTS5,T1,R2) 随着试验进行 ，学生们会故意地对教师提出的问题给出错误的答案 ，从而带来不同程度的电击惩罚 ，甚至达到 300伏或者更高 。

unify [’juːnɪfaɪ]

释义 • v. to form (sth.) into a single unit or make uniform 统一，使一致

词根 • uni(one)+fy(做 )→做成一个 →统一 ，使一致

派生 • unification n. 统一 ，单一化

例句 • That said, different groups of researchers attacked different problems, from speech recognition to chess playing, in different ways; AI unified the field in name only. (IELTS5,T3,R3) 说到此 ，不同小组的研究者们用不同的方法攻克不同的问题 ，从理解言语到下棋 ，人工智能只是这些领域一个统一的名字罢了 。

unimpeded [ˌʌnɪm’piːdɪd]

释义 • adj. happening or moving without being stopped or having difficulty 不受阻碍的

词根 • un(not)+impeded(阻碍的 )→不受阻碍的

例句 • This would have allowed river traffic to continue unimpeded during construction. (IELTS7,TB,R3) 这使得江河交通在建设过程中继续畅通 。

unleash [ˌʌn’liːʃ]

释义 • v. to set sth. free from a leash or restraint 把(情绪、力量等)宣泄出来，释放

搭配 • unleash sth. (against/on/upon sb./sth.)宣泄 ，释放

例句 • And if they are within the central, tensile region of the pane, the stresses this unleashes can shatter the whole sheet. (IELTS5,T4,R2) 如果它们处于玻璃中间可拉伸的区域 ，那么 ，释放出来的压力会粉碎整块玻璃 。

unprejudiced [ʌn’predʒʊdɪst]

释义 • adj. free from prejudice; not biased 无偏见的，公正的

词根 • un(not)+prejudiced(有偏见的 )→无偏见的

例句 • The myth of scientific method is that it is inductive: that the formulation of scientific theory starts with the basic, raw evidence of the senses—simple, unbiased, unprejudiced observation. (IELTS3,T1,R3) 科学方法的神秘之处在于它是归纳得出的 ：科学理论的形成始于基本的 、原始的感性认识 ——简单 、公正 、客观的观察 。

unrivalled [ʌn’raɪvəld]

释义 • adj. having no rival; unequalled 无与伦比的

词根 • un(not)+rival(对手 )+ed→没有对手的 →无与伦比的

例句 • Finally, they offer those condemned to spend five days a week in an urban environment an unrivalled area of freedom to unwind and take part in a range of leisure activities, such as hunting, riding and hiking. (IELTS7,T3,R3) 最后 ，对于那些一周五天不得不待在城市的人来说 ，他们为其提供无与伦比的自由释放空间 ，他们还可以参加一系列休闲活动 ，例如打猎 、骑马和远足 。

unscathed [ʌn’skeɪðd]

释义 • adj. not injured or hurt; unharmed (身心)没有受损伤的

例句 • Yet it left the magnificent five-storey pagoda at the Toji temple in nearby Kyoto unscathed , though it levelled a number of buildings in the neighbourhood. (IELTS7,T2,R1) 虽然它把附近许多建筑物夷为平地 ，但是它把宏伟的五层宝塔毫无损坏地保留在了京都附近的太极寺中 。

unsolicited [’ʌnsə’lɪsɪtɪd]

释义 • adj. given or sent voluntarily; not asked for 未经请求的，主动提供的，自发的；无缘无故的；多事的，多余的

词根 • un(not)+solicit(引发 )+ed→未经请求的

例句 • Despite your best efforts, unsolicited email or spam can clutter up the most organised inbox and infect your computer system with viruses. (IELTS7,TB,R2) 尽管你努力抵制 ，不请自来的电邮或垃圾邮件可能会堆满你井井有条的收件箱 ，并且通过病毒感染电脑系统 。

unswerving [ʌn’swɜːvɪŋ]

释义 • adj. steady or constant; unchanging 坚定的，不改变的

词根 • un(not)+swerve(改变方向 )+ing→不改变方向的 →坚定的

例句 • It turns out that it’ s not Florence’ s nose that makes her a top drug dog, but her unswerving concentration, plus a few other essential traits. (IELTS7,TA,R3)结果表明 ，Florence成为顶级的缉毒犬并不是靠它的鼻子 ，而是靠它持久的专注力 ，还有其他一些基本特征 。

unveil [ˌʌn’veɪl]

释义 • v. to remove one’ s veil; to remove a veil from (sth./sb.) 除去……的覆盖，取下面纱 ；to remove a cloth, etc. from (sth.), esp. as part of a public ceremony 举行……的揭牌典礼 ；to show or announce (sth.) publicly for the first time 揭露，吐露

词根 • un(not)+veil(面纱 ，遮盖 )→除去 ……的覆盖

例句 • Some years ago, the AIS unveiled coolant-lined jackets for endurance athletes. (IELTS6,T1,R1)几年前 ，澳大利亚体育学院展示了他们为耐力运动员设计的冷凝缝合运动衣 。

upright [’ʌpraɪt]

释义 • adj. in a vertical position; erect 垂直的，直立的 ；strictly honest or honourable 正直的，诚实的

词根 • up(向上 )+right(笔直 )→笔直向上的 →垂直的

例句 • Yet in 826, with only pegs and wedges to keep his wooden structure upright , the master builder Kobodaishi had no hesitation in sending his majestic Toji pagoda soaring fifty-five metres into the sky … (IELTS7,T2,R1) 然而在 826年 ，在那个只能用挂钉和楔子来使得木结构直立的时代 ，建筑大师 Kobodaishi毫不犹豫地建立了这座高达 55米的庄严的东寺塔 。

urgency [’ɜːdʒənsɪ]

释义 • n. the quality or condition of being urgent; pressing importance 紧急，紧急性

派生 • urgent11 adj. 紧急的

urgently2 adv. 紧急地

例句 • They may request brief details of your symptoms or illness—this enables the doctors to assess the degree of urgency . (IELTS6,TA,R1) 他们可能要求你讲一下你的症状或者不适 ——这就能让医生知道病情的紧急程度 。

vaccine [væk’si:n]

释义 • n. a substance used to stimulate the production of antibodies and provide immunity against one or several diseases, prepared from the causative agent of a disease, its products, or a synthetic substitute, treated to act as an antigen without inducing the disease 疫苗，菌苗

派生 • vaccinate1 vt. 给 ……种痘 ，给 ……打预防针 vaccination2 n . 种痘 ，疫苗接种

例句 • And, in what would have been particularly pleasing to Perkin, their current use is in the search for a vaccine against malaria. (IELTS9,T1,R1) 尤其让珀金感到欣慰的是 ，它们 （这些染料 ）目前正用于疟疾疫苗的研究中 。

vague [ve ɪ ɡ]

释义 • adj . of uncertain, indefinite, or unclear character or meaning 不明确的，不清楚的 ；thinking or communicating in an unfocused or imprecise way 含糊的，模糊的

同义 • indefinite, unclear, faint, uncertain, obscure

例句 • Having identified this fundamental unit, Shannon set about defining otherwise vague ideas about information and how to transmit it from place to place. (IELTS9,T3,R3) 在确定这一基本单位之后 ，Shannon又转而致力于明确一些模棱两可的信息 ，以及如何进行信息传递 。

van [væn]

释义 • n. an enclosed boxlike motor vehicle having rear or side doors and side panels especially for transporting people 运货车 ；a covered or enclosed truck or wagon often used for transporting goods or livestock 有棚盖的铁路货车

联想 • 运货车 (van)能够 (can)运很多东西

例句 • Think about how vans and lorries will deliver and collect goods from the premises. (IELTS7,TA,R2) 考虑一下运货车和卡车怎么样从建筑物中运送和收集货物 。

vandalism [’vændlɪzəm]

释义 • n . action involving deliberate destruction of or damage to public or private property 故意破坏他人(或公共)财产行为；涂鸦行为

例句 • After the fire it had become apparent just how much remained of the structure with its splendidly decorated interiors; to have pulled the house down, as one commentator suggested, would have been vandalism . (IELTS9,TA,R3) 大火之后 ，内饰豪华的建筑遗留部分显而易见 。正如一名评论员所说 ，将整座房屋推倒是对它的破坏 。

variability [ˌveərɪə’bɪlɪtɪ]

释义 • n. the quality, state, or degree of being variable or changeable. 可变性，易变性

派生 • vary24 v. 改变 ，变动

variable7 adj. 易变的 n. 变量

variant7 n. 变体 ，变型

variation11 n. 变化 ，变动

variety54 n. 多样化

various37 adj. 各种各样的

例句 • That’ s part of an ongoing variability study but the results are still a long way off. (IELTS7,T3,L3) 虽然这只是正在进行的可变性研究的一部分 ，但是结果还需要很长时间才能出来 。

vend [vend]

释义 • v. to offer(esp. small articles) for sale 卖，售

搭配 • vending machine 自动贩卖机

派生 • vender/vendor n. 摊贩 ，小贩

例句 • The Save-a-Cup scheme was set up by the vending and plastics industries to recycle as many as possible of the three-and-a-half billion polystyrene cups used each year. (IELTS5,T3,L4) 节省一个杯子的计划是由商贩们和塑料行业出台的 ，目的是尽可能多地循环利用每年用掉的 35亿只聚苯乙烯杯子 。

vent [vent]

释义 • n. an opening that allows air, gas, liquid, etc. to pass out of or into a confined space 通风孔，排气管；排气 ；venting 发泄 v. to find or provide an outlet for (an emotion) 发泄

搭配 • give vent to 发泄

派生 • ventilate v. 使通风

ventilation2 n. 通风

例句 • Over the sound of roaring engines, rushing air vents and grinding generators, a dog barks. (IELTS7,TA,R3) 在机器的轰鸣声 、气孔的强风声和巨大的发电机声中混杂着狗的叫声 。

veracity [və’ræsəti]

释义 • n. conformity to facts; accuracy 真实；准确 ；habitual truthfulness 诚实

派生 • veracious adj . 诚实的 ；真实的

例句 • As one writer observes: “Although it is now evident that artefacts are as easily altered as chronicles, public faith in their veracity endures: a tangible relic seems ipso facto real.” (IELTS9,T4,R3) 一位作家说道 ：“尽管现在手工艺品如历史记录一般容易作假 ，但公众还是坚信它们的真实性 ，因为一件有形文物本身就是一种真实 。”

veranda [və’rændə]

释义 • n. a large, open porch, usually roofed and partly enclosed, as by a railing, often extending across the front and sides of a house; gallery 阳台，走廊

例句 • On the fourth side, verandas which are supported by ornate pillars overlook the steps. (IELTS10,T1,R1)在第四面 ，由装饰华丽的柱子所支撑的阳台能够俯瞰台阶 。

versatile [’vɜːsətaɪl]

释义 • adj. turning easily or readily from one subject, skill or occupation to another 多才多艺的，多种技能的 ；having various uses 有多种用途的

词根 • vers(转 )+atile→各方都转得动 →多才多艺的

派生 • versatility n. 多才多艺

例句 • Bakelite was immediately welcomed as a practical and versatile material. (IELTS5,T2,R1) 酚醛塑料是实用的 、有多种用途的材料 ，它很快就受到了人们的欢迎 。

vested [’vestɪd]

释义 • adj. law settled, fixed, or absolute; being without contingency 法律规定的，既定的

例句 • Growth and environmentalism can actually go hand in hand, if politicians have the courage to confront the vested interest that subsidies create. (IELTS3,T2,R2) 经济增长和环境保护实际上是可以同时进行的 ， 前提是政治家们有勇气去面对补贴带来的既得利益 。

veteran [’vetərən]

释义 • n . a person who has served in a military force, especially one who has fought in a war 老兵；退伍军人

例句 • If your project is being resisted, for example, by a group of veteran employees, ask another old-timer to speak up for it. (IELTS10,T1,R3)如果你的提议遭到反对 ，例如一些资历老的员工反对你的计划 ，那么就让一些元老为你说话 。

vexingly [’veksɪŋlɪ]

释义 • adv. annoyingly 令人烦恼地，令人苦恼地

派生 • vex v. 使苦恼 ，使困扰

vexation n. 烦恼 ，忧虑

vexatious adj. 使人恼怒的

例句 • Once you study athletics, you learn that it’ s a vexingly complex issue, says John Smith. (IELTS4,T4,R1) 约翰 · 史密斯说 ，一旦研究竞技运动 ，你就会发现它是极其复杂的问题 。

vicissitude [vɪ’sɪsɪtjuːd]

释义 • n. a change in one’ s circumstances, esp. for the worse 变化，盛衰，兴败

例句 • After many vicissitudes the Dictionary was finally published on 15 April 1775. (IELTS5,T1,R1) 在经历了许多波折之后 ，这本字典最终于 1775年 4月 15日出版了 。

victimise [’vɪktəmaɪz]

释义 • v. to harm sb. or make sb. suffer unfairly; to bully sb. 不正当地使某人受损害

派生 • victim8 n. 牺牲者 ，受害者

例句 • Victimised pupils are more likely to experience difficulties with interpersonal relation. (IELTS6,T4,R3) 受害的小学生更可能经历人际交往障碍 。

villa [’vɪlə]

释义 • n. any imposing or pretentious residence, especially one in the country or suburbs maintained as a retreat by a wealthy person 别墅

例句 • Seaside resorts located at Pompeii and Herculaneum afforded citizens the opportunity to escape to their vacation villas in order to avoid the summer heat of Rome. (IELTS10,T3,R1)位于庞贝古城和赫库兰尼姆古城的海边度假胜地让居民能够逃到他们的度假别墅中 ，躲避罗马的炎炎夏日 。

virgin [’vɜːdʒɪn]

释义 • n. a person, esp. a girl or woman, who has never had sexual intercourse 处女 adj. of a virgin 贞洁的 ；in an original or natural condition; untouched 未经使用的，未经开发的

例句 • The production of recycled glass and paper uses much less energy than producing them from virgin materials. (IELTS5,T3,L4) 对玻璃和纸张的循环利用要比使用原材料生产它们节约很多能源 。

virtue [’vɜːtjuː]

释义 • n. an attractive or useful quality 优点， 长处，用处 ；behaviour or attitudes that show high moral standards 美德，优秀品质，良好习惯

同义 • goodness, excellence, morality; advantage, merit

派生 • virtual adj. 实际的

virtually16 adv. 实际上 ，事实上

例句 • The virtue of job descriptions is that they lessen this role ambiguity. (IELTS3,T2,R3) 职位描述的优点是他们可以明确角色 。

vitality [vaɪ’tælɪtɪ]

释义 • n. persistent energy; liveliness or vigour 活力，生机，元气

词根 • vit(生命 )+ality→事关生命的东西 →生机

派生 • vital12 adj. 生死攸关的 ，极其重要的

vitalize v. 赋予生命

例句 • When you see the Asiatic lion in India, what you sense is enormous vitality . (IELTS6,T4,L4) 当你看到印度的亚洲狮时 ，你能感觉到它们有着极强的生命力 。

vow [vaʊ]

释义 • v. to make a vow of; promise by a vow, as to God or a saint 发誓

同义 • pledge, oath, assert

例句 • He also vowed to look for the joy in everything, including failure, as this could help him learn about his research and himself. (IELTS10,T4,R2)他也发誓要从一切事情 ，包括失败中寻求快乐 ，因为这有助于了解他的研究和自己 。

wade [weɪd]

释义 • v. to cross (a stream, etc.) by wading 趟水，跋涉 ；to walk with an effort (through water, mud or anything that makes walking difficult) 费力地前进，困难地通过

例句 • Statistics indicate that office workers need to wade through an average of more than 30 emails a day. (IELTS7,TB,R2) 统计数据表明 ，办公室工作人员平均每天都要费力地处理 30多封电邮 。

waist [weɪst]

释义 • n. the part of the body between the ribs and the hips, usu. narrower than the rest of the trunk 腰，腰部

例句 • They’ re large puppets on long sticks, controlled by puppeteers standing waist deep in the lake. (IELTS4,T3,L2) 这些木偶被固定在长棍子上 ，操纵木偶的人站在湖水中 ，水没过他们的腰部 。

wander [’wɒndə]

释义 • v. to move around in an area or go from place to place without any special purpose or destination; roam 闲逛，漫游 ；to be inattentive, confused or delirious 走神，恍惚 ；to leave the right place or way; to stray from one’ s group 迷路

联想 • 人们经常在十字路口闲逛 (wander)，想知道 (wonder)该如何选择下一步

派生 • wanderer n. 徘徊者 ，流浪者

wandering adj. 徘徊的 ，流浪的

例句 • I suggest you spend a good hour wandering around this lovely building. (IELTS6,T3,L2) 我建议你花一个小时逛一逛这个可爱的建筑 。

wardrobe [’wɔːdrəʊb]

释义 • n. a place where clothes are stored, usu. a large cupboard with shelves and a rail for hanging things on 衣柜，藏衣室

词根 • ward(存放 )+robe(衣服 )→存放衣服的地方 →衣柜

例句 • And many employees now welcome a company wardrobe . (IELTS3,TB,R3) 公司储衣柜很受员工的欢迎 。

warrant [’wɒrənt]

释义 • n. a written order giving authority to do sth. 授权，许可证 v. to be a warrant for (sth.); justify or deserve 保证，证明……正当

派生 • warranty n. (商品的 )保证书

例句 • And even in regions where new projects seem warranted , we must find ways to meet demands with fewer resources, respecting ecological criteria and to a smaller budget. (IELTS7,T1,R2) 即便在新项目受许可的地区 ，我们也需要找到办法来节约资源 、尊重生态标准 、减少预算 。

wary [’weəri]

释义 • adj. arising from or characterized by caution 谨慎的，小心翼翼的

同义 • attentive, suspicious, watchful

例句 • The theory sounds eccentric but once he starts to explain the detective work that went into his deduction, the scepticism gives way to wary admiration. (IELTS10,T2,R1)这一理论听起来很古怪 ，但当他开始解释推理过程中的侦查工作时 ，这种怀疑最终变成了谨慎的钦佩 。

watertight [’wɔːtətaɪt]

释义 • adj. so tightly made that water cannot enter or escape 不透水的，防水的

词根 • water+tight(不漏的 )→不漏水的

例句 • The outside of the pots was often polished to make them watertight . (IELTS6,T3,L4) 罐的外围常常被涂上东西 ，使其能够防水 。

water 水:

watercolor n. 水彩

watermelon n. 西瓜

waterway n. 水路，航道

waterfall n. 瀑布

water bird 水鸟

waterworks n. 自来水厂

watershed n. 分水岭

wax [wæks]

释义 • n. a solid substance used, after being bleached and purified, for making candles, modelling, etc. 蜡 v. to polish (sth.) with wax 给……打蜡 ；to show a large bright area that gradually increases until the moon is full (月亮)渐圆；渐满

搭配 • wax and wane (月的 )盈亏圆缺 ；〈喻 〉盛衰

例句 • For those living near the equator in particular, its waxing and waning was more conspicuous than the passing of the seasons. (IELTS8,T1, R1) 尤其对于那些生活在赤道附近的人来说 ，月圆月缺比季节交替更明显 。

wean [wiːn]

释义 • v. to gradually stop feeding (a baby or young animal) with its mother’ s milk and start feeding it with solid food (使)断奶 ；to cause sb. to stop doing sth., esp. gradually (使)戒掉

例句 • It is not effective for all insomniacs, but many users have weaned themselves off sleeping tablets as a result of its application. (IELTS5,TA,R3) 虽然它并不一定对所有的失眠患者有效 ，但是许多患者用了它之后 ，就不再需要安眠药了 。

wedge [wedʒ]

释义 • n. a piece of wood or metal that is thick at one end and narrows at the other to a sharp edge, used e.g. to split wood or rock, to widen an opening or to keep things apart 楔子 v. to firmly or force (sth.) apart using a wedge 用楔子把……固定住

例句 • Yet in 826, with only pegs and wedges to keep his wooden structure upright, the master builder Kobodaishi had no hesitation in sending his majestic Toji pagoda soaring fifty-five metres into the sky … (IELTS7,T2,R1) 然而在 826年 ，在那个只能用挂钉和楔子来使得木结构直立的时代 ，建筑大师 Kobodaishi毫不犹豫地建立起高达 55米的庄严的东寺塔 。

weird [wɪəd]

释义 • adj. unnatural, uncanny or strange 不可思议的，古怪的

同义 • strange, eccentric

例句 • In any event, whether or not the reason is the energy expense, it seems to be the case that, with the possible exception of some weird deep-sea fish, no animal apart from man uses manufactured light to find its way about. (IELTS7,T1,R1) 无论如何 ，不管原因是否是耗费能量 ，情况好像是除了一些古怪的深海鱼 ，除了人类之外再也没有动物通过自己造光来探路 。

weld [weld]

释义 • v. to join (pieces of metal) by hammering or pressing (usu. when the metal is softened by heat) or fuse them by using an oxy-acetylene flame or an electric arc 焊接，熔接 ；to unite (people or things) into an effective whole 使成一体

例句 • The bridge wasn’ t welded or bolted together as metal bridges are these days. (IELTS7,TB,R3) 与现在的铁桥不同 ，那时的桥不是焊接或栓在一起的 。

well-being [’wel’biːɪŋ]

释义 • n. the state of being healthy, happy, or prosperous; welfare 安宁，福利

例句 • As most people spend a major part of their adult life at work, job satisfaction is an important element of individual well-being . (IELTS7,T3,W2) 由于大多数人成年后的时间都花在工作中 ，因此工作中的满足感是个人幸福的重要因素 。

whim [wɪm]

释义 • n. a sudden desire or idea, esp. an unusual or unreasonable one; caprice 突然的怪念头，一时的兴致

派生 • whimsical adj. 异想天开的 ，突发奇想的

例句 • A still picture could only imply the existence of time, while time in a novel passed at the whim of the reader. (IELTS6,T4,R1) 一幅静止的画只能暗指时间的存在 ，而小说中的时间却存在于读者的闪念间 。

wilderness [’wɪldənɪs]

释义 • n. an area of wild uncultivated land; desert 荒野，沙漠

搭配 • be in the wilderness (政治家 )在野 ，不再当政 (或掌权 )

例句 • a unique wilderness retreat on the edge of the World Heritage-listed National Park（IELTS8,T1,R1）一个独具特色的荒野 ，位于世界遗产名录上的国家公园的边缘

worship [’wɜ:ʃɪp]

释义 • n. reverent honor and homage paid to God or a sacred personage, or to any object regarded as sacred 礼拜，崇拜

例句 • During their heyday, they were places of gathering, of leisure and relaxation and of worship for villagers of all but the lowest classes. (IELTS10,T1,R1)在最鼎盛时期 ，它们是休闲聚会的场所 ，也是村民们做礼拜的地方 ——除了最底层的村民之外 。

wrap [ræp]

释义 • v. to cover or enclose sth. (in soft or flexible material) 裹，包，卷 ；to fold (a piece of material) round sb./sth. as covering or protection 隐藏，掩饰

搭配 • wrap up 包好 ，把 ……包起来

派生 • wrapper n. 包装纸 ，封套 ，封皮

例句 • Inside the case, within styrofoam casing, packed in loose pepper and coffee, wrapped in freezer paper and heat-sealed in plastic, are 18 kilograms of hashish. (IELTS7,TA,R3) 箱子里有一个聚苯乙烯泡沫塑封的包装 ，里面散放着一些辣椒和咖啡 ，其中杂带着一个热塑封的冷藏纸包装物 ，内藏 18千克印度大麻 。

wring [rɪŋ]

释义 • v. to twist and squeeze sth. in order to remove liquid from it 把……拧干，扭，绞 ；to extract or obtain sth. from sb. with effort or difficulty 榨取，勒索，逼供

例句 • This data is used to wring improvements out of athletes. (IELTS6,T1,R1) 这个数据是用来改善运动员表现的 。

writhe [raɪð]

释义 • v. (of sb. or sb’ s body) to twist or roll about, esp. because of great pain (人体)扭动，翻滚(尤指因剧痛)

搭配 • writhe at (under, with)sth. 因某事遭受精神痛苦

例句 • The supposed pupil was in reality an actor hired by Milgram to simulate receiving the shocks by emitting a spectrum of groans, screams and writhings together with an assortment of statements and expletives denouncing both the experiment and the experimenter. (IELTS5,T1,R2) 所谓的学生实际上是由 Milgram雇来的演员 。他们通过发出一系列呻吟 、尖叫来假装受到电击的痛苦 ，还骂骂咧咧地谴责试验与试验者 ，同时将身体翻滚 、扭动 。

yacht [jɒt]

释义 • n. a vessel used for private cruising, racing, or other noncommercial purposes 快艇

例句 • You could become an experienced yacht skipper or instructor and many people go on to spend their future holidays being paid to enjoy their favourite sport. (IELTS10,TB,R2) 你可以成为经验丰富的快艇船长或教练 。许多人在以后的度假中 ，也会继续享受他们最喜爱的运动 。

youngster [’jʌŋstə]

释义 • n. a young person; a child or youth 年轻人，小伙子，小孩

词根 • young(年轻的 )+ster(表示人 )→年轻人

例句 • At the Australian Institute of Sport (AIS), hundreds of youngsters and pros live and train under the eyes of coaches. (IELTS6,T1,R1)在澳大利亚体育学院 ，成百上千的年轻人和体育专业人士在教练的眼皮底下生活和训练 。

-ster 表示人：

songster n. 歌手，歌唱家

eenster n. 十几岁的少年

oldster n. 老人

spinster n. 纺织女

minister n. 部长，大臣

speedster n. 超速驾驶者

gangster n. 匪徒，歹徒

mobster n. 暴徒

zipper [’zɪpə]

释义 • n. a fastening device consisting of parallel rows of metal, plastic, or nylon teeth on adjacent edges of an opening that are interlocked by a sliding tab 拉链，拉锁

派生 • zip v. 用拉锁扣上

例句 • Jacket W—waterproof with zipper front, all sizes (IELTS5,TA,R1) 夹克 W——防水 ，前侧有拉链 ，尺寸齐全
